\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{PLOT{\_}CHAR}}{PLOT:unCHAR}{PYNWmai0-GKJMRCHOW2FWSNTGL6NTUR7XCE000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{PLOT{\_}CHAR}}{PLOT:unCHAR}}}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{PRINT{\_}FONTCHAR{\_}AT{\_}TEXT{\_}POS}}{PRINT:unFONTCHAR:unAT:unTEXT:unPOS}}\\{{\nwixident{TEXT{\_}COL}}{TEXT:unCOL}}\\{{\nwixident{TEXT{\_}ROW}}{TEXT:unROW}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{PRINT{\_}FONTCHAR{\_}AT{\_}TEXT{\_}POS}}{PRINT:unFONTCHAR:unAT:unTEXT:unPOS}{PYNWmai0-GKJMRCHOW2FWSNTGL6NTUR7XCE000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{TEXT{\_}COL}}{TEXT:unCOL}{PYNWmai0-GKJMRCHOW2FWSNTGL6NTUR7XCE000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{TEXT{\_}ROW}}{TEXT:unROW}{PYNWmai0-GKJMRCHOW2FWSNTGL6NTUR7XCE000000-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{161}\nwdocspar

\chapter{Sound}

The {\Tt{}TONE{\_}RANDOMIZE{\_}MASK\nwendquote} is initially set to 1 to apply a little bit of
randomness to the song notes. However, this can be set to {\Tt{}00\nwendquote} via opcode {\Tt{}NORAND\nwendquote}
to play exact notes, or set to {\Tt{}0F\nwendquote} via opcode {\Tt{}HIRAND\nwendquote} to provide high
randomness.

\begin{table}[]
\begin{tabular}{llll}
\multicolumn{1}{c}{Byte} & \multicolumn{1}{c}{Opcode} & \multicolumn{1}{c}{Argument} & \multicolumn{1}{c}{Operation} \\
{\Tt{}1F\nwendquote} & {\Tt{}MARK2\nwendquote} & none & {\Tt{}SCRIPT{\textbackslash}{\_}LOOP{\textbackslash}{\_}ADDR\ <-\ IP+1\nwendquote} \\
{\Tt{}20\nwendquote} & {\Tt{}MARK1\nwendquote} & none & {\Tt{}SCRIPT{\textbackslash}{\_}GOSUB{\textbackslash}{\_}ADDR\ <-\ IP+1\nwendquote} \\
{\Tt{}21\nwendquote} & {\Tt{}GOTO1\nwendquote} & none & {\Tt{}IP\ <-\ SCRIPT{\textbackslash}{\_}GOSUB{\textbackslash}{\_}ADDR\nwendquote} \\
{\Tt{}22\nwendquote} & {\Tt{}LOW\nwendquote} & none & {\Tt{}TONE{\_}ROUTINE{\_}ADDR\ <-\ tone\nwendquote} \\
{\Tt{}23\nwendquote} & {\Tt{}HIGH\nwendquote} & none & {\Tt{}TONE{\_}ROUTINE{\_}ADDR\ <-\ high{\_}tone\nwendquote} \\
{\Tt{}24\nwendquote} & {\Tt{}END\nwendquote} & none & Ends the song routine \\
{\Tt{}25\nwendquote} & {\Tt{}HIRAND\nwendquote} & none & {\Tt{}TONE{\_}RANDOMIZE{\_}MASK\ <-\ 0F\nwendquote} \\
{\Tt{}26\nwendquote} & {\Tt{}NORAND\nwendquote} & none & {\Tt{}TONE{\_}RANDOMIZE{\_}MASK\ <-\ 00\nwendquote} \\
{\Tt{}27-FF\nwendquote} & {\Tt{}NOTE\nwendquote} & duration & Plays note \\
\end{tabular}
\caption{Song program opcodes}
\label{table:song}
\end{table}

Playing a tone involves accessing the speaker address twice per audio cycle.
The {\Tt{}tone\nwendquote} routine delays {\Tt{}10X+31\nwendquote} cycles between speaker accesses, and
based on an average Apple II cycle time of {\Tt{}0.98\nwendquote} microseconds, this means
that the frequency of the note played will be equal to {\Tt{}510204\ /\ (10X+31)\nwendquote} Hz.
See \href{https://6502disassembly.com/a2-rom/}{The Oft Misunderstood WAIT} for a derivation of average cycle time.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{162}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-6MB7TIK43W7I5YBJMUI2RMCLGA000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-6MB7TIK43W7I5YBJMUI2RMCLGA000000-1}}}\moddef{tone~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-6MB7TIK43W7I5YBJMUI2RMCLGA000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwenddeflinemarkup
\nwlinkedidentc{tone}{PYNWmai0-6MB7TIK43W7I5YBJMUI2RMCLGA000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    LDY      #$0A           ; 2 cycles

.outer_loop:
    LDA      SPKR           ; 4 cycles

.inner_loop:
    ROL      DAT_00e3       ; 5 cycles
    DEX                     ; 2 cycles
    BNE      .inner_loop    ; 3 cycles

    LDX      note_freq      ; 3 cycles
    ROL      DAT_00e3       ; 5 cycles
    ROR      DAT_00e3       ; 5 cycles
    NOP                     ; 3 cycles
    NOP                     ; 3 cycles
    NOP                     ; 3 cycles
    DEY                     ; 2 cycles
    BNE      .outer_loop    ; 3 cycles

    DEC      note_duration  ; 5 cycles
    BNE      \nwlinkedidentc{tone}{PYNWmai0-6MB7TIK43W7I5YBJMUI2RMCLGA000000-1}           ; 3 cycles
    RTS
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{tone}}{tone}{PYNWmai0-6MB7TIK43W7I5YBJMUI2RMCLGA000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{tone}}{tone}}}\nwnotused{tone}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{163}\nwdocspar

The {\Tt{}high{\_}tone\nwendquote} routine does the same thing, but with shorter delays.
The frequency of the note played by {\Tt{}high{\_}tone\nwendquote} will be equal to
{\Tt{}510204\ /\ (5X+12)\nwendquote} Hz.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{164}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-UIZGU6YNKDK4XWBDBMWRAWBZIY000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-UIZGU6YNKDK4XWBDBMWRAWBZIY000000-1}}}\moddef{high tone~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-UIZGU6YNKDK4XWBDBMWRAWBZIY000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwenddeflinemarkup
\nwlinkedidentc{high_tone}{PYNWmai0-UIZGU6YNKDK4XWBDBMWRAWBZIY000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    LDY      #$0A           ; 2 cycles

.outer_loop:
    LDA      SPKR           ; 4 cycles

.inner_loop:
    DEX                     ; 2 cycles
    BNE      .inner_loop    ; 3 cycles

    LDX      note_freq      ; 3 cycles
    DEY                     ; 2 cycles
    BNE      .outer_loop    ; 3 cycles

    DEC      note_duration  ; 5 cycles
    BNE      \nwlinkedidentc{high_tone}{PYNWmai0-UIZGU6YNKDK4XWBDBMWRAWBZIY000000-1}      ; 3 cycles
    RTS
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{high{\_}tone}}{high:untone}{PYNWmai0-UIZGU6YNKDK4XWBDBMWRAWBZIY000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{high{\_}tone}}{high:untone}}}\nwnotused{high tone}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{165}\nwdocspar

Based on cycle times, these are the closest values for various notes. At the higher
frequencies, the values get so low that they differ only by one, which means the
notes aren't very accurate.

We run into an issue when we look at the song table for the splash screen. The
very first note played is low {\Tt{}3F\nwendquote}. This is closest to {\Tt{}G5\nwendquote}, although it
results in a frequency of {\Tt{}771.9\nwendquote} Hz, which is less accurate than the {\Tt{}783.7\nwendquote} Hz
that would be given by {\Tt{}3F\nwendquote}. In fact, all the low tones are off by a bit,
unless we assume that the programmer erred, thinking that the low tones were
just one octave below the high tones. In that case, we should just use the high
tone table and subtract one octave for the low tones.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{166}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-2J5GFOS7BQMCUPTS3GOLUMOYEM000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-2J5GFOS7BQMCUPTS3GOLUMOYEM000000-1}}}\moddef{song table~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-2J5GFOS7BQMCUPTS3GOLUMOYEM000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwenddeflinemarkup
SPLASH_SONG:
    LOW
    TONE 3F, 65     ; G5  @ 655ms
    HIGH
    TONE 3F, 49     ; G6  @ 469ms
    TONE 3F, 8A     ; G6  @ 887ms
    TONE 3F, 8A     ; G6  @ 887ms
    TONE 3F, 8A     ; G6  @ 887ms
    TONE 3F, 5C     ; G6  @ 591ms
    LOW
    TONE C1, 0C     ; C4  @ 231ms
    TONE 80, 04     ; G4  @  51ms
    TONE 50, 06     ; Eb5 @  49ms
    TONE 3F, 08     ; G5  @  52ms
    HIGH
    TONE 60, 0A     ; C6  @  97ms (\nwlinkedidentc{tone}{PYNWmai0-6MB7TIK43W7I5YBJMUI2RMCLGA000000-1} inaccurate)
    TONE 50, 0C     ; Eb5 @  97ms
    TONE 3F, 2E     ; G6  @ 296ms
    TONE 47, 1B     ; F5  @ 195ms
    TONE 3F, 1F     ; G6  @ 199ms
    TONE 47, 1B     ; F5  @ 195ms
    TONE 50, 18     ; Eb5 @ 194ms
    TONE 47, 1B     ; F5  @ 195ms
    TONE 50, 18     ; Eb5 @ 194ms
    TONE 55, 17     ; D6  @ 197ms (\nwlinkedidentc{tone}{PYNWmai0-6MB7TIK43W7I5YBJMUI2RMCLGA000000-1} inaccurate)
\nwnotused{song table}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{tone}}{tone}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{tone}}{tone}{PYNWmai0-2J5GFOS7BQMCUPTS3GOLUMOYEM000000-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{167}\nwdocspar

The {\Tt{}start{\_}sound\nwendquote} routine goes through a sound table, executing each
instruction until it encounters a {\Tt{}TONE\nwendquote} instruction. It then
plays that tone, and then jumps to a routine given by {\Tt{}indirect{\_}routine\nwendquote}. This
routine should do something, and then return to the song-playing loop by
jumping to {\Tt{}next{\_}table{\_}entry\nwendquote}. This allows the game to play a sound while doing
something else, for example, animating the splash screen at the beginning of the
game, and also interrupts the sound on keypress or joystick button press.

If {\Tt{}start{\_}sound\nwendquote} encounters an {\Tt{}END\nwendquote} instruction, it returns, and that ends
the song.

{\Tt{}start{\_}sound\nwendquote} also checks for a keypress or a joystick button press, and this
is the same as an {\Tt{}END\nwendquote} instruction.

\chapter{The Attract Screen}
\label{ch:attract}

When the main program starts at {\Tt{}{\$}0800\nwendquote}, it calls {\Tt{}GAME{\_}INIT\nwendquote} to set up
hardware and graphics, then checks {\Tt{}TOTAL{\textbackslash}{\_}MOB{\textbackslash}{\_}COUNT\nwendquote}. If zero (first run), it enters
the \emph{attract screen}---the title sequence that cycles through story scenes
until the player presses a key.

\section{Top-level flow}

\subsection{Main entry (\$0800)}

The first thing the main program does:

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{168}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-RWM37KK47QPMZDB6ORCTDQOT2Y000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-RWM37KK47QPMZDB6ORCTDQOT2Y000000-1}}}\moddef{main entry~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-RWM37KK47QPMZDB6ORCTDQOT2Y000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $0800
\nwlinkedidentc{MAIN_ENTRY}{PYNWmai0-RWM37KK47QPMZDB6ORCTDQOT2Y000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{GAME_INIT}{PYNWmai0-XR5IMSHLGD4AKOBGLQGCQ6POTY000000-1}
    LDA     #$09                    ; \\
    STA     $FA                     ;  | $FA/$FB = $4009 (character record base)
    LDA     #$40                    ;  |
    STA     $FB                     ; /
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{TOTAL_MOB_COUNT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-10}         ; zero on first run (no mobs yet)
    BNE     .skip                   ; nonzero = game in progress
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{ATTRACT_SCREEN}{PYNWmai0-J5774R6PCWTLDLXH4MIVVDMLZE000000-1}
.skip:
    ; ... continues to game loop ...
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{MAIN{\_}ENTRY}}{MAIN:unENTRY}{PYNWmai0-RWM37KK47QPMZDB6ORCTDQOT2Y000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{MAIN{\_}ENTRY}}{MAIN:unENTRY}}}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{ATTRACT{\_}SCREEN}}{ATTRACT:unSCREEN}}\\{{\nwixident{GAME{\_}INIT}}{GAME:unINIT}}\\{{\nwixident{TOTAL{\_}MOB{\_}COUNT}}{TOTAL:unMOB:unCOUNT}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{ATTRACT{\_}SCREEN}}{ATTRACT:unSCREEN}{PYNWmai0-RWM37KK47QPMZDB6ORCTDQOT2Y000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{GAME{\_}INIT}}{GAME:unINIT}{PYNWmai0-RWM37KK47QPMZDB6ORCTDQOT2Y000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{TOTAL{\_}MOB{\_}COUNT}}{TOTAL:unMOB:unCOUNT}{PYNWmai0-RWM37KK47QPMZDB6ORCTDQOT2Y000000-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{169}\nwdocspar

\subsection{select\_input\_mode (\$084E)}

Prompts the player to choose keyboard or joystick input.  Displays
message~\$38 (the prompt), then polls the keyboard and paddle button~1
in a tight loop.  If the player presses the space bar, {\Tt{}INPUT{\textbackslash}{\_}MODE\nwendquote}
is set to~0 (keyboard).  If the paddle button state changes (pressed or
released), {\Tt{}INPUT{\textbackslash}{\_}MODE\nwendquote} is set to~1 (joystick), the cursor is
repositioned, and message~\$2F (joystick confirmation) is displayed.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{172}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-IJNWOWVOLMPQXWDRQGGDMX6BUI000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-IJNWOWVOLMPQXWDRQGGDMX6BUI000000-1}}}\moddef{select input mode~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-IJNWOWVOLMPQXWDRQGGDMX6BUI000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $084E
\nwlinkedidentc{SELECT_INPUT_MODE}{PYNWmai0-IJNWOWVOLMPQXWDRQGGDMX6BUI000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    LDA     #$38                    ; message $38: input mode prompt
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{DISPLAY_MESSAGE}{PYNWmai0-PLQAK2MUE37THNKRCI7RJB7UJY000000-1}
    LDA     $C061                   ; read paddle button 1
    AND     #$80                    ; isolate bit 7 (pressed state)
    STA     $BA                     ; save initial button state
.clear:
    STA     $C010                   ; clear keyboard strobe
.poll:
    LDX     $C000                   ; read keyboard
    BMI     .key                    ; key pressed → check it
    LDA     $C061                   ; re-read paddle button
    EOR     $BA                     ; compare with initial state
    BMI     .joystick               ; button state changed → joystick
    BPL     .poll                   ; keep polling
.key:
    CPX     #$A0                    ; space bar?
    BEQ     .keyboard               ; yes → keyboard mode
    BNE     .clear                  ; other key → ignore, clear strobe
.keyboard:
    LDA     #$00
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{INPUT_MODE}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-10}              ; 0 = keyboard
    RTS
.joystick:
    LDA     #$01
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{INPUT_MODE}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-10}              ; 1 = joystick
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SET_CURSOR_ROW21}{PYNWmai0-UOBA5Y3PKYLQKGPLIBUCA3M2SE000000-1}
    LDA     #$2F                    ; message $2F: joystick confirmation
    JMP     \nwlinkedidentc{DISPLAY_MESSAGE}{PYNWmai0-PLQAK2MUE37THNKRCI7RJB7UJY000000-1}
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{SELECT{\_}INPUT{\_}MODE}}{SELECT:unINPUT:unMODE}{PYNWmai0-IJNWOWVOLMPQXWDRQGGDMX6BUI000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{SELECT{\_}INPUT{\_}MODE}}{SELECT:unINPUT:unMODE}}}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{DISPLAY{\_}MESSAGE}}{DISPLAY:unMESSAGE}}\\{{\nwixident{INPUT{\_}MODE}}{INPUT:unMODE}}\\{{\nwixident{SET{\_}CURSOR{\_}ROW21}}{SET:unCURSOR:unROW21}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{DISPLAY{\_}MESSAGE}}{DISPLAY:unMESSAGE}{PYNWmai0-IJNWOWVOLMPQXWDRQGGDMX6BUI000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{INPUT{\_}MODE}}{INPUT:unMODE}{PYNWmai0-IJNWOWVOLMPQXWDRQGGDMX6BUI000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SET{\_}CURSOR{\_}ROW21}}{SET:unCURSOR:unROW21}{PYNWmai0-IJNWOWVOLMPQXWDRQGGDMX6BUI000000-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{173}\nwdocspar

\subsection{init\_world (\$62E5)}

Thin wrapper that passes a pointer to the world initialization data
at {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}62B9\nwendquote} to the game setup routine at {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}5F19\nwendquote}.  Called once
from {\Tt{}GAME{\textbackslash}{\_}INIT\nwendquote} to initialize locations and scene state.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{174}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-KCDZMKWSK2V7SIS3PFUTBW2DJQ000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-KCDZMKWSK2V7SIS3PFUTBW2DJQ000000-1}}}\moddef{init world~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-KCDZMKWSK2V7SIS3PFUTBW2DJQ000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $62E5
INIT_WORLD:
    SUBROUTINE

    LDX     #>\nwlinkedidentc{WORLD_INIT_DATA}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-11}       ; \\ X/Y = pointer to init data
    LDY     #<\nwlinkedidentc{WORLD_INIT_DATA}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-11}       ; /
    JMP     $5F19                   ; initialize world from data table

\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{WORLD{\_}INIT{\_}DATA}}{WORLD:unINIT:unDATA}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{WORLD{\_}INIT{\_}DATA}}{WORLD:unINIT:unDATA}{PYNWmai0-KCDZMKWSK2V7SIS3PFUTBW2DJQ000000-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegincode{175}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-11}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-11}}}\moddef{defines~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-1}}}\plusendmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwprevnextdefs{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-10}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-12}\nwenddeflinemarkup
\nwlinkedidentc{WORLD_INIT_DATA}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-11}         EQU     $62B9   ; world initialization data table

\subsection{game\_init (\$78C7)}

Sets up the Apple II for the game---reset vector, graphics mode, and
various subsystem initialization.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{178}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-XR5IMSHLGD4AKOBGLQGCQ6POTY000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-XR5IMSHLGD4AKOBGLQGCQ6POTY000000-1}}}\moddef{game init~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-XR5IMSHLGD4AKOBGLQGCQ6POTY000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $78C7

    SUBROUTINE

    LDX     #$6F                    ; \\
    LDY     #$A5                    ;  | reset vector = $A56F
    STX     $03F2                   ;  |
    STY     $03F3                   ; /
    JSR     $FB6F                   ; ROM: set reset vector checksum
    LDA     #$14
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{BLINK_COL}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-5}               ; disable blink cursor
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{RELOCATE_HIRES_STAGING}{PYNWmai0-2NL3TPDIV6BH32KNILRIC2G5ZE000000-1}  ; copy $2000+ to $9600+/$B300+
    LDA     $C050                   ; GR mode
    LDA     $C052                   ; full screen (no text split)
    LDA     $C054                   ; page 1
    LDA     $C057                   ; hi-res
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{INIT_DISK_IOB}{PYNWmai0-MFXGDBBCK3Q7RVR5U57NVVC6RI000000-1}
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{INIT_HRCG}{PYNWmai0-ZKKBW7IOFWPQONKCR23DIN7HAI000000-1}
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SET_TEXT_WINDOW_WRAP}{PYNWmai0-GPDXH5KV66ADU2Z2YB5ZFVWGM4000000-1}
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{INIT_STUB}{PYNWmai0-A5IDJFPW4YOQ5EAI2Y4LCAAB5U000000-1}
    JSR     INIT_GAME_STATE
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{FILL_MAP}{PYNWmai0-GLAMCDF6RJVWAHNXVLZP2YDB7M000000-1}
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SET_TEXT_WINDOW_BOTTOM}{PYNWmai0-UOBA5Y3PKYLQKGPLIBUCA3M2SE000000-1}
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{INIT_STUB2}{PYNWmai0-IFY6XEMQGG4JTQ6TNKPP64CWGA000000-1}

    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{LOCATION_FLAG2}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-10}          ;  |
    STA     $F9                     ; /

    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{INIT_MOB_COUNT}{PYNWmai0-FUVGEE5QFLBSHT5MZWRVT5CDCY000000-1}

    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{CURRENT_PLAYER}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-10}
    RTS

ent{SELECT{\_}INPUT{\_}MODE}}{SELECT:unINPUT:unMODE}{PYNWmai0-XR5IMSHLGD4AKOBGLQGCQ6POTY000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SET{\_}TEXT{\_}WINDOW{\_}BOTTOM}}{SET:unTEXT:unWINDOW:unBOTTOM}{PYNWmai0-XR5IMSHLGD4AKOBGLQGCQ6POTY000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SET{\_}TEXT{\_}WINDOW{\_}WRAP}}{SET:unTEXT:unWINDOW:unWRAP}{PYNWmai0-XR5IMSHLGD4AKOBGLQGCQ6POTY000000-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{179}\nwdocspar

The soft-switch reads at {\Tt{}{\$}C050\nwendquote}--{\Tt{}{\$}C057\nwendquote} configure the Apple II display:
{\Tt{}GR\nwendquote}, full-screen (no split text), page 1, hi-res. This puts the display
into HGR mode showing the framebuffer at {\Tt{}{\$}2000\nwendquote}--{\Tt{}{\$}3FFF\nwendquote}.

\subsection{attract\_screen (\$09F4)}
\label{sec:attract_screen}

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{180}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-J5774R6PCWTLDLXH4MIVVDMLZE000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-J5774R6PCWTLDLXH4MIVVDMLZE000000-1}}}\moddef{attract screen~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-J5774R6PCWTLDLXH4MIVVDMLZE000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $09F4
\nwlinkedidentc{ATTRACT_SCREEN}{PYNWmai0-J5774R6PCWTLDLXH4MIVVDMLZE000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    LDA     #$01
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{ACTIVE_CHAR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-10}             ; scene/character index = 1
    STA     $423E                   ; flag
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{COMPUTE_SCENE_PTR}{PYNWmai0-AW5VLYKLITE6VBTFNOR2WD6FNQ000000-1}       ; scene 1 pointer → $BA/$BB
    LDA     $BA                     ; \\
    STA     $F4                     ;  | $F4/$F5 = $BA/$BB (save pointer)
    LDA     $BB                     ;  |
    STA     $F5                     ; /
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SCENE_SETUP}{PYNWmai0-EDKCSDZ4YL2YCTUIJVHBQRMHYY000000-1}
    LDA     #$00
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{LOCATION_FLAG}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-10}           ; clear location-change flag
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SET_CURSOR_ROW21}{PYNWmai0-UOBA5Y3PKYLQKGPLIBUCA3M2SE000000-1}
    LDA     #$26                    ; scene number $26 (38 decimal)
    JMP     \nwlinkedidentc{SCENE_LOOP}{PYNWmai0-5E23YPEUUG4SZHWM2ZQ6MSHERE000000-1}              ; tail-call
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{ATTRACT{\_}SCREEN}}{ATTRACT:unSCREEN}{PYNWmai0-J5774R6PCWTLDLXH4MIVVDMLZE000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{ATTRACT{\_}SCREEN}}{ATTRACT:unSCREEN}}}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{ACTIVE{\_}CHAR}}{ACTIVE:unCHAR}}\\{{\nwixident{COMPUTE{\_}SCENE{\_}PTR}}{COMPUTE:unSCENE:unPTR}}\\{{\nwixident{LOCATION{\_}FLAG}}{LOCATION:unFLAG}}\\{{\nwixident{SCENE{\_}LOOP}}{SCENE:unLOOP}}\\{{\nwixident{SCENE{\_}SETUP}}{SCENE:unSETUP}}\\{{\nwixident{SET{\_}CURSOR{\_}ROW21}}{SET:unCURSOR:unROW21}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{ACTIVE{\_}CHAR}}{ACTIVE:unCHAR}{PYNWmai0-J5774R6PCWTLDLXH4MIVVDMLZE000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{COMPUTE{\_}SCENE{\_}PTR}}{COMPUTE:unSCENE:unPTR}{PYNWmai0-J5774R6PCWTLDLXH4MIVVDMLZE000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{LOCATION{\_}FLAG}}{LOCATION:unFLAG}{PYNWmai0-J5774R6PCWTLDLXH4MIVVDMLZE000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SCENE{\_}LOOP}}{SCENE:unLOOP}{PYNWmai0-J5774R6PCWTLDLXH4MIVVDMLZE000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SCENE{\_}SETUP}}{SCENE:unSETUP}{PYNWmai0-J5774R6PCWTLDLXH4MIVVDMLZE000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SET{\_}CURSOR{\_}ROW21}}{SET:unCURSOR:unROW21}{PYNWmai0-J5774R6PCWTLDLXH4MIVVDMLZE000000-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{181}\nwdocspar

The attract screen starts with scene index 1 (the first story character
setup) and begins playing scene \$26.

\subsection{decr/incr\_group\_count (\$102F/\$1033)}

Characters are organized into groups via linked lists threaded through
byte~2 of each 16-byte mob data record (accessed via {\Tt{}GET{\textbackslash}{\_}MOB{\textbackslash}{\_}DATA\nwendquote}).
Byte~8 of the \emph{group head}'s mob data record is a packed field:
\begin{itemize}
\item bits 3--0: \textbf{group member count} --- how many characters
      are in this group's chain (0--4 in initial data)
\item bits 6--4: \textbf{pending XP} --- experience points accumulated
      but not yet applied to the character's level (0--7).
      The XP award routine at~\$7248 writes new values here; the
      flush routine at~\$6EE9 adds pending XP to byte~11's level
      field and clears it.
\item bit~7: \textbf{status flag} --- always zero in initial data;
      set during gameplay (controls message selection at~\$18AB).
      Preserved across XP flush.
\end{itemize}

These two entry points adjust the group member count (low nibble of
byte~8) on the head record pointed to by~{\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}BE/{\textbackslash}{\$}BF\nwendquote}:
\begin{itemize}
\item {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}102F\nwendquote} ({\Tt{}DECR{\textbackslash}{\_}GROUP{\textbackslash}{\_}COUNT\nwendquote}): decrements by~1 (source group lost a member)
\item {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}1033\nwendquote} ({\Tt{}INCR{\textbackslash}{\_}GROUP{\textbackslash}{\_}COUNT\nwendquote}): increments by~1 (destination group gained a member)
\end{itemize}
Guards: bails out if {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}BE\nwendquote} is zero (null pointer) or if byte~4 of the
record at~{\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}BC/{\textbackslash}{\$}BD\nwendquote} is~$\ge$~\$15 (inactive/dead character).
Called exclusively from {\Tt{}REORDER{\textbackslash}{\_}CHAR\nwendquote} (\$0F84).

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{182}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-54W2OTUWX7KPVKAUABQU6MTVVE000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-54W2OTUWX7KPVKAUABQU6MTVVE000000-1}}}\moddef{adjust char byte8~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-54W2OTUWX7KPVKAUABQU6MTVVE000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $102F
\nwlinkedidentc{DECR_GROUP_COUNT}{PYNWmai0-54W2OTUWX7KPVKAUABQU6MTVVE000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    LDA     #$FF                    ; delta = -1
    BNE     .apply                  ; always taken
\nwlinkedidentc{INCR_GROUP_COUNT}{PYNWmai0-54W2OTUWX7KPVKAUABQU6MTVVE000000-1}:
    LDA     #$01                    ; delta = +1
.apply:
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{GROUP_COUNT_DELTA}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-9}       ; save delta for later
    LDA     $BE                     ; \\
    CMP     #$00                    ;  | bail if $BE/$BF is null
    BNE     .not_null               ;  |
    RTS                             ; /
.not_null:
    LDY     #$04                    ; \\
    LDA     ($BC),Y                 ;  | bail if byte 4 of ($BC) >= $15
    CMP     #$15                    ;  |   ($15+ = inactive/dead)
    BCC     .ok                     ;  |
    RTS                             ; /
.ok:
    LDY     #$08                    ; \\
    LDA     ($BE),Y                 ;  | group count (low nibble) += delta
    CLC                             ;  |
    ADC     \nwlinkedidentc{GROUP_COUNT_DELTA}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-9}       ;  |
    STA     ($BE),Y                 ; /
    RTS
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{DECR{\_}GROUP{\_}COUNT}}{DECR:unGROUP:unCOUNT}{PYNWmai0-54W2OTUWX7KPVKAUABQU6MTVVE000000-1}\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{INCR{\_}GROUP{\_}COUNT}}{INCR:unGROUP:unCOUNT}{PYNWmai0-54W2OTUWX7KPVKAUABQU6MTVVE000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{DECR{\_}GROUP{\_}COUNT}}{DECR:unGROUP:unCOUNT}}\\{{\nwixident{INCR{\_}GROUP{\_}COUNT}}{INCR:unGROUP:unCOUNT}}}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{GROUP{\_}COUNT{\_}DELTA}}{GROUP:unCOUNT:unDELTA}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{GROUP{\_}COUNT{\_}DELTA}}{GROUP:unCOUNT:unDELTA}{PYNWmai0-54W2OTUWX7KPVKAUABQU6MTVVE000000-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{183}\nwdocspar

\subsection{reorder\_char (\$0F84)}

Performs one step of an insertion-sort on a linked list of characters,
ordered by byte~11 (level, masked to 5~bits).  It unlinks the character
at index~{\Tt{}SOURCE{\textbackslash}{\_}CHAR\nwendquote} from the list and re-inserts it in sorted order
relative to index~{\Tt{}ACTIVE{\textbackslash}{\_}CHAR\nwendquote}.

The linked-list ``next'' pointer is byte~2 of each character record.
{\Tt{}GET{\textbackslash}{\_}MOB{\textbackslash}{\_}DATA\nwendquote} (\$0C32) resolves a byte-2 value into a record pointer
at {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}BA/{\textbackslash}{\$}BB\nwendquote}.

Phase~1 (removal): walks the chain from {\Tt{}SOURCE{\textbackslash}{\_}CHAR\nwendquote}'s record, following
byte-2 links via {\Tt{}GET{\textbackslash}{\_}MOB{\textbackslash}{\_}DATA\nwendquote} until {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}BA/{\textbackslash}{\$}BB\nwendquote} equals
{\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}BC/{\textbackslash}{\$}BD\nwendquote} (found the predecessor).  Then patches the predecessor's
byte~2 to skip the removed node.  Decrements the source group's
member count via {\Tt{}DECR{\textbackslash}{\_}GROUP{\textbackslash}{\_}COUNT\nwendquote}.

Phase~2 (insertion): walks the chain from {\Tt{}ACTIVE{\textbackslash}{\_}CHAR\nwendquote}'s record, comparing
byte~11 (level) values.  Inserts the removed character before the first
node with a lower level, or at the end if none found.  Increments the
destination group's member count via {\Tt{}INCR{\textbackslash}{\_}GROUP{\textbackslash}{\_}COUNT\nwendquote}.  Adjusts the
{\Tt{}TOTAL{\textbackslash}{\_}MOB{\textbackslash}{\_}COUNT\nwendquote} to track list membership changes.

When {\Tt{}ACTIVE{\textbackslash}{\_}CHAR\nwendquote} is zero, a random decision (via {\Tt{}STEP{\textbackslash}{\_}PRNG\nwendquote}) determines
the insertion point instead of the level comparison.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{184}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-TSZHS7O2FMNRYEK2W57DEKVPQE000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-TSZHS7O2FMNRYEK2W57DEKVPQE000000-1}}}\moddef{reorder char~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-TSZHS7O2FMNRYEK2W57DEKVPQE000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $0F84
\nwlinkedidentc{REORDER_CHAR}{PYNWmai0-TSZHS7O2FMNRYEK2W57DEKVPQE000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

; --- Phase 1: unlink character \nwlinkedidentc{SOURCE_CHAR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-10} from its current chain ---
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{SOURCE_CHAR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-10}             ; source character index
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{GET_CHAR_RECORD}{PYNWmai0-PDZVFDW3WMN7YKZPZWVSWNODJE000000-1}         ; $BE/$BF = record pointer
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{DECR_GROUP_COUNT}{PYNWmai0-54W2OTUWX7KPVKAUABQU6MTVVE000000-1}        ; source group lost a member
.walk1:
    LDY     #$02                    ; \\
    LDA     ($BE),Y                 ;  | \nwlinkedidentc{REORDER_LINK}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-10} = byte 2 of current record
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{REORDER_LINK}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-10}            ; /  (the "next" link we're removing)
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{GET_MOB_DATA}{PYNWmai0-VTKXUQPSOCRIDYWOEIFECHPTSM000000-1}            ; $BA/$BB = resolve link; $BC/$BD = mob data
    LDA     $BA                     ; \\
    CMP     $BC                     ;  | compare $BA/$BB with $BC/$BD
    BNE     .advance1               ;  | if different, keep walking
    LDA     $BB                     ;  |
    CMP     $BD                     ; /
    BNE     .advance1
    ; Found predecessor: $BC/$BD points to the node being removed
    LDY     #$02
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{REORDER_LINK}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-10}            ; \\  if removed node's link == $5A03,
    CMP     $5A03                   ;  |   update $5A03 to new link
    BNE     .patch1                 ; /
    LDA     ($BC),Y                 ; \\
    STA     $5A03                   ; /  $5A03 = ($BC)[2] (successor's link)
.patch1:
    LDA     ($BC),Y                 ; \\  predecessor.byte2 = removed.byte2
    STA     ($BE),Y                 ; /  (skip over removed node)
    JMP     .phase2
.advance1:
    LDA     $BA                     ; \\  $BE/$BF = $BA/$BB
    STA     $BE                     ;  | (advance to next record)
    LDA     $BB                     ;  |
    STA     $BF                     ; /
    JMP     .walk1

; --- Phase 2: re-insert at correct sorted position in \nwlinkedidentc{ACTIVE_CHAR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-10}'s chain ---
.phase2:
    LDY     #$0B                    ; \\
    LDA     ($BC),Y                 ;  | \nwlinkedidentc{REORDER_SORT_KEY}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-10} = byte 11 of removed node
    AND     #$1F                    ;  |   (level, 5-bit)
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{REORDER_SORT_KEY}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-10}        ; /
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{ACTIVE_CHAR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-10}             ; destination character index
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{GET_CHAR_RECORD}{PYNWmai0-PDZVFDW3WMN7YKZPZWVSWNODJE000000-1}         ; $BE/$BF = dest record pointer
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{INCR_GROUP_COUNT}{PYNWmai0-54W2OTUWX7KPVKAUABQU6MTVVE000000-1}        ; dest group gained a member
.walk2:
    LDY     #$02                    ; \\
    LDA     ($BE),Y                 ;  | check byte 2 of current record
    CMP     #$00                    ;  | if zero (end of chain) -> insert here
    BEQ     .insert                 ; /
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{GET_MOB_DATA}{PYNWmai0-VTKXUQPSOCRIDYWOEIFECHPTSM000000-1}            ; resolve link
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{ACTIVE_CHAR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-10}             ; \\
    BEQ     .random                 ; /  if dest index = 0, use random decision
    LDY     #$0B                    ; \\
    LDA     ($BA),Y                 ;  | compare candidate's level
    AND     #$1F                    ;  | with removed node's level
    CMP     \nwlinkedidentc{REORDER_SORT_KEY}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-10}        ;  |
    BPL     .advance2               ; /  if >= , keep walking (insert later)
.insert:
    LDY     #$02                    ; \\
    LDA     ($BE),Y                 ;  | ($BC)[2] = ($BE)[2]  (link successor)
    STA     ($BC),Y                 ;  |
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{REORDER_LINK}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-10}            ;  | ($BE)[2] = saved link (insert node)
    STA     ($BE),Y                 ; /
    LDY     #$04                    ; \\
    LDA     ($BC),Y                 ;  | if byte 4 of ($BC) >= $15, done
    CMP     #$15                    ;  |
    BCC     .adjust                 ;  |
    RTS                             ; /
.adjust:
    LDA     #$00                    ; \\
    CMP     \nwlinkedidentc{ACTIVE_CHAR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-10}             ;  | if inserted into index 0's slot,
    BNE     .chk28                  ;  |   decrement \nwlinkedidentc{TOTAL_MOB_COUNT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-10}
    DEC     \nwlinkedidentc{TOTAL_MOB_COUNT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-10}         ; /
.chk28:
    CMP     \nwlinkedidentc{SOURCE_CHAR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-10}             ; \\  if removed from index 0's slot,
    BNE     .done                   ;  |   increment \nwlinkedidentc{TOTAL_MOB_COUNT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-10}
    INC     \nwlinkedidentc{TOTAL_MOB_COUNT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-10}         ; /
.done:
    RTS
.advance2:
    LDA     $BA                     ; \\  $BE/$BF = $BA/$BB
    STA     $BE                     ;  | (advance to next record)
    LDA     $BB                     ;  |
    STA     $BF                     ; /
    JMP     .walk2
.random:
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{STEP_PRNG}{PYNWmai0-3OGDZ4EYEYE7YXQHNEV2CZPRBM000000-1}               ; \\  random decision
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{PRNG_OUTPUT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-9}             ;  | if PRNG < 1 (i.e., == 0) -> insert
    CMP     #$01                    ;  |
    BMI     .insert                 ;  | else keep walking
    BPL     .advance2               ; /
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{REORDER{\_}CHAR}}{REORDER:unCHAR}{PYNWmai0-TSZHS7O2FMNRYEK2W57DEKVPQE000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{REORDER{\_}CHAR}}{REORDER:unCHAR}}}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{ACTIVE{\_}CHAR}}{ACTIVE:unCHAR}}\\{{\nwixident{DECR{\_}GROUP{\_}COUNT}}{DECR:unGROUP:unCOUNT}}\\{{\nwixident{GET{\_}CHAR{\_}RECORD}}{GET:unCHAR:unRECORD}}\\{{\nwixident{GET{\_}MOB{\_}DATA}}{GET:unMOB:unDATA}}\\{{\nwixident{INCR{\_}GROUP{\_}COUNT}}{INCR:unGROUP:unCOUNT}}\\{{\nwixident{PRNG{\_}OUTPUT}}{PRNG:unOUTPUT}}\\{{\nwixident{REORDER{\_}LINK}}{REORDER:unLINK}}\\{{\nwixident{REORDER{\_}SORT{\_}KEY}}{REORDER:unSORT:unKEY}}\\{{\nwixident{SOURCE{\_}CHAR}}{SOURCE:unCHAR}}\\{{\nwixident{STEP{\_}PRNG}}{STEP:unPRNG}}\\{{\nwixident{TOTAL{\_}MOB{\_}COUNT}}{TOTAL:unMOB:unCOUNT}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{ACTIVE{\_}CHAR}}{ACTIVE:unCHAR}{PYNWmai0-TSZHS7O2FMNRYEK2W57DEKVPQE000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{DECR{\_}GROUP{\_}COUNT}}{DECR:unGROUP:unCOUNT}{PYNWmai0-TSZHS7O2FMNRYEK2W57DEKVPQE000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{GET{\_}CHAR{\_}RECORD}}{GET:unCHAR:unRECORD}{PYNWmai0-TSZHS7O2FMNRYEK2W57DEKVPQE000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{GET{\_}MOB{\_}DATA}}{GET:unMOB:unDATA}{PYNWmai0-TSZHS7O2FMNRYEK2W57DEKVPQE000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{INCR{\_}GROUP{\_}COUNT}}{INCR:unGROUP:unCOUNT}{PYNWmai0-TSZHS7O2FMNRYEK2W57DEKVPQE000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{PRNG{\_}OUTPUT}}{PRNG:unOUTPUT}{PYNWmai0-TSZHS7O2FMNRYEK2W57DEKVPQE000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{REORDER{\_}LINK}}{REORDER:unLINK}{PYNWmai0-TSZHS7O2FMNRYEK2W57DEKVPQE000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{REORDER{\_}SORT{\_}KEY}}{REORDER:unSORT:unKEY}{PYNWmai0-TSZHS7O2FMNRYEK2W57DEKVPQE000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SOURCE{\_}CHAR}}{SOURCE:unCHAR}{PYNWmai0-TSZHS7O2FMNRYEK2W57DEKVPQE000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{STEP{\_}PRNG}}{STEP:unPRNG}{PYNWmai0-TSZHS7O2FMNRYEK2W57DEKVPQE000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{TOTAL{\_}MOB{\_}COUNT}}{TOTAL:unMOB:unCOUNT}{PYNWmai0-TSZHS7O2FMNRYEK2W57DEKVPQE000000-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{185}\nwdocspar

\subsection{get\_char\_record (\$1053)}

Computes a pointer to a character record from a 1-based index in~A.
Each character record is 9~bytes, stored sequentially starting at {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}4000\nwendquote}.
Returns {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}BE/{\textbackslash}{\$}BF\ =\ {\textbackslash}{\$}4000\ +\ A\ {\$}{\textbackslash}times{\$}\ 9\nwendquote}.  If A~=~0, returns
{\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}BE/{\textbackslash}{\$}BF\ =\ {\textbackslash}{\$}4000\nwendquote} immediately (index 0 is the base/header record).

Note: Ghidra groups this with a separate routine at {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}106F\nwendquote} (entered via
JMP from other functions) that handles character elimination/death logic.
That code is not part of this entry point's normal return path.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{186}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-PDZVFDW3WMN7YKZPZWVSWNODJE000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-PDZVFDW3WMN7YKZPZWVSWNODJE000000-1}}}\moddef{get char record~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-PDZVFDW3WMN7YKZPZWVSWNODJE000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $1053
\nwlinkedidentc{GET_CHAR_RECORD}{PYNWmai0-PDZVFDW3WMN7YKZPZWVSWNODJE000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    TAX                             ; X = index (loop counter)
    LDA     #$00                    ; \\
    STA     $BE                     ;  | $BE/$BF = $4000 (base)
    LDA     #$40                    ;  |
    STA     $BF                     ; /
.loop:
    DEX
    BPL     .advance                ; more records to skip
    RTS                             ; done: $BE/$BF points to record
.advance:
    CLC                             ; \\
    LDA     $BE                     ;  | $BE/$BF += 9
    ADC     #$09                    ;  | (9 bytes per record)
    STA     $BE                     ;  |
    LDA     $BF                     ;  |
    ADC     #$00                    ;  |
    STA     $BF                     ; /
    BNE     .loop                   ; always taken ($BF >= $40)
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{GET{\_}CHAR{\_}RECORD}}{GET:unCHAR:unRECORD}{PYNWmai0-PDZVFDW3WMN7YKZPZWVSWNODJE000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{GET{\_}CHAR{\_}RECORD}}{GET:unCHAR:unRECORD}}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{187}\nwdocspar

\subsection{scene\_setup (\$0A17)}

Initializes a scene for display.  Loads the character record for index
{\Tt{}ACTIVE{\textbackslash}{\_}CHAR\nwendquote}, reads the character's bounding box from bytes~3--4 of the
record at {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}BE\nwendquote}, converts to column/row ranges, picks a random
position within those bounds, sets the font cursor there, and performs
additional character-record bookkeeping.

The bounding box bytes are packed map positions decoded by
{\Tt{}POS{\textbackslash}{\_}TO{\textbackslash}{\_}COLROW\nwendquote}.  The routine increments the minimums (so the range
is exclusive of the border), then calls {\Tt{}RANDOM{\textbackslash}{\_}IN{\textbackslash}{\_}RANGE\nwendquote} twice to
pick a random column and row within the bounds.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{188}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-EDKCSDZ4YL2YCTUIJVHBQRMHYY000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-EDKCSDZ4YL2YCTUIJVHBQRMHYY000000-1}}}\moddef{scene setup~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-EDKCSDZ4YL2YCTUIJVHBQRMHYY000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $0A17
\nwlinkedidentc{SCENE_SETUP}{PYNWmai0-EDKCSDZ4YL2YCTUIJVHBQRMHYY000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{ACTIVE_CHAR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-10}             ; character/scene index
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{GET_CHAR_RECORD}{PYNWmai0-PDZVFDW3WMN7YKZPZWVSWNODJE000000-1}         ; index → $BE/$BF = char record
    LDY     #$03
    LDA     ($BE),Y                 ; byte 3: min position (packed)
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{POS_TO_COLROW}{PYNWmai0-AMTAHZ55D6ORMSENT2EMDCDU24000000-1}           ; → A=min_col, Y=min_row
    STA     $5A51                   ; min_col
    STY     $5A53                   ; min_row
    LDY     #$04
    LDA     ($BE),Y                 ; byte 4: max position (packed)
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{POS_TO_COLROW}{PYNWmai0-AMTAHZ55D6ORMSENT2EMDCDU24000000-1}           ; → A=max_col, Y=max_row
    STA     $5A52                   ; max_col
    STY     $5A54                   ; max_row
    INC     $5A51                   ; min_col++ (exclusive border)
    INC     $5A53                   ; min_row++
    CLC
    LDA     $5A52                   ; \\
    SBC     $5A51                   ;  | col_range = max_col - min_col
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{RANDOM_IN_RANGE}{PYNWmai0-F6322QSFMTRJBO2IS2F3GEYRZU000000-1}         ;  | random column offset
    CLC                             ;  |
    ADC     $5A51                   ;  | col = min_col + offset
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{FONT_COL}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-3}                ; / set font column
    CLC
    LDA     $5A54                   ; \\
    SBC     $5A53                   ;  | row_range = max_row - min_row
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{RANDOM_IN_RANGE}{PYNWmai0-F6322QSFMTRJBO2IS2F3GEYRZU000000-1}         ;  | random row offset
    CLC                             ;  |
    ADC     $5A53                   ; / row = min_row + offset
    TAY                             ; Y = row
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{FONT_COL}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-3}                ; A = col
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{COLROW_TO_POS}{PYNWmai0-YXZOC7KQXOV5OPKZ6P7KWNTLUM000000-1}           ; → A = linear position
    LDY     #$03
    STA     ($F4),Y                 ; store position in record byte 3
    LDA     $F4                     ; \\
    STA     $BC                     ;  | $BC/$BD = $F4/$F5
    LDA     $F5                     ;  |
    STA     $BD                     ; /
    LDA     #$00
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{SOURCE_CHAR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-10}             ; clear source char index
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{REORDER_CHAR}{PYNWmai0-TSZHS7O2FMNRYEK2W57DEKVPQE000000-1}            ; reorder character in linked list
    LDY     #$0D
    LDA     #$00                    ; \\
    STA     ($F4),Y                 ;  | clear bytes 13-14 of record
    INY                             ;  |
    STA     ($F4),Y                 ; /
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{CLAMP_CHAR_FIELD}{PYNWmai0-VZAAE44D7YBBIC7MO6FZNDLI6M000000-1}        ; ensure byte 6 >= byte 5 minimum
    LDA     $5A02                   ; current player index
    CMP     \nwlinkedidentc{ACTIVE_CHAR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-10}             ; compare with scene index
    BNE     .done                   ; not current player → skip
    LDY     #$03
    LDA     ($F4),Y                 ; load position from record
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{DRAW_CHAR_AT_POS}{PYNWmai0-RAACK23HC5EFMXFBXXME6ZKJTE000000-1}        ; draw character at position
.done:
    RTS
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{SCENE{\_}SETUP}}{SCENE:unSETUP}{PYNWmai0-EDKCSDZ4YL2YCTUIJVHBQRMHYY000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{SCENE{\_}SETUP}}{SCENE:unSETUP}}}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{ACTIVE{\_}CHAR}}{ACTIVE:unCHAR}}\\{{\nwixident{CLAMP{\_}CHAR{\_}FIELD}}{CLAMP:unCHAR:unFIELD}}\\{{\nwixident{COLROW{\_}TO{\_}POS}}{COLROW:unTO:unPOS}}\\{{\nwixident{DRAW{\_}CHAR{\_}AT{\_}POS}}{DRAW:unCHAR:unAT:unPOS}}\\{{\nwixident{FONT{\_}COL}}{FONT:unCOL}}\\{{\nwixident{GET{\_}CHAR{\_}RECORD}}{GET:unCHAR:unRECORD}}\\{{\nwixident{POS{\_}TO{\_}COLROW}}{POS:unTO:unCOLROW}}\\{{\nwixident{RANDOM{\_}IN{\_}RANGE}}{RANDOM:unIN:unRANGE}}\\{{\nwixident{REORDER{\_}CHAR}}{REORDER:unCHAR}}\\{{\nwixident{SOURCE{\_}CHAR}}{SOURCE:unCHAR}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{ACTIVE{\_}CHAR}}{ACTIVE:unCHAR}{PYNWmai0-EDKCSDZ4YL2YCTUIJVHBQRMHYY000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{CLAMP{\_}CHAR{\_}FIELD}}{CLAMP:unCHAR:unFIELD}{PYNWmai0-EDKCSDZ4YL2YCTUIJVHBQRMHYY000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{COLROW{\_}TO{\_}POS}}{COLROW:unTO:unPOS}{PYNWmai0-EDKCSDZ4YL2YCTUIJVHBQRMHYY000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{DRAW{\_}CHAR{\_}AT{\_}POS}}{DRAW:unCHAR:unAT:unPOS}{PYNWmai0-EDKCSDZ4YL2YCTUIJVHBQRMHYY000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{FONT{\_}COL}}{FONT:unCOL}{PYNWmai0-EDKCSDZ4YL2YCTUIJVHBQRMHYY000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{GET{\_}CHAR{\_}RECORD}}{GET:unCHAR:unRECORD}{PYNWmai0-EDKCSDZ4YL2YCTUIJVHBQRMHYY000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{POS{\_}TO{\_}COLROW}}{POS:unTO:unCOLROW}{PYNWmai0-EDKCSDZ4YL2YCTUIJVHBQRMHYY000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{RANDOM{\_}IN{\_}RANGE}}{RANDOM:unIN:unRANGE}{PYNWmai0-EDKCSDZ4YL2YCTUIJVHBQRMHYY000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{REORDER{\_}CHAR}}{REORDER:unCHAR}{PYNWmai0-EDKCSDZ4YL2YCTUIJVHBQRMHYY000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SOURCE{\_}CHAR}}{SOURCE:unCHAR}{PYNWmai0-EDKCSDZ4YL2YCTUIJVHBQRMHYY000000-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{189}\nwdocspar

\subsection{scene\_loop (\$6C37)}
\subsection{init\_disk\_iob (\$6C2E)}

Sets the zero-page pointer {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}08/{\textbackslash}{\$}09\nwendquote} to the RWTS Input/Output Block
at {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}B7E8\nwendquote}.  Called once during {\Tt{}GAME{\textbackslash}{\_}INIT\nwendquote}.  The game's disk I/O
routines (relocated to \$B300--\$BFFF during {\Tt{}game{\textbackslash}{\_}init\nwendquote}) use this
pointer to access the IOB fields via indirect-indexed addressing:
e.g.\ {\Tt{}STA\ ({\textbackslash}{\$}08),Y\nwendquote} with {\Tt{}Y\nwendquote} selecting the field (track, sector,
command code, buffer address, etc.).  The RWTS entry point is at {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}B7B5\nwendquote}.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{190}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-AJE4SNIWWSAT23GB2VNG3SS6JI000000-3}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-AJE4SNIWWSAT23GB2VNG3SS6JI000000-3}}}\moddef{zero page defines~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-AJE4SNIWWSAT23GB2VNG3SS6JI000000-1}}}\plusendmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwprevnextdefs{PYNWmai0-AJE4SNIWWSAT23GB2VNG3SS6JI000000-2}{\relax}\nwenddeflinemarkup
\nwlinkedidentc{RWTS_IOB_PTR}{PYNWmai0-AJE4SNIWWSAT23GB2VNG3SS6JI000000-3}            EQU     $08     ; ZP pointer to RWTS IOB ($B7E8)
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{RWTS{\_}IOB{\_}PTR}}{RWTS:unIOB:unPTR}{PYNWmai0-AJE4SNIWWSAT23GB2VNG3SS6JI000000-3}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{RWTS{\_}IOB{\_}PTR}}{RWTS:unIOB:unPTR}}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{191}\nwdocspar

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{192}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-12}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-12}}}\moddef{defines~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-1}}}\plusendmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwprevnextdefs{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-11}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-13}\nwenddeflinemarkup

\label{sec:scene_loop}

This is the main scene display loop.  It is called with the scene number
in~A.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{198}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-5E23YPEUUG4SZHWM2ZQ6MSHERE000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-5E23YPEUUG4SZHWM2ZQ6MSHERE000000-1}}}\moddef{scene loop~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-5E23YPEUUG4SZHWM2ZQ6MSHERE000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $6C37
\nwlinkedidentc{SCENE_LOOP}{PYNWmai0-5E23YPEUUG4SZHWM2ZQ6MSHERE000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{SCENE_NUMBER}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-10}            ; store scene number
    LDA     #$14
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{BLINK_COL}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-5}               ; disable blink cursor

    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SAVE_ZP_POINTERS}{PYNWmai0-XTFMNQODSGOW3IGUAVI6HJU56I000000-1}

    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{STEP_PRNG}{PYNWmai0-3OGDZ4EYEYE7YXQHNEV2CZPRBM000000-1}
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{PRNG_OUTPUT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-9}             ; PRNG output
    AND     #$0A                    ; test bits 1 and 3
    BNE     .display                ; if any set, skip disk load
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{LOAD_SCENE_DATA}{PYNWmai0-3XMQPOG4ARI455O23BBDT5GCTE000000-1}

.display:
    JSR     $A478                   ; keyboard/timing check (EALDR resident)
    BCS     .exit                   ; carry set = user pressed key

    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{DISPLAY_STATUS_BAR}{PYNWmai0-CAQTAAOHJTMFOSJ452F3J7I5JQ000000-1}
    LDA     #<$5C00                 ; \\
    STA     $06                     ;  | $06/$07 = $5C00 (scene text data)
    LDA     #>$5C00                 ;  |
    STA     $07                     ; /
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{TEXT_RENDERER}{PYNWmai0-4PQFNHIY4HEZD756HZHHCIBVCA000000-1}

    LDX     #$06                    ; script index 6
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_ENGINE}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-6}           ; run script #3 ($A300)
    LDA     $5CFF                   ; scene transition flag
    BEQ     .done                   ; zero = no transition
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{SCENE_NUMBER}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-10}            ; set new scene number
    JMP     .display                ; continue

.exit:
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SET_TEXT_WINDOW_BOTTOM}{PYNWmai0-UOBA5Y3PKYLQKGPLIBUCA3M2SE000000-1}
    LDA     #$1B
    JSR     $761E                   ; sound/mode off
                                    ; fall through to .done

.done:
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SET_TEXT_WINDOW_BOTTOM}{PYNWmai0-UOBA5Y3PKYLQKGPLIBUCA3M2SE000000-1}
    LDA     #$00                    ; \\
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{LOCATION_FLAG}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-10}           ;  | clear location flags
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{LOCATION_FLAG2}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-10}          ; /
    JSR     $72A7                   ; update display
    JMP     \nwlinkedidentc{RESTORE_ZP_POINTERS}{PYNWmai0-34VA5T5PRGU2LZRT6RKWJJ2FQI000000-1}     ; restore and return
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{SCENE{\_}LOOP}}{SCENE:unLOOP}{PYNWmai0-5E23YPEUUG4SZHWM2ZQ6MSHERE000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{SCENE{\_}LOOP}}{SCENE:unLOOP}}}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{BLINK{\_}COL}}{BLINK:unCOL}}\\{{\nwixident{DISPLAY{\_}STATUS{\_}BAR}}{DISPLAY:unSTATUS:unBAR}}\\{{\nwixident{LOAD{\_}SCENE{\_}DATA}}{LOAD:unSCENE:unDATA}}\\{{\nwixident{LOCATION{\_}FLAG}}{LOCATION:unFLAG}}\\{{\nwixident{LOCATION{\_}FLAG2}}{LOCATION:unFLAG2}}\\{{\nwixident{PRNG{\_}OUTPUT}}{PRNG:unOUTPUT}}\\{{\nwixident{RESTORE{\_}ZP{\_}POINTERS}}{RESTORE:unZP:unPOINTERS}}\\{{\nwixident{SAVE{\_}ZP{\_}POINTERS}}{SAVE:unZP:unPOINTERS}}\\{{\nwixident{SCENE{\_}NUMBER}}{SCENE:unNUMBER}}\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}ENGINE}}{SCRIPT:unENGINE}}\\{{\nwixident{SET{\_}TEXT{\_}WINDOW{\_}BOTTOM}}{SET:unTEXT:unWINDOW:unBOTTOM}}\\{{\nwixident{STEP{\_}PRNG}}{STEP:unPRNG}}\\{{\nwixident{TEXT{\_}RENDERER}}{TEXT:unRENDERER}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{BLINK{\_}COL}}{BLINK:unCOL}{PYNWmai0-5E23YPEUUG4SZHWM2ZQ6MSHERE000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{DISPLAY{\_}STATUS{\_}BAR}}{DISPLAY:unSTATUS:unBAR}{PYNWmai0-5E23YPEUUG4SZHWM2ZQ6MSHERE000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{LOAD{\_}SCENE{\_}DATA}}{LOAD:unSCENE:unDATA}{PYNWmai0-5E23YPEUUG4SZHWM2ZQ6MSHERE000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{LOCATION{\_}FLAG}}{LOCATION:unFLAG}{PYNWmai0-5E23YPEUUG4SZHWM2ZQ6MSHERE000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{LOCATION{\_}FLAG2}}{LOCATION:unFLAG2}{PYNWmai0-5E23YPEUUG4SZHWM2ZQ6MSHERE000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{PRNG{\_}OUTPUT}}{PRNG:unOUTPUT}{PYNWmai0-5E23YPEUUG4SZHWM2ZQ6MSHERE000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{RESTORE{\_}ZP{\_}POINTERS}}{RESTORE:unZP:unPOINTERS}{PYNWmai0-5E23YPEUUG4SZHWM2ZQ6MSHERE000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SAVE{\_}ZP{\_}POINTERS}}{SAVE:unZP:unPOINTERS}{PYNWmai0-5E23YPEUUG4SZHWM2ZQ6MSHERE000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SCENE{\_}NUMBER}}{SCENE:unNUMBER}{PYNWmai0-5E23YPEUUG4SZHWM2ZQ6MSHERE000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}ENGINE}}{SCRIPT:unENGINE}{PYNWmai0-5E23YPEUUG4SZHWM2ZQ6MSHERE000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SET{\_}TEXT{\_}WINDOW{\_}BOTTOM}}{SET:unTEXT:unWINDOW:unBOTTOM}{PYNWmai0-5E23YPEUUG4SZHWM2ZQ6MSHERE000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{STEP{\_}PRNG}}{STEP:unPRNG}{PYNWmai0-5E23YPEUUG4SZHWM2ZQ6MSHERE000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{TEXT{\_}RENDERER}}{TEXT:unRENDERER}{PYNWmai0-5E23YPEUUG4SZHWM2ZQ6MSHERE000000-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{199}\nwdocspar

The scene loop calls {\Tt{}{\$}A478\nwendquote} (a resident routine from EALDR, still in
memory at {\Tt{}{\$}A000\nwendquote}--{\Tt{}{\$}BFFF\nwendquote}) each iteration to check for user input.
If carry is set (key pressed), the loop exits.  Otherwise, it displays
the status bar, renders the scene text from {\Tt{}{\$}5C00\nwendquote}, runs script \#3
(the attract animation at {\Tt{}{\$}A300\nwendquote}), and checks {\Tt{}{\$}5CFF\nwendquote} for a scene
transition.

The {\Tt{}{\$}5C00\nwendquote} region is populated dynamically by {\Tt{}LOAD{\textbackslash}{\_}SCENE{\textbackslash}{\_}DATA\nwendquote}
from disk.  Its contents change with each scene.

\section{Utility routines}

\subsection{save\_zp\_pointers / restore\_zp\_pointers}

These routines save and restore four zero-page pointer pairs to/from
fixed addresses in the {\Tt{}{\$}5A00\nwendquote} page.  The pointers are used throughout
the game for character records, text buffers, and cursor state.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{200}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-13}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-13}}}\moddef{defines~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-1}}}\plusendmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwprevnextdefs{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-12}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-14}\nwenddeflinemarkup
\nwlinkedidentc{SAVED_BC}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-13}            EQU     $5A9A   ; saved $BC/$BD pointer (2 bytes)
\nwlinkedidentc{SAVED_F8}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-13}            EQU     $5A9C   ; saved $F8/$F9 pointer (2 bytes)
\nwlinkedidentc{SAVED_BE}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-13}            EQU     $5A9E   ; saved $BE/$BF pointer (2 bytes)
\nwlinkedidentc{SAVED_F4}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-13}            EQU     $5AA0   ; saved $F4/$F5 pointer (2 bytes)
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{SAVED{\_}BC}}{SAVED:unBC}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-13}\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{SAVED{\_}BE}}{SAVED:unBE}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-13}\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{SAVED{\_}F4}}{SAVED:unF4}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-13}\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{SAVED{\_}F8}}{SAVED:unF8}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-13}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{SAVED{\_}BC}}{SAVED:unBC}}\\{{\nwixident{SAVED{\_}BE}}{SAVED:unBE}}\\{{\nwixident{SAVED{\_}F4}}{SAVED:unF4}}\\{{\nwixident{SAVED{\_}F8}}{SAVED:unF8}}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{201}\nwdocspar

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{202}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-XTFMNQODSGOW3IGUAVI6HJU56I000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-XTFMNQODSGOW3IGUAVI6HJU56I000000-1}}}\moddef{save zp pointers~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-XTFMNQODSGOW3IGUAVI6HJU56I000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $6D53
\nwlinkedidentc{SAVE_ZP_POINTERS}{PYNWmai0-XTFMNQODSGOW3IGUAVI6HJU56I000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    LDA     $BC
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{SAVED_BC}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-13}
    LDA     $BD
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{SAVED_BC}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-13}+1
    LDA     $F8
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{SAVED_F8}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-13}
    LDA     $F9
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{SAVED_F8}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-13}+1
    LDA     $BE
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{SAVED_BE}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-13}
    LDA     $BF
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{SAVED_BE}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-13}+1
    LDA     $F4
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{SAVED_F4}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-13}
    LDA     $F5
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{SAVED_F4}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-13}+1
    RTS
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{SAVE{\_}ZP{\_}POINTERS}}{SAVE:unZP:unPOINTERS}{PYNWmai0-XTFMNQODSGOW3IGUAVI6HJU56I000000-1}\eatline

\subsection{relocate\_hires\_staging (\$6DA5)}

During startup, tracks {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}0F\nwendquote} and {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}10\nwendquote} are loaded into the hi-res
page area {\Tt{}{\$}2000--{\$}3FFF\nwendquote} as a staging area.  This routine, called from
{\Tt{}game{\textbackslash}{\_}init\nwendquote}, copies the staged data to its runtime addresses and clears
the hi-res page:

\begin{center}
\begin{tabular}{ccl}
\toprule
\thead{Source} & \thead{Destination} & \thead{Size} \\
\midrule
\$2000--\$32FF & \$9600--\$A8FF & 19 pages (HRCG code + standard font) \\
\$3300--\$3FFF & \$B300--\$BFFF & 13 pages (disk I/O routines) \\
\bottomrule
\end{tabular}
\end{center}

The copy loop at {\Tt{}.copy\nwendquote} also clears each source byte, leaving the
hi-res page zeroed for use as a graphics buffer.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{207}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-2NL3TPDIV6BH32KNILRIC2G5ZE000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-2NL3TPDIV6BH32KNILRIC2G5ZE000000-1}}}\moddef{relocate hires staging~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-2NL3TPDIV6BH32KNILRIC2G5ZE000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $6DA5
\nwlinkedidentc{RELOCATE_HIRES_STAGING}{PYNWmai0-2NL3TPDIV6BH32KNILRIC2G5ZE000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    LDA     #$00
    STA     $BA                         ; \\  dest = $9600
    STA     $BC                         ; \\  src  = $2000
    LDA     #$20                        ;  |
    STA     $BD                         ; /  src hi
    LDA     #$96                        ;  |
    STA     $BB                         ; /  dest hi
    LDY     #$00
    LDX     #$13                        ; 19 pages: $2000-$32FF -> $9600-$A8FF
    JSR     .copy
    LDX     #$0D                        ; 13 pages: $3300-$3FFF -> $B300-$BFFF
    LDA     #$B3
    STA     $BB                         ; dest hi = $B3
    INC     $BD                         ; src hi = $33 (was $32 after first pass)

.copy:
    LDA     ($BC),Y                     ; load from source
    STA     ($BA),Y                     ; store to dest
    LDA     #$00
    STA     ($BC),Y                     ; clear source byte
    DEY
    BNE     .copy                       ; inner loop (256 bytes)
    DEX
    BNE     .next_page                  ; more pages?
    RTS

.next_page:
    INC     $BD                         ; next source page
    INC     $BB                         ; next dest page
    JMP     .copy
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{RELOCATE{\_}HIRES{\_}STAGING}}{RELOCATE:unHIRES:unSTAGING}{PYNWmai0-2NL3TPDIV6BH32KNILRIC2G5ZE000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{RELOCATE{\_}HIRES{\_}STAGING}}{RELOCATE:unHIRES:unSTAGING}}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{208}\nwdocspar

\subsection{step\_prng (\$78A8)}

The pseudo-random number generator computes:
$$\texttt{val}_{n+1} = 69 \cdot \texttt{val}_n + \$53 \pmod{256}$$
and stores both the full result and a shifted copy.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{209}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-3OGDZ4EYEYE7YXQHNEV2CZPRBM000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-3OGDZ4EYEYE7YXQHNEV2CZPRBM000000-1}}}\moddef{step prng~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-3OGDZ4EYEYE7YXQHNEV2CZPRBM000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $78A8
\nwlinkedidentc{STEP_PRNG}{PYNWmai0-3OGDZ4EYEYE7YXQHNEV2CZPRBM000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{PRNG_STATE}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-9}              ; val
    ASL     A                       ; val*2
    ASL     A                       ; val*4
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{PRNG_TEMP}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-9}               ; temp = val*4
    ASL     A                       ; val*8
    ASL     A                       ; val*16
    ASL     A                       ; val*32
    ASL     A                       ; val*64
    CLC
    ADC     \nwlinkedidentc{PRNG_TEMP}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-9}               ; val*64 + val*4 = val*68
    CLC
    ADC     \nwlinkedidentc{PRNG_STATE}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-9}              ; val*68 + val = val*69
    CLC
    ADC     #$53                    ; + $53
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{PRNG_STATE}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-9}              ; store full result
    LSR                             ; val >> 1
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{PRNG_OUTPUT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-9}             ; shifted copy (used for random tests)
    RTS
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{STEP{\_}PRNG}}{STEP:unPRNG}{PYNWmai0-3OGDZ4EYEYE7YXQHNEV2CZPRBM000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{STEP{\_}PRNG}}{STEP:unPRNG}}}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{PRNG{\_}OUTPUT}}{PRNG:unOUTPUT}}\\{{\nwixident{PRNG{\_}STATE}}{PRNG:unSTATE}}\\{{\nwixident{PRNG{\_}TEMP}}{PRNG:unTEMP}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{PRNG{\_}OUTPUT}}{PRNG:unOUTPUT}{PYNWmai0-3OGDZ4EYEYE7YXQHNEV2CZPRBM000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{PRNG{\_}STATE}}{PRNG:unSTATE}{PYNWmai0-3OGDZ4EYEYE7YXQHNEV2CZPRBM000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{PRNG{\_}TEMP}}{PRNG:unTEMP}{PYNWmai0-3OGDZ4EYEYE7YXQHNEV2CZPRBM000000-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{210}\nwdocspar

Two shifts produce {\Tt{}val*4\nwendquote}, saved to {\Tt{}PRNG{\textbackslash}{\_}TEMP\nwendquote}.  Four more shifts give
{\Tt{}val*64\nwendquote}.  Adding {\Tt{}val*4\nwendquote} gives {\Tt{}val*68\nwendquote}, then adding {\Tt{}val\nwendquote} gives
{\Tt{}val*69\nwendquote}.  Adding {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}53\nwendquote} completes the LCG step.  This is a linear
congruential generator with multiplier 69, increment \$53, and modulus 256.

\subsection{random\_in\_range (\$1317)}

Returns a uniform random integer in {\Tt{}0..A{\$}-{\$}1\nwendquote} using rejection sampling.
The routine finds the smallest bitmask that covers the range, then repeatedly
calls {\Tt{}STEP{\textbackslash}{\_}PRNG\nwendquote} and masks {\Tt{}PRNG{\textbackslash}{\_}OUTPUT\nwendquote} until the result is less than
or equal to the shifted limit.  This avoids modulo bias.

Input: A~=~range limit (1--127).  If A~=~0, returns~0 immediately.
Output: A~=~random value in {\Tt{}0..limit{\$}-{\$}1\nwendquote}.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{211}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-14}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-14}}}\moddef{defines~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-1}}}\plusendmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwprevnextdefs{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-13}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-15}\nwenddeflinemarkup
\nwlinkedidentc{RNG_LIMIT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-14}           EQU     $5A11   ; random\\_in\\_range temporary (limit/shift count)
\nwlinkedidentc{RNG_MASK}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-14}            EQU     $5A12   ; random\\_in\\_range bit mask
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{RNG{\_}LIMIT}}{RNG:unLIMIT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-14}\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{RNG{\_}MASK}}{RNG:unMASK}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-14}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{RNG{\_}LIMIT}}{RNG:unLIMIT}}\\{{\nwixident{RNG{\_}MASK}}{RNG:unMASK}}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{212}\nwdocspar

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{213}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-F6322QSFMTRJBO2IS2F3GEYRZU000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-F6322QSFMTRJBO2IS2F3GEYRZU000000-1}}}\moddef{random in range~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-F6322QSFMTRJBO2IS2F3GEYRZU000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $1317
\nwlinkedidentc{RANDOM_IN_RANGE}{PYNWmai0-F6322QSFMTRJBO2IS2F3GEYRZU000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{RNG_LIMIT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-14}               ; save range limit
    CMP     #$00
    BNE     .nonzero
    RTS                             ; range=0 → return 0

.nonzero:
    CMP     #$02                    ; \\
    BPL     .ge2                    ;  |
    LDY     #$06                    ;  | range 1: mask=$40, shift=6
    LDA     #$40                    ;  |
    BNE     .have_mask              ; /
.ge2:
    CMP     #$04                    ; \\
    BPL     .ge4                    ;  |
    LDY     #$05                    ;  | range 2-3: mask=$60, shift=5
    LDA     #$60                    ;  |
    BNE     .have_mask              ; /
.ge4:
    CMP     #$08                    ; \\
    BPL     .ge8                    ;  |
    LDY     #$04                    ;  | range 4-7: mask=$70, shift=4
    LDA     #$70                    ;  |
    BNE     .have_mask              ; /
.ge8:
    CMP     #$10                    ; \\
    BPL     .ge16                   ;  |
    LDY     #$03                    ;  | range 8-15: mask=$78, shift=3
    LDA     #$78                    ;  |
    BNE     .have_mask              ; /
.ge16:
    CMP     #$20                    ; \\
    BPL     .ge32                   ;  |
    LDY     #$02                    ;  | range 16-31: mask=$7C, shift=2
    LDA     #$7C                    ;  |
    BNE     .have_mask              ; /
.ge32:
    CMP     #$40                    ; \\
    BPL     .ge64                   ;  |
    LDY     #$01                    ;  | range 32-63: mask=$7E, shift=1
    LDA     #$7E                    ;  |
    BNE     .have_mask              ; /
.ge64:
    LDY     #$00                    ; range 64-127: mask=$7F, shift=0
    LDA     #$7F

.have_mask:
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{RNG_MASK}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-14}                ; save bit mask
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{RNG_LIMIT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-14}               ; reload range limit
    STY     \nwlinkedidentc{RNG_LIMIT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-14}               ; save shift count in \nwlinkedidentc{RNG_LIMIT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-14}
.shift_loop:
    DEY                             ; \\
    BMI     .shifted                ;  | shift limit left by (shift count)
    CLC                             ;  | positions so it aligns with the
    ROL     A                       ;  | mask bits
    BNE     .shift_loop             ; /
.shifted:
    LDY     \nwlinkedidentc{RNG_LIMIT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-14}               ; Y = shift count
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{RNG_LIMIT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-14}               ; save shifted limit

.sample:
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{STEP_PRNG}{PYNWmai0-3OGDZ4EYEYE7YXQHNEV2CZPRBM000000-1}               ; get next random byte
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{PRNG_OUTPUT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-9}
    AND     \nwlinkedidentc{RNG_MASK}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-14}                ; mask to relevant bits
    CMP     \nwlinkedidentc{RNG_LIMIT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-14}               ; compare with shifted limit
    BEQ     .accept                 ; equal → accept
    BPL     .sample                 ; greater → reject, retry

.accept:
    DEY                             ; \\
    BPL     .shift_right            ;  | shift result right by (shift count)
    RTS                             ;  | to recover the final value
.shift_right:
    CLC                             ;  |
    ROR     A                       ;  |
    BCC     .accept                 ; / (always taken: masked bit is 0)
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{RANDOM{\_}IN{\_}RANGE}}{RANDOM:unIN:unRANGE}{PYNWmai0-F6322QSFMTRJBO2IS2F3GEYRZU000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{RANDOM{\_}IN{\_}RANGE}}{RANDOM:unIN:unRANGE}}}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{PRNG{\_}OUTPUT}}{PRNG:unOUTPUT}}\\{{\nwixident{RNG{\_}LIMIT}}{RNG:unLIMIT}}\\{{\nwixident{RNG{\_}MASK}}{RNG:unMASK}}\\{{\nwixident{STEP{\_}PRNG}}{STEP:unPRNG}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{PRNG{\_}OUTPUT}}{PRNG:unOUTPUT}{PYNWmai0-F6322QSFMTRJBO2IS2F3GEYRZU000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{RNG{\_}LIMIT}}{RNG:unLIMIT}{PYNWmai0-F6322QSFMTRJBO2IS2F3GEYRZU000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{RNG{\_}MASK}}{RNG:unMASK}{PYNWmai0-F6322QSFMTRJBO2IS2F3GEYRZU000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{STEP{\_}PRNG}}{STEP:unPRNG}{PYNWmai0-F6322QSFMTRJBO2IS2F3GEYRZU000000-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{214}\nwdocspar

\subsection{first/next\_group\_member (\$12FA/\$1300)}

Group iteration uses two zero-page pointer pairs: {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}FA/{\textbackslash}{\$}FB\nwendquote} points
to the group head (or the member currently being processed), and
{\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}F4/{\textbackslash}{\$}F5\nwendquote} is the iteration cursor that advances through the chain.
Both routines follow the ``next'' link in byte~2 of a mob data record,
resolve it via {\Tt{}GET{\textbackslash}{\_}MOB{\textbackslash}{\_}DATA\nwendquote}, and store the result in~{\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}F4/{\textbackslash}{\$}F5\nwendquote}.
If the link is zero (end of chain), {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}F4/{\textbackslash}{\$}F5\nwendquote} is set to null.

\begin{itemize}
\item {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}12FA\nwendquote} ({\Tt{}FIRST{\textbackslash}{\_}GROUP{\textbackslash}{\_}MEMBER\nwendquote}): begins iteration by following
      byte~2 of the group head at~{\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}FA/{\textbackslash}{\$}FB\nwendquote}.  If that link is zero,
      falls through to check {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}F4/{\textbackslash}{\$}F5\nwendquote} as a fallback.
\item {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}1300\nwendquote} ({\Tt{}NEXT{\textbackslash}{\_}GROUP{\textbackslash}{\_}MEMBER\nwendquote}): continues iteration by following
      byte~2 of the current cursor at~{\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}F4/{\textbackslash}{\$}F5\nwendquote}.
\end{itemize}

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{215}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-N5WF7CLBP626OQIPH6GSP4CDCA000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-N5WF7CLBP626OQIPH6GSP4CDCA000000-1}}}\moddef{advance group link~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-N5WF7CLBP626OQIPH6GSP4CDCA000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $12FA
\nwlinkedidentc{FIRST_GROUP_MEMBER}{PYNWmai0-N5WF7CLBP626OQIPH6GSP4CDCA000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    LDY     #$02                    ; \\
    LDA     ($FA),Y                 ;  | check byte 2 of group head ($FA)
    BNE     .resolve                ; /  if nonzero, follow it
\nwlinkedidentc{NEXT_GROUP_MEMBER}{PYNWmai0-N5WF7CLBP626OQIPH6GSP4CDCA000000-1}:
    LDY     #$02                    ; \\
    LDA     ($F4),Y                 ;  | check byte 2 of cursor ($F4)
    BNE     .resolve                ; /  if nonzero, follow it
    STA     $F4                     ; \\  end of chain:
    STA     $F5                     ; /  null out $F4/$F5
    RTS
.resolve:
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{GET_MOB_DATA}{PYNWmai0-VTKXUQPSOCRIDYWOEIFECHPTSM000000-1}            ; resolve link -> $BA/$BB
    LDA     $BA                     ; \\
    STA     $F4                     ;  | $F4/$F5 = $BA/$BB
    LDA     $BB                     ;  | (advance cursor to next record)
    STA     $F5                     ; /
    RTS
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{FIRST{\_}GROUP{\_}MEMBER}}{FIRST:unGROUP:unMEMBER}{PYNWmai0-N5WF7CLBP626OQIPH6GSP4CDCA000000-1}\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{NEXT{\_}GROUP{\_}MEMBER}}{NEXT:unGROUP:unMEMBER}{PYNWmai0-N5WF7CLBP626OQIPH6GSP4CDCA000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{FIRST{\_}GROUP{\_}MEMBER}}{FIRST:unGROUP:unMEMBER}}\\{{\nwixident{NEXT{\_}GROUP{\_}MEMBER}}{NEXT:unGROUP:unMEMBER}}}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{GET{\_}MOB{\_}DATA}}{GET:unMOB:unDATA}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{GET{\_}MOB{\_}DATA}}{GET:unMOB:unDATA}{PYNWmai0-N5WF7CLBP626OQIPH6GSP4CDCA000000-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{216}\nwdocspar

\subsection{clamp\_char\_field (\$0A93)}

Ensures that byte~6 of the character record at {\Tt{}{\$}F4\nwendquote} has its lower 6~bits
at least as large as byte~5's lower 5~bits.  If byte~6 is smaller, its low
bits are replaced with byte~5's value (preserving byte~6's top 2~bits).
This clamps a stat floor---likely ensuring current HP does not fall below
a minimum derived from another field.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{217}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-VZAAE44D7YBBIC7MO6FZNDLI6M000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-VZAAE44D7YBBIC7MO6FZNDLI6M000000-1}}}\moddef{clamp char field~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-VZAAE44D7YBBIC7MO6FZNDLI6M000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $0A93
\nwlinkedidentc{CLAMP_CHAR_FIELD}{PYNWmai0-VZAAE44D7YBBIC7MO6FZNDLI6M000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    LDY     #$05
    LDA     ($F4),Y                 ; byte 5 of record
    AND     #$1F                    ; low 5 bits = minimum
    STA     $BA
    INY
    LDA     ($F4),Y                 ; byte 6 of record
    AND     #$3F                    ; low 6 bits = current value
    CMP     $BA
    BCC     .clamp                  ; current < minimum → clamp
    RTS                             ; current >= minimum → done
.clamp:
    LDA     ($F4),Y                 ; reload byte 6
    AND     #$C0                    ; preserve top 2 bits
    ORA     $BA                     ; set low bits to minimum
    STA     ($F4),Y
    RTS
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{CLAMP{\_}CHAR{\_}FIELD}}{CLAMP:unCHAR:unFIELD}{PYNWmai0-VZAAE44D7YBBIC7MO6FZNDLI6M000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{CLAMP{\_}CHAR{\_}FIELD}}{CLAMP:unCHAR:unFIELD}}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{218}\nwdocspar

\subsection{draw\_char\_at\_pos (\$1156)}

Given a map position in~A, sets the font cursor to the corresponding
column and row, looks up what character or mob occupies that position,
determines its font character, and draws it.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{219}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-RAACK23HC5EFMXFBXXME6ZKJTE000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-RAACK23HC5EFMXFBXXME6ZKJTE000000-1}}}\moddef{draw char at pos~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-RAACK23HC5EFMXFBXXME6ZKJTE000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $1156
\nwlinkedidentc{DRAW_CHAR_AT_POS}{PYNWmai0-RAACK23HC5EFMXFBXXME6ZKJTE000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{POS_TO_COLROW}{PYNWmai0-AMTAHZ55D6ORMSENT2EMDCDU24000000-1}           ; A=pos → A=col, Y=row
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{FONT_COL}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-3}                ; set font column
    STY     \nwlinkedidentc{FONT_ROW}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-3}                ; set font row
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{COLROW_TO_POS}{PYNWmai0-YXZOC7KQXOV5OPKZ6P7KWNTLUM000000-1}           ; re-linearize (A = col + row*20)
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{FIND_ENTITY_AT_POS}{PYNWmai0-PLJFN4SECKS5ALV334RXDZNCVU000000-1}      ; look up entity at position → $BE
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{GET_ENTITY_FONTCHAR}{PYNWmai0-KWRR7HOSUHEUTDUYCEFKKXY7QE000000-1}     ; determine font char from entity data
    JMP     \nwlinkedidentc{RENDER_FONT_CHAR}{PYNWmai0-X3D3646XM7VEHJGRKDML2UKINQ000000-1}        ; render the font character
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{DRAW{\_}CHAR{\_}AT{\_}POS}}{DRAW:unCHAR:unAT:unPOS}{PYNWmai0-RAACK23HC5EFMXFBXXME6ZKJTE000000-1}\eatline

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{221}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-CAQTAAOHJTMFOSJ452F3J7I5JQ000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-CAQTAAOHJTMFOSJ452F3J7I5JQ000000-1}}}\moddef{display status bar~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-CAQTAAOHJTMFOSJ452F3J7I5JQ000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup

\subsection{print\_from\_ptr (\$775C)}

Prints a length-prefixed string from {\Tt{}{\$}BC/{\$}BD\nwendquote} via COUT:

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{223}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-XAPVU72S6LIKQGYUGORXPGRLK4000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-XAPVU72S6LIKQGYUGORXPGRLK4000000-1}}}\moddef{print from ptr~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-XAPVU72S6LIKQGYUGORXPGRLK4000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
