\section{Resident bytecode interpreter (\$0500--\$07FF)}
\label{sec:resident_interp}

EALDR copies 768 bytes from {\Tt{}{\$}A300\nwendquote}--{\Tt{}{\$}A5FF\nwendquote} to {\Tt{}{\$}0500\nwendquote}--{\Tt{}{\$}07FF\nwendquote}
before entering the main program.  This region contains a second bytecode
interpreter, separate from the EALDR VM, that runs during gameplay and
the attract screen.  It uses the same XOR encryption scheme as the EALDR
VM (low byte XOR {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}03\nwendquote}, high byte XOR {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}D9\nwendquote}).

\subsection{attract\_loop (\$0569)}

The entry point for the resident interpreter.  Each iteration swaps
context (zero-page state) and dispatches one bytecode instruction.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{292}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-Y3PF34ZZHWG7GMSG7XZGBPWN5A000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-Y3PF34ZZHWG7GMSG7XZGBPWN5A000000-1}}}\moddef{attract loop~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-Y3PF34ZZHWG7GMSG7XZGBPWN5A000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $0569
\nwlinkedidentc{ATTRACT_LOOP}{PYNWmai0-Y3PF34ZZHWG7GMSG7XZGBPWN5A000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{CONTEXT_SWAP}{PYNWmai0-A5IY6LARV2ZVHGEJNTTVGGK3PU000000-1}
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{RESIDENT_DISPATCH}{PYNWmai0-2FARJ2CLNXYFYA6O756BE3RHTA000000-1}
    JMP     \nwlinkedidentc{ATTRACT_LOOP}{PYNWmai0-Y3PF34ZZHWG7GMSG7XZGBPWN5A000000-1}
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{ATTRACT{\_}LOOP}}{ATTRACT:unLOOP}{PYNWmai0-Y3PF34ZZHWG7GMSG7XZGBPWN5A000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{ATTRACT{\_}LOOP}}{ATTRACT:unLOOP}}}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{CONTEXT{\_}SWAP}}{CONTEXT:unSWAP}}\\{{\nwixident{RESIDENT{\_}DISPATCH}}{RESIDENT:unDISPATCH}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{CONTEXT{\_}SWAP}}{CONTEXT:unSWAP}{PYNWmai0-Y3PF34ZZHWG7GMSG7XZGBPWN5A000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{RESIDENT{\_}DISPATCH}}{RESIDENT:unDISPATCH}{PYNWmai0-Y3PF34ZZHWG7GMSG7XZGBPWN5A000000-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{293}\nwdocspar

\subsection{context\_swap (\$06E0)}

Swaps 16 bytes between zero page {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}50\nwendquote}--{\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}5F\nwendquote} and {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}07E5\nwendquote}--{\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}07F4\nwendquote}.
This gives the resident interpreter its own private set of zero-page
temporaries that don't interfere with the main program.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{294}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-A5IY6LARV2ZVHGEJNTTVGGK3PU000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-A5IY6LARV2ZVHGEJNTTVGGK3PU000000-1}}}\moddef{context swap~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-A5IY6LARV2ZVHGEJNTTVGGK3PU000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $06E0
\nwlinkedidentc{CONTEXT_SWAP}{PYNWmai0-A5IY6LARV2ZVHGEJNTTVGGK3PU000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    LDX     #$0F
.loop:
    LDA     $50,X                   ; load ZP byte
    PHA                             ; save on stack
    LDA     $7E5,X                  ; load shadow byte
    STA     $50,X                   ; → ZP
    PLA                             ; recover old ZP byte
    STA     $7E5,X                  ; → shadow
    DEX
    BPL     .loop
    RTS
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{CONTEXT{\_}SWAP}}{CONTEXT:unSWAP}{PYNWmai0-A5IY6LARV2ZVHGEJNTTVGGK3PU000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{CONTEXT{\_}SWAP}}{CONTEXT:unSWAP}}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{295}\nwdocspar

\subsection{resident\_dispatch (\$06B3)}

Dispatches one bytecode instruction using a stack trick.  X and Y hold
the bytecode pointer from the previous iteration.  They are pushed onto
the stack at entry, then {\Tt{}PULL{\textbackslash}{\_}TWO{\textbackslash}{\_}RET{\textbackslash}{\_}ADDRS\nwendquote} rearranges the stack
so the saved X/Y values end up in {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}52/{\$}53\nwendquote} as the new bytecode pointer.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{296}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-2FARJ2CLNXYFYA6O756BE3RHTA000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-2FARJ2CLNXYFYA6O756BE3RHTA000000-1}}}\moddef{resident dispatch~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-2FARJ2CLNXYFYA6O756BE3RHTA000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $06B3
\nwlinkedidentc{RESIDENT_DISPATCH}{PYNWmai0-2FARJ2CLNXYFYA6O756BE3RHTA000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    TXA                             ; \\
    PHA                             ;  | save X, Y on stack
    TYA                             ;  | (these ARE the bytecode pointer)
    PHA                             ; /
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{PULL_TWO_RET_ADDRS}{PYNWmai0-ZQ3HACWSYBTTFFJTEM5GLS64PU000000-1}      ; rearrange stack, jump to .resume

    ; Control returns here via JMP ($54):
.resume:
    PLA                             ; \\  recover saved Y
    STA     $52                     ;  | $52/$53 = bytecode pointer
    PLA                             ;  | recover saved X
    STA     $53                     ; /

    LDY     #$04                    ; skip 4 bytes
.fetch:
    LDA     ($52),Y                 ; read opcode
    INY
    BNE     .no_carry
    INC     $53
.no_carry:
    TAX                             ; opcode → X (also saves position)
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{RESIDENT_DISPATCH_TABLE}{PYNWmai0-LZD7UO27WADGX7M4TS77RNCD74000000-1},X
    STA     resident_jmp+1          ; self-modify: JMP low byte
resident_jmp:
    JMP     \nwlinkedidentc{RESIDENT_DECODE_DISPATCH}{PYNWmai0-BGQWA2JRONNKYOAYDUITG47DXM000000-1} ; self-modified → $07xx
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{RESIDENT{\_}DISPATCH}}{RESIDENT:unDISPATCH}{PYNWmai0-2FARJ2CLNXYFYA6O756BE3RHTA000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{RESIDENT{\_}DISPATCH}}{RESIDENT:unDISPATCH}}}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{PULL{\_}TWO{\_}RET{\_}ADDRS}}{PULL:unTWO:unRET:unADDRS}}\\{{\nwixident{RESIDENT{\_}DECODE{\_}DISPATCH}}{RESIDENT:unDECODE:unDISPATCH}}\\{{\nwixident{RESIDENT{\_}DISPATCH{\_}TABLE}}{RESIDENT:unDISPATCH:unTABLE}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{PULL{\_}TWO{\_}RET{\_}ADDRS}}{PULL:unTWO:unRET:unADDRS}{PYNWmai0-2FARJ2CLNXYFYA6O756BE3RHTA000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{RESIDENT{\_}DECODE{\_}DISPATCH}}{RESIDENT:unDECODE:unDISPATCH}{PYNWmai0-2FARJ2CLNXYFYA6O756BE3RHTA000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{RESIDENT{\_}DISPATCH{\_}TABLE}}{RESIDENT:unDISPATCH:unTABLE}{PYNWmai0-2FARJ2CLNXYFYA6O756BE3RHTA000000-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{297}\nwdocspar
\nwenddocs{}\nwbegindocs{298}\nwdocspar

{\Tt{}PULL{\textbackslash}{\_}TWO{\textbackslash}{\_}RET{\textbackslash}{\_}ADDRS\nwendquote} pulls both return addresses from the stack
(its own and the caller's), increments each by 1 (since RTS pushes
addr\textminus{}1), and jumps through {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}54/{\$}55\nwendquote} back to the code
after the {\Tt{}JSR\nwendquote} in {\Tt{}RESIDENT{\textbackslash}{\_}DISPATCH\nwendquote}.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{299}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-ZQ3HACWSYBTTFFJTEM5GLS64PU000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-ZQ3HACWSYBTTFFJTEM5GLS64PU000000-1}}}\moddef{pull two ret addrs~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-ZQ3HACWSYBTTFFJTEM5GLS64PU000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $0738
\nwlinkedidentc{PULL_TWO_RET_ADDRS}{PYNWmai0-ZQ3HACWSYBTTFFJTEM5GLS64PU000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    PLA                             ; own return addr (low)
    STA     $54
    PLA                             ; own return addr (high)
    STA     $55
    PLA                             ; caller's return addr (low)
    STA     $52
    PLA                             ; caller's return addr (high)
    STA     $53
    INC     $52                     ; +1 (RTS pushed addr-1)
    INC     $54                     ; +1
    BNE     .done
    INC     $55                     ; carry
.done:
    JMP     ($54)                   ; jump back to .resume
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{PULL{\_}TWO{\_}RET{\_}ADDRS}}{PULL:unTWO:unRET:unADDRS}{PYNWmai0-ZQ3HACWSYBTTFFJTEM5GLS64PU000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{PULL{\_}TWO{\_}RET{\_}ADDRS}}{PULL:unTWO:unRET:unADDRS}}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{300}\nwdocspar

\subsection{Dispatch table (\$06D3)}

The 18-byte table maps opcode indices to handler addresses in page {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}07\nwendquote}:

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{301}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-LZD7UO27WADGX7M4TS77RNCD74000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-LZD7UO27WADGX7M4TS77RNCD74000000-1}}}\moddef{resident dispatch table~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-LZD7UO27WADGX7M4TS77RNCD74000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $06D3
\nwlinkedidentc{RESIDENT_DISPATCH_TABLE}{PYNWmai0-LZD7UO27WADGX7M4TS77RNCD74000000-1}:
    HEX     00 27 55 5F 6D 8A AD B9
    HEX     4F A2 CE 26 79 A2 0F B5
    HEX     50 48
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{RESIDENT{\_}DISPATCH{\_}TABLE}}{RESIDENT:unDISPATCH:unTABLE}{PYNWmai0-LZD7UO27WADGX7M4TS77RNCD74000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{RESIDENT{\_}DISPATCH{\_}TABLE}}{RESIDENT:unDISPATCH:unTABLE}}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{302}\nwdocspar
\nwenddocs{}\nwbegindocs{303}\nwdocspar

\begin{center}
\begin{tabular}{ccl}

\midrule

Opcodes \$09 and \$0D share the same handler (\$07A2).

\subsection{decode\_encrypted\_addr (\$0710)}

Decodes a 2-byte encrypted address from the bytecode stream.
Uses the same XOR scheme as the EALDR VM.  The decoded address is
left in {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}54/{\$}55\nwendquote}.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{304}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-QPGMZCBHONP3ALTVEWGVE7O2I4000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-QPGMZCBHONP3ALTVEWGVE7O2I4000000-1}}}\moddef{decode encrypted addr~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-QPGMZCBHONP3ALTVEWGVE7O2I4000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $0710
\nwlinkedidentc{DECODE_ENCRYPTED_ADDR}{PYNWmai0-QPGMZCBHONP3ALTVEWGVE7O2I4000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    LDA     ($52),Y                 ; read low byte
    EOR     #$03                    ; decrypt
    INY
    BNE     .no_carry1
    INC     $53
.no_carry1:
    STA     $54                     ; decoded low
    LDA     ($52),Y                 ; read high byte
    INY
    BNE     .no_carry2
    INC     $53
.no_carry2:
    EOR     #$D9                    ; decrypt
    STA     $55                     ; decoded high
    RTS
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{DECODE{\_}ENCRYPTED{\_}ADDR}}{DECODE:unENCRYPTED:unADDR}{PYNWmai0-QPGMZCBHONP3ALTVEWGVE7O2I4000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{DECODE{\_}ENCRYPTED{\_}ADDR}}{DECODE:unENCRYPTED:unADDR}}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{305}\nwdocspar

\subsection{resident\_decode\_dispatch (\$0700)}

Opcode \$00 handler---the resident interpreter's GOTO instruction.
Decodes an address and redirects execution there.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{306}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-BGQWA2JRONNKYOAYDUITG47DXM000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-BGQWA2JRONNKYOAYDUITG47DXM000000-1}}}\moddef{resident decode dispatch~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-BGQWA2JRONNKYOAYDUITG47DXM000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $0700
\nwlinkedidentc{RESIDENT_DECODE_DISPATCH}{PYNWmai0-BGQWA2JRONNKYOAYDUITG47DXM000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{DECODE_ENCRYPTED_ADDR}{PYNWmai0-QPGMZCBHONP3ALTVEWGVE7O2I4000000-1}   ; → $54/$55
    LDA     $54                     ; \\
    STA     $52                     ;  | $52/$53 = decoded address
    LDA     $55                     ;  |
    STA     $53                     ; /
    LDY     #$00
    JMP     \nwlinkedidentc{RESIDENT_DISPATCH}{PYNWmai0-2FARJ2CLNXYFYA6O756BE3RHTA000000-1}.fetch ; fetch from new location
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{RESIDENT{\_}DECODE{\_}DISPATCH}}{RESIDENT:unDECODE:unDISPATCH}{PYNWmai0-BGQWA2JRONNKYOAYDUITG47DXM000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{RESIDENT{\_}DECODE{\_}DISPATCH}}{RESIDENT:unDECODE:unDISPATCH}}}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{DECODE{\_}ENCRYPTED{\_}ADDR}}{DECODE:unENCRYPTED:unADDR}}\\{{\nwixident{RESIDENT{\_}DISPATCH}}{RESIDENT:unDISPATCH}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{DECODE{\_}ENCRYPTED{\_}ADDR}}{DECODE:unENCRYPTED:unADDR}{PYNWmai0-BGQWA2JRONNKYOAYDUITG47DXM000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{RESIDENT{\_}DISPATCH}}{RESIDENT:unDISPATCH}{PYNWmai0-BGQWA2JRONNKYOAYDUITG47DXM000000-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{307}\nwdocspar

\section{Script/event engine (\$795B)}
\label{sec:script_engine}

The script engine runs short bytecode programs that control animations,
sound, and game events.  It is called with a script index in X.

\subsection{Entry and setup}

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{308}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-1}}}\moddef{script engine~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwprevnextdefs{\relax}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-2}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $795B
\nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_ENGINE}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-6}:
    SUBROUTINE

    STA     $C010                   ; clear keyboard strobe
    LDA     #$00
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{ATTRACT_FLAG}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-10}            ; attract_flag = 0
    CPX     #$06                    ; script index 6 = attract
    BNE     .not_attract
    INC     \nwlinkedidentc{ATTRACT_FLAG}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-10}            ; attract_flag = 1
.not_attract:

    CPX     #$02                    ; special setup for index 2
    BEQ     .setup_2
    CPX     #$04                    ; special setup for index 4
    BEQ     .setup_4
    JMP     .load_ptr

.setup_2:
    DEY
    STY     $80D5
    JMP     .load_ptr
.setup_4:
    DEY
    STY     $80E3
\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{ATTRACT{\_}FLAG}}{ATTRACT:unFLAG}}\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}ENGINE}}{SCRIPT:unENGINE}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{ATTRACT{\_}FLAG}}{ATTRACT:unFLAG}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}ENGINE}}{SCRIPT:unENGINE}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{309}\nwdocspar

\subsection{Script pointer table}

The script base address is loaded from the table at {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}80AE\nwendquote}:

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{310}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-2}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-2}}}\moddef{script engine~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-1}}}\plusendmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwprevnextdefs{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-1}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-3}\nwenddeflinemarkup

.load_ptr:
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_TABLE}{PYNWmai0-33FGP2UXYD5EEQJUC5DEXEFVLE000000-1},X          ; low byte
    STA     $E4
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_TABLE}{PYNWmai0-33FGP2UXYD5EEQJUC5DEXEFVLE000000-1}+1,X        ; high byte
    STA     $E5                     ; $E4/$E5 = script start address
\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}TABLE}}{SCRIPT:unTABLE}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}TABLE}}{SCRIPT:unTABLE}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-2}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{311}\nwdocspar

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{312}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-33FGP2UXYD5EEQJUC5DEXEFVLE000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-33FGP2UXYD5EEQJUC5DEXEFVLE000000-1}}}\moddef{script pointer table~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-33FGP2UXYD5EEQJUC5DEXEFVLE000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $80AE
\nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_TABLE}{PYNWmai0-33FGP2UXYD5EEQJUC5DEXEFVLE000000-1}:
    DC.W    $80C6                   ; script 0
    DC.W    $80C7                   ; script 1
    DC.W    $80D7                   ; script 2
    DC.W    $A300                   ; script 3 (attract -- EALDR resident)
    DC.W    $A3C3                   ; script 4
    DC.W    $A3CE                   ; script 5
    DC.W    $A3DE                   ; script 6
    DC.W    $A409                   ; script 7
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}TABLE}}{SCRIPT:unTABLE}{PYNWmai0-33FGP2UXYD5EEQJUC5DEXEFVLE000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}TABLE}}{SCRIPT:unTABLE}}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{313}\nwdocspar
\nwenddocs{}\nwbegindocs{314}\nwdocspar

Scripts 3--7 are in the {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}A300\nwendquote}--{\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}A5FF\nwendquote} resident region (which was
also copied to {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}0500\nwendquote}--{\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}07FF\nwendquote} by EALDR, but the script table
points to the original addresses).

\subsection{Script interpreter}

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{315}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-24}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-24}}}\moddef{defines~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-1}}}\plusendmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwprevnextdefs{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-23}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}\nwenddeflinemarkup
\nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_LOOP_CTR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-24}     EQU     $5A8D   ; script loop iteration counter
\nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_LOOP_ADDR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-24}    EQU     $5A8E   ; script loop address (2 bytes)
\nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_GOSUB_ADDR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-24}   EQU     $5A90   ; script gosub return address (2 bytes)
\nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_PRNG_MASK}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-24}    EQU     $5A92   ; PRNG mask for action randomization
\nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_ACTION_VEC}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-24}   EQU     $5A93   ; action handler vector (2 bytes)
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}ACTION{\_}VEC}}{SCRIPT:unACTION:unVEC}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-24}\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}GOSUB{\_}ADDR}}{SCRIPT:unGOSUB:unADDR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-24}\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}LOOP{\_}ADDR}}{SCRIPT:unLOOP:unADDR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-24}\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}LOOP{\_}CTR}}{SCRIPT:unLOOP:unCTR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-24}\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}PRNG{\_}MASK}}{SCRIPT:unPRNG:unMASK}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-24}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}ACTION{\_}VEC}}{SCRIPT:unACTION:unVEC}}\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}GOSUB{\_}ADDR}}{SCRIPT:unGOSUB:unADDR}}\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}LOOP{\_}ADDR}}{SCRIPT:unLOOP:unADDR}}\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}LOOP{\_}CTR}}{SCRIPT:unLOOP:unCTR}}\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}PRNG{\_}MASK}}{SCRIPT:unPRNG:unMASK}}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{316}\nwdocspar

After setup, the interpreter initializes its loop counter and PRNG mask:

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{317}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-3}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-3}}}\moddef{script engine~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-1}}}\plusendmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwprevnextdefs{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-2}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-4}\nwenddeflinemarkup

    LDA     #$00
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_LOOP_CTR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-24}         ; loop counter = 0
    LDA     #$01
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_PRNG_MASK}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-24}        ; PRNG mask = 1
.fetch:
    LDY     #$00
    LDA     ($E4),Y                 ; read script byte
    CMP     #$27
    BCC     .control                ; < $27 → control command
    JMP     .action                 ; ≥ $27 → action dispatch
\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}LOOP{\_}CTR}}{SCRIPT:unLOOP:unCTR}}\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}PRNG{\_}MASK}}{SCRIPT:unPRNG:unMASK}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}LOOP{\_}CTR}}{SCRIPT:unLOOP:unCTR}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-3}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}PRNG{\_}MASK}}{SCRIPT:unPRNG:unMASK}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-3}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{318}\nwdocspar

\subsubsection{Control commands (< \$27)}

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{319}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-4}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-4}}}\moddef{script engine~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-1}}}\plusendmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwprevnextdefs{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-3}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-5}\nwenddeflinemarkup

.control:
    CMP     #$25
    BEQ     .cmd_25                 ; set PRNG mask = $0F
    BCS     .cmd_26                 ; $26: PRNG mask = $00

    CMP     #$23
    BEQ     .cmd_23                 ; set action vector → $7A7F
    BCS     .cmd_24                 ; set action vector → $7A91

    CMP     #$21
    BEQ     .cmd_21                 ; gosub
    BCS     .cmd_22                 ; nop (return)

    CMP     #$1F
    BEQ     .cmd_1F                 ; set loop address
    BCS     .cmd_20                 ; set gosub address

    ; --- Loop/end-loop (byte < $1F) ---
    CMP     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_LOOP_CTR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-24}         ; compare with loop counter
    BEQ     .end_loop
    BCC     .end_loop

    INC     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_LOOP_CTR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-24}         ; counter++
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_LOOP_ADDR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-24}        ; \\
    STA     $E4                     ;  | $E4/$E5 = loop address
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_LOOP_ADDR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-24}+1      ;  |
    STA     $E5                     ; /
    JMP     .fetch

.end_loop:
    LDA     #$00
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_LOOP_CTR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-24}         ; reset loop counter
    JMP     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_ADVANCE}{PYNWmai0-V3JA2NOBVSV23YOIWF45X5ET3A000000-1}
\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}ADVANCE}}{SCRIPT:unADVANCE}}\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}LOOP{\_}ADDR}}{SCRIPT:unLOOP:unADDR}}\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}LOOP{\_}CTR}}{SCRIPT:unLOOP:unCTR}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}ADVANCE}}{SCRIPT:unADVANCE}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-4}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}LOOP{\_}ADDR}}{SCRIPT:unLOOP:unADDR}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-4}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}LOOP{\_}CTR}}{SCRIPT:unLOOP:unCTR}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-4}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{320}\nwdocspar

When the byte value equals or exceeds the loop counter, the loop
terminates and the counter resets.  Otherwise, the counter increments
and execution jumps back to the saved loop address.

\subsubsection{Command implementations}

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{321}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-5}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-5}}}\moddef{script engine~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-1}}}\plusendmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwprevnextdefs{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-4}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-6}\nwenddeflinemarkup

.cmd_25:                            ; PRNG mask = $0F
    LDA     #$0F
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_PRNG_MASK}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-24}
    JMP     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_ADVANCE}{PYNWmai0-V3JA2NOBVSV23YOIWF45X5ET3A000000-1}

.cmd_26:                            ; PRNG mask = $00
    LDA     #$00
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_PRNG_MASK}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-24}
    JMP     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_ADVANCE}{PYNWmai0-V3JA2NOBVSV23YOIWF45X5ET3A000000-1}

.cmd_23:                            ; action vector → $7A7F
    \nwlinkedidentc{STOW}{PYNWmai0-UDRZI6QCMYPCHBPEW5VLDMJPJU000000-1}    $7A7F,\nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_ACTION_VEC}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-24}
    JMP     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_ADVANCE}{PYNWmai0-V3JA2NOBVSV23YOIWF45X5ET3A000000-1}

.cmd_24:                            ; action vector → $7A91
    \nwlinkedidentc{STOW}{PYNWmai0-UDRZI6QCMYPCHBPEW5VLDMJPJU000000-1}    $7A91,\nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_ACTION_VEC}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-24}
    JMP     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_ADVANCE}{PYNWmai0-V3JA2NOBVSV23YOIWF45X5ET3A000000-1}

.cmd_22:                            ; nop (return from script)
    RTS

.cmd_21:                            ; gosub: jump to saved address
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_GOSUB_ADDR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-24}
    STA     $E4
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_GOSUB_ADDR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-24}+1
    STA     $E5
    JMP     .fetch

.cmd_1F:                            ; set loop address = current+1
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_INC_E4}{PYNWmai0-YKM7U5LKWXQRE6XMMPCFSM6W4I000000-1}
    LDA     $E4
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_LOOP_ADDR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-24}
    LDA     $E5
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_LOOP_ADDR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-24}+1
    JMP     .fetch

.cmd_20:                            ; set gosub address = current+1
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_INC_E4}{PYNWmai0-YKM7U5LKWXQRE6XMMPCFSM6W4I000000-1}
    LDA     $E4
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_GOSUB_ADDR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-24}
    LDA     $E5
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_GOSUB_ADDR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-24}+1
    JMP     .fetch
\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}ACTION{\_}VEC}}{SCRIPT:unACTION:unVEC}}\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}ADVANCE}}{SCRIPT:unADVANCE}}\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}GOSUB{\_}ADDR}}{SCRIPT:unGOSUB:unADDR}}\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}INC{\_}E4}}{SCRIPT:unINC:unE4}}\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}LOOP{\_}ADDR}}{SCRIPT:unLOOP:unADDR}}\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}PRNG{\_}MASK}}{SCRIPT:unPRNG:unMASK}}\\{{\nwixident{STOW}}{STOW}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}ACTION{\_}VEC}}{SCRIPT:unACTION:unVEC}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-5}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}ADVANCE}}{SCRIPT:unADVANCE}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-5}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}GOSUB{\_}ADDR}}{SCRIPT:unGOSUB:unADDR}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-5}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}INC{\_}E4}}{SCRIPT:unINC:unE4}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-5}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}LOOP{\_}ADDR}}{SCRIPT:unLOOP:unADDR}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-5}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}PRNG{\_}MASK}}{SCRIPT:unPRNG:unMASK}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-5}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{STOW}}{STOW}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-5}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{322}\nwdocspar

\subsubsection{Action dispatch ($\geq$ \$27)}

When the script byte is {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}27\nwendquote} or higher, the PRNG output is masked and
XORed with the action byte, introducing randomness.  The action vector
at {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}F6\nwendquote} is set by the handlers at {\Tt{}SCRIPT{\textbackslash}{\_}ACTION{\textbackslash}{\_}VEC\nwendquote}.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{323}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-6}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-6}}}\moddef{script engine~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-1}}}\plusendmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwprevnextdefs{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-5}{\relax}\nwenddeflinemarkup

.action:
    STA     $E2                     ; save action byte
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{STEP_PRNG}{PYNWmai0-3OGDZ4EYEYE7YXQHNEV2CZPRBM000000-1}
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{PRNG_OUTPUT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-9}             ; PRNG output
    AND     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_PRNG_MASK}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-24}        ; apply mask
    EOR     $E2                     ; XOR with action byte
    STA     $E1                     ; modified action
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_INC_E4}{PYNWmai0-YKM7U5LKWXQRE6XMMPCFSM6W4I000000-1}           ; advance script pointer
    LDY     #$00
    LDA     ($E4),Y                 ; read parameter byte
    STA     $E2
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_ACTION_INDIRECT}{PYNWmai0-YKM7U5LKWXQRE6XMMPCFSM6W4I000000-1}  ; → JMP (\nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_ACTION_VEC}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-24})
    JMP     ($F6)                   ; dispatch via action vector
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}ENGINE}}{SCRIPT:unENGINE}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-6}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}ENGINE}}{SCRIPT:unENGINE}}}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{PRNG{\_}OUTPUT}}{PRNG:unOUTPUT}}\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}ACTION{\_}INDIRECT}}{SCRIPT:unACTION:unINDIRECT}}\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}ACTION{\_}VEC}}{SCRIPT:unACTION:unVEC}}\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}INC{\_}E4}}{SCRIPT:unINC:unE4}}\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}PRNG{\_}MASK}}{SCRIPT:unPRNG:unMASK}}\\{{\nwixident{STEP{\_}PRNG}}{STEP:unPRNG}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{PRNG{\_}OUTPUT}}{PRNG:unOUTPUT}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-6}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}ACTION{\_}INDIRECT}}{SCRIPT:unACTION:unINDIRECT}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-6}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}ACTION{\_}VEC}}{SCRIPT:unACTION:unVEC}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-6}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}INC{\_}E4}}{SCRIPT:unINC:unE4}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-6}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}PRNG{\_}MASK}}{SCRIPT:unPRNG:unMASK}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-6}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{STEP{\_}PRNG}}{STEP:unPRNG}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-6}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{324}\nwdocspar

\subsection{advance (\$7A4F)}

The ``advance'' routine is the target of all {\Tt{}JMP\ SCRIPT{\textbackslash}{\_}ADVANCE\nwendquote} in
the control commands.  It increments the script pointer, checks for user
input (during attract mode), and loops back to {\Tt{}.fetch\nwendquote}.

During the attract screen ({\Tt{}ATTRACT{\textbackslash}{\_}FLAG\nwendquote} = 1), this routine checks for
keyboard or joystick input.  If detected, it returns immediately via RTS,
which exits the entire {\Tt{}SCRIPT{\textbackslash}{\_}ENGINE\nwendquote} call.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{325}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-V3JA2NOBVSV23YOIWF45X5ET3A000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-V3JA2NOBVSV23YOIWF45X5ET3A000000-1}}}\moddef{script advance~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-V3JA2NOBVSV23YOIWF45X5ET3A000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $7A4F
\nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_ADVANCE}{PYNWmai0-V3JA2NOBVSV23YOIWF45X5ET3A000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_INC_E4}{PYNWmai0-YKM7U5LKWXQRE6XMMPCFSM6W4I000000-1}           ; advance script pointer
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{ATTRACT_FLAG}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-10}            ; attract_flag
    BEQ     .continue               ; not attract mode → skip input check

    ; Attract mode: check keyboard
    LDA     $C000                   ; keyboard register
    BPL     .check_joy              ; no key → check joystick
    RTS                             ; key pressed → exit

.check_joy:
    LDA     $5A00                   ; joystick flag
    BEQ     .continue               ; no joystick → continue script
    LDX     #$00
    LDA     $C061,X                 ; button 0
    BPL     .btn1                   ; not pressed
    RTS                             ; pressed → exit
.btn1:
    INX
    LDA     $C061,X                 ; button 1
    BPL     .continue               ; not pressed → continue
    RTS                             ; pressed → exit

.continue:
    LSR     $5A8C                   ; shift timing flag
    JMP     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_ENGINE}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-6}.fetch     ; loop back to interpreter
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}ADVANCE}}{SCRIPT:unADVANCE}{PYNWmai0-V3JA2NOBVSV23YOIWF45X5ET3A000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}ADVANCE}}{SCRIPT:unADVANCE}}}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{ATTRACT{\_}FLAG}}{ATTRACT:unFLAG}}\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}ENGINE}}{SCRIPT:unENGINE}}\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}INC{\_}E4}}{SCRIPT:unINC:unE4}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{ATTRACT{\_}FLAG}}{ATTRACT:unFLAG}{PYNWmai0-V3JA2NOBVSV23YOIWF45X5ET3A000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}ENGINE}}{SCRIPT:unENGINE}{PYNWmai0-V3JA2NOBVSV23YOIWF45X5ET3A000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}INC{\_}E4}}{SCRIPT:unINC:unE4}{PYNWmai0-V3JA2NOBVSV23YOIWF45X5ET3A000000-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{326}\nwdocspar

\subsection{script helpers}

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{327}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-YKM7U5LKWXQRE6XMMPCFSM6W4I000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-YKM7U5LKWXQRE6XMMPCFSM6W4I000000-1}}}\moddef{script helpers~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-YKM7U5LKWXQRE6XMMPCFSM6W4I000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup

    BEQ     .carry

    INC     $E5
    RTS

    ORG     $7A4C

\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}ACTION{\_}INDIRECT}}{SCRIPT:unACTION:unINDIRECT}{PYNWmai0-YKM7U5LKWXQRE6XMMPCFSM6W4I000000-1}\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}INC{\_}E4}}{SCRIPT:unINC:unE4}{PYNWmai0-YKM7U5LKWXQRE6XMMPCFSM6W4I000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}ACTION{\_}INDIRECT}}{SCRIPT:unACTION:unINDIRECT}}\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}INC{\_}E4}}{SCRIPT:unINC:unE4}}}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}ACTION{\_}VEC}}{SCRIPT:unACTION:unVEC}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}ACTION{\_}VEC}}{SCRIPT:unACTION:unVEC}{PYNWmai0-YKM7U5LKWXQRE6XMMPCFSM6W4I000000-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{328}\nwdocspar

\section{Scene data loading (\$6DD8)}

Loads scene-specific data from disk into the {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}5C00\nwendquote} region.  The disk
read calls {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}B300\nwendquote}, which is part of the EALDR disk I/O code still
resident in memory.  If the read fails, the routine fills a byte with
PRNG output (a graceful degradation rather than crashing).

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{329}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-3XMQPOG4ARI455O23BBDT5GCTE000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-3XMQPOG4ARI455O23BBDT5GCTE000000-1}}}\moddef{load scene data~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-3XMQPOG4ARI455O23BBDT5GCTE000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $6DD8
\nwlinkedidentc{LOAD_SCENE_DATA}{PYNWmai0-3XMQPOG4ARI455O23BBDT5GCTE000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    BIT     $C0E9                   ; check disk controller
    LDA     #$05                    ; \\
    LDY     #$04                    ;  | ($08)+4 = 5 (track configuration)
    STA     ($08),Y                 ; /
    LDA     #$00
    JSR     $6C18                   ; prepare disk parameters
    CLC
    JSR     $B300                   ; EALDR disk read routine
    BCS     .error
    RTS

.error:
    LDY     \nwlinkedidentc{PRNG_OUTPUT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-9}             ; on error: fill with PRNG data
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{STEP_PRNG}{PYNWmai0-3OGDZ4EYEYE7YXQHNEV2CZPRBM000000-1}
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{PRNG_OUTPUT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-9}
    STA     $9AA6,Y
    RTS
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{LOAD{\_}SCENE{\_}DATA}}{LOAD:unSCENE:unDATA}{PYNWmai0-3XMQPOG4ARI455O23BBDT5GCTE000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{LOAD{\_}SCENE{\_}DATA}}{LOAD:unSCENE:unDATA}}}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{PRNG{\_}OUTPUT}}{PRNG:unOUTPUT}}\\{{\nwixident{STEP{\_}PRNG}}{STEP:unPRNG}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{PRNG{\_}OUTPUT}}{PRNG:unOUTPUT}{PYNWmai0-3XMQPOG4ARI455O23BBDT5GCTE000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{STEP{\_}PRNG}}{STEP:unPRNG}{PYNWmai0-3XMQPOG4ARI455O23BBDT5GCTE000000-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{330}\nwdocspar

\section{Unresolved: \$A478}
\label{sec:a478}

The scene loop calls {\Tt{}JSR\ {\textbackslash}{\$}A478\nwendquote} every iteration to check for user
input.  This address is in the EALDR region ({\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}A000\nwendquote}--{\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}BFFF\nwendquote}),
which remains in memory after the main program starts.

The bytes at {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}A478\nwendquote} include the undocumented NMOS 6502 opcode {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}04\nwendquote}
(a 2-byte NOP).  This could mean the code legitimately uses undocumented
instructions, or that the region is modified at runtime before being called.

Partial decode:

\begin{verbatim}
    A478: 04 E5         ; NOP $E5 (DOP: 2-byte NOP, reads zp $E5)
    A47A: 19 03 64      ; ORA $6403,Y
    ...
    A483: CA            ; DEX
    A484: D0 FD         ; BNE $A483   (inner delay loop)
    A486: 38            ; SEC
    A487: E9 01         ; SBC #$01
    A489: D0 F6         ; BNE $A481   (outer delay loop)
    A48B: 60            ; RTS
\end{verbatim}

The inner loop at {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}A483\nwendquote}--{\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}A484\nwendquote} ({\Tt{}DEX;\ BNE\nwendquote}) is a standard
delay loop.  The outer loop decrements A and repeats, making this a
nested delay.  The carry flag state on exit likely indicates whether a
key was pressed (C=1) or the timer expired (C=0).  Further analysis
requires an emulator that supports undocumented 6502 opcodes.

\section{Summary}

The attract screen call flow:

\begin{itemize}
  \item {\Tt{}MAIN{\textbackslash}{\_}ENTRY\nwendquote} ({\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}0800\nwendquote}): calls {\Tt{}GAME{\textbackslash}{\_}INIT\nwendquote}, then
        {\Tt{}ATTRACT{\textbackslash}{\_}SCREEN\nwendquote} if {\Tt{}TOTAL{\textbackslash}{\_}MOB{\textbackslash}{\_}COUNT\nwendquote} is zero.
  \item {\Tt{}ATTRACT{\textbackslash}{\_}SCREEN\nwendquote} ({\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}09F4\nwendquote}): sets scene index 1, calls
        {\Tt{}COMPUTE{\textbackslash}{\_}SCENE{\textbackslash}{\_}PTR\nwendquote}, tail-calls {\Tt{}SCENE{\textbackslash}{\_}LOOP\nwendquote} with scene \$26.
  \item {\Tt{}SCENE{\textbackslash}{\_}LOOP\nwendquote} ({\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}6C37\nwendquote}): saves ZP pointers, steps PRNG,
        conditionally loads scene data from disk.  In a loop: checks
        keyboard/timer via {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}A478\nwendquote}, displays status bar, renders scene
        text via {\Tt{}TEXT{\textbackslash}{\_}RENDERER\nwendquote}, runs {\Tt{}SCRIPT{\textbackslash}{\_}ENGINE\nwendquote} with script \#3.
        Exits when user presses a key or scene sequence ends.
\end{itemize}

Key subsystems:
\begin{itemize}
  \item \textbf{Text renderer} ({\Tt{}TEXT{\textbackslash}{\_}RENDERER\nwendquote}): Reads byte streams with
        position commands, pause/reset control codes, and character data
        for the HRCG font.
  \item \textbf{Script engine} ({\Tt{}SCRIPT{\textbackslash}{\_}ENGINE\nwendquote}): Runs short bytecode
        programs from {\Tt{}SCRIPT{\textbackslash}{\_}TABLE\nwendquote}.  Supports loops, gosub, action
        dispatch with PRNG randomization.
  \item \textbf{Resident interpreter} ({\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}0500\nwendquote}--{\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}07FF\nwendquote}): A
        secondary VM copied from EALDR, using context-swapped zero-page
        state and XOR-encrypted addresses.
  \item \textbf{PRNG} ({\Tt{}STEP{\textbackslash}{\_}PRNG\nwendquote}): Linear congruential generator with
        formula $\texttt{val}_{n+1} = 69 \cdot \texttt{val}_n + \$53
        \pmod{256}$.
\end{itemize}


\chapter{Animating the splash screen}

The {\Tt{}start{\_}splash{\_}screen\nwendquote} routine first loads up the initial splash screen,
sets {\Tt{}indirect{\_}routine\nwendquote} to {\Tt{}note{\_}played\nwendquote}, and begins the sound routine by
calling {\Tt{}start{\_}sound\nwendquote}.

{\Tt{}note{\_}played\nwendquote} plots a mob, then sets {\Tt{}indirect{\_}routine\nwendquote} to {\Tt{}splash{\_}routine{\_}2\nwendquote}
and jumps to {\Tt{}next{\_}table{\_}entry\nwendquote}.

{\Tt{}splash{\_}routine{\_}2\nwendquote} calls a routine first with {\Tt{}{\$}5E1F\nwendquote} then with {\Tt{}{\$}5E3A\nwendquote},
then jumps to {\Tt{}splash{\_}screen{\_}step\nwendquote}.

{\Tt{}splash{\_}screen{\_}step\nwendquote} then sets {\Tt{}indirect{\_}routine\nwendquote} to {\Tt{}splash{\_}routine{\_}1\nwendquote}
then {\Tt{}splash{\_}routine{\_}0\nwendquote} and calls {\Tt{}set{\_}splash{\_}routine\nwendquote} within {\Tt{}note{\_}played\nwendquote}.
After that, {\Tt{}splash{\_}screen{\_}step\nwendquote} presumably moves mobs around.


When the user ends the splash screen, the {\Tt{}start{\_}splash{\_}screen\nwendquote} routine
replaces the indirect jump to {\Tt{}indirect{\_}routine\nwendquote} in {\Tt{}start{\_}sound\nwendquote} to an
absolute jump to {\Tt{}next{\_}table{\_}entry\nwendquote}, since there is no further need to
animate while playing sound.


\chapter{The data}
\subsection{Message data}

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{331}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-MA3WDYAYUKINVQ6W4447HHOCBE000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-MA3WDYAYUKINVQ6W4447HHOCBE000000-1}}}\moddef{Message data~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-MA3WDYAYUKINVQ6W4447HHOCBE000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwenddeflinemarkup

\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{MESSAGE{\_}DATA}}{MESSAGE:unDATA}}}\nwnotused{Message data}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{332}\nwdocspar

\subsection{Location data}

Location data and character data share the same 9-byte record table at
{\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}4000\nwendquote}.  {\Tt{}GET{\textbackslash}{\_}CHAR{\textbackslash}{\_}RECORD\nwendquote} indexes into this table (index~$\times$~9
+ \$4000).  Record~0 at \$4000 is a header; records~1--62 are the actual
entries.  {\Tt{}LOCATION{\textbackslash}{\_}DATA\nwendquote} points to record~1 (\$4009).

Each record is 9~bytes:

\begin{center}
\begin{tabular}{cll}
\textbf{Offset} & \textbf{Name}     & \textbf{Description} \\
\hline
0--1 & name\_ptr   & 16-bit pointer to length-prefixed location name \\
2    & mob\_head   & Head of mob linked list (character index, 0~=~none) \\
3    & min\_pos    & Top-left bounding box (row $\times$ 20 + col) \\
4    & max\_pos    & Bottom-right bounding box (row $\times$ 20 + col) \\
5    & map\_id     & Bits 0--6: map scene ID.  Bit~7: visited flag (set at runtime) \\
6--7 & event\_ptr  & 16-bit pointer to event/object list (3-byte entries) \\
8    & mob\_count  & Number of mobs (summed into {\Tt{}TOTAL{\textbackslash}{\_}MOB{\textbackslash}{\_}COUNT\nwendquote})
\end{tabular}
\end{center}

The event list at {\Tt{}event{\textbackslash}{\_}ptr\nwendquote} consists of 3-byte entries (see
\S\ref{sec:event-format} for the full format).  Byte~0 is a map position
(\$FE~=~empty slot, \$FF~=~end-of-list); byte~1 encodes the event type
and status; byte~2 is type-dependent action data.

The map scene~ID (field~5, bits~0--6) is compared with {\Tt{}LOCATION{\textbackslash}{\_}FLAG2\nwendquote}
(\$5A56); when it changes, {\Tt{}FILL{\textbackslash}{\_}MAP\nwendquote} is called to redraw the map.
Bit~7 is set on first entry via {\Tt{}ORA\ {\textbackslash}{\#}{\textbackslash}{\$}80\nwendquote} and tested with {\Tt{}BMI\nwendquote} to
skip first-visit logic on subsequent entries.

The sentinel {\Tt{}FFFF\nwendquote} in the name pointer marks the end of the table.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{333}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-ERFGCV2MLBMWTJDOVNONPK6K3I000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-ERFGCV2MLBMWTJDOVNONPK6K3I000000-1}}}\moddef{Location data~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-ERFGCV2MLBMWTJDOVNONPK6K3I000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwenddeflinemarkup

\subsection{Event list format}
\label{sec:event-format}

Each location has a variable-length event list pointed to by
{\Tt{}event{\textbackslash}{\_}ptr\nwendquote} (location record fields~6--7).  Entries are 3~bytes each,
terminated by {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}FF\nwendquote} followed by two {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}FF\nwendquote} padding bytes.  Each
location's first entry is normally an empty slot ({\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}FE\nwendquote}) reserved for
runtime use (e.g.\ dropped treasure after combat).

\paragraph{Byte~0: map position.}
A value 0--199 encodes a grid position (row~$\times$~20~+~col).
{\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}FE\nwendquote} marks an empty slot that can be filled at runtime.
{\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}FF\nwendquote} marks the end of the list.

\paragraph{Byte~1: event type.}
The top two bits select the category:

\begin{center}
\begin{tabular}{lll}
\textbf{Byte~1 range} & \textbf{Category} & \textbf{Details} \\
\hline
\$00--\$3F & Random encounter & Probability check vs.\ character stat; \\
           &                  & on fail, bit~6 is set $\to$ becomes specific encounter \\
\$40--\$BF & Specific encounter & bits~5--0 = mob index $\to$ {\Tt{}ACTIVE{\textbackslash}{\_}CHAR\nwendquote} \\
\$C0--\$D1 & Dropped treasure & gold = ((\texttt{byte1} $-$ \$C0) $\times$ 256) + \texttt{byte2} \\
\$D2       & Persistent scene & \texttt{byte2} = scene ID; not cleared after trigger \\
\$D3       & One-time scene   & \texttt{byte2} = scene ID; slot cleared to \$FE \\
\$D4       & Scene + item drop & like \$D3 but also spawns 1--4 bonus items \\
\$D5--\$DA & Map/area event   & indexed from table at \$7EDD \\
\$DB--\$FD & (unknown)        & \\
\$FE       & Empty-slot data  & \texttt{byte2} has sub-encoding
\end{tabular}
\end{center}

\paragraph{Byte~2: action data} (meaning depends on byte~1).
For encounters (\$40--\$BF), this is the map position where the mob
appears.  For treasure (\$C0--\$D1), the gold amount low byte.
For scene events (\$D2--\$D4), a scene/event~ID.

\paragraph{Key routines.}
\begin{itemize}
\item \$0B62 --- searches a position for mobs first, then events;
      returns {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}BE/{\textbackslash}{\$}BF\nwendquote} pointing to the found entry.
\item {\Tt{}FUN{\textbackslash}{\_}138D\nwendquote} (\$138D) --- finds the nearest non-activated event
      (byte~1~$<$~\$C0) using Manhattan distance; used for AI
      pathfinding.
\item \$1260 --- fills empty {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}FE\nwendquote} slots with combat loot, or
      accumulates value in \$C0--\$D0 entries (treasure drops).
      Entries saturate at byte~1~=~\$D1.
\item {\Tt{}HANDLE{\textbackslash}{\_}ENCOUNTER\nwendquote} (\$1C01) --- encounter handler: dispatches
      random vs.\ specific encounters based on byte~1~$<$~\$40.
\end{itemize}

\chapter{Combat}

\section{Manual}

According to the original manual:

Strike probability

Whenever any character tries to strike another character, the game will
compute his chance of success. Any character's base chance of striking
his victim is 3.125% times their dexterity. Thus, a player with a dexterity of
11 has a 34.375% chance of striking his victim. However, the base chance is
adjusted by several factors:

If the victim is:

particularly difficult to hit

(halflings and elves have this ability to dodge) . . .. .. . ... subtract 12.5%
particularly easy to hit. . . . . . ....... . .. . .. .. .. .. . .. . . . .. . add 12.5%
extremely easy to hit ....... . . ... . . .. . . .. .. .. . .. . . . .. ... . add 25%
down (unconscious, in hand to hand combat, or resting) .. . . add 18.75%
currently resting (this is in
addition to the adjustment for being down) . . . .. .. . . . . . .. . add 9.375 %
defending . .. .. ..... .. .. . ... . . . ... . ........ . ..... subtract 9.375%
attacking ..... . ... . ... . ..... . ... ... ..... .... . . ... . no adjustment
running . . .... . .. . ..... .. .... . ... . .. .. .. . ..... . .. subtract 3.125 %
on the same space with attacker, the stronger character is
is given an advantage .. . .. . add 1.5625% times attackers strength and
subtract 1.5625% times victim's strength

The chance of striking the victim is then adjusted, if necessary, so that it
is never less than 3.125% nor greater than 96.875%.

The probabilities are in increments of 1/32. In the code, 1/32 is represented by
a single count in 6 bits, so the maximum count is 31 (96.875%).

DATA[0,1] = name
DATA[4] = creature type:
  0x00: Human
  0x01: Elf
  0x02: Dwarf
  0x03: Halfling
  0x15: Human
  0x23: Human (Morgiana, Princess Buddir)
  0x3C: Owl
  0x3F: Statue, Sultan, Right guard, Left guard, small zombie, big zombie
  0x41: Dwarf
  0x43: Thief
  0x44: Bear
  0x45: Rat
  0x46: Wolf
  0x47: Dragon
  0x48: Greasy
  0x4A: Sword
  0x4B: Ram
  0x4C: Scorpion
  0x4D: Succubus
  0x4E: Tiger, Leo, Jackal
  0x4F: Crab
  0x50: Bull
  0x54: Zombie (Witless)
  0x58: Thief
  0x59: Brown Bear
  0x5E: Wanderer
  0x5F: Mechanical Sword
  0x61: Scorpion (Giant)
  0x65: Sonny Boy Minotaur
  0x93: Statue (Gemini I, Gemini II)
  0x93: Aladdin
  0x94: Elf
  0x9B: White Dragon
  0x9E: Bane of Thieves
  0xA6: Unicorn

DATA[5] = STR
DATA[6] = CON/HP 0-3F
DATA[7] = MEL-1
DATA[9] = HTH-1
DATA[B] =
  7: Extremely easy to hit
  6: Particularly difficult to hit
  5: ? Incredibly easy to hit?
  4: DEX-1
  3: DEX-1
  2: DEX-1
  1: DEX-1
  0: DEX-1

DATA[C] = SPD
DATA[F] =
  7:
  6:
  5:
  4:
  3:
  2: Unconscious/Down
  1: State
  0: State

State:
  0:
  1:
  2:
  3: Defending

\section{Turn processing}

\subsection{game\_turn\_loop (\$19AD)}
\label{sec:game-turn-loop}

Handles one character's complete turn---movement, input, encounters,
and event dispatch.  Called once per character per game tick.

\paragraph{Setup.}
The character's current position (field~3 of the record at {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}F8\nwendquote})
is split into column and row.  Movement flags are cleared, and the
number of movement points is read from field~12 (low nibble).
If the character's constitution (field~6, bits~0--5) is below~3,
or if {\Tt{}CHECK{\textbackslash}{\_}ENCOUNTER\nwendquote} returns~2 (hostile territory), a
``restricted'' flag is set (bit~2 of field~15).

\paragraph{Input.}
For the player ({\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}5A05\nwendquote}~=~0), keyboard input is read via the
resident dispatch at {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}A44C\nwendquote}.  For NPCs, {\Tt{}AI{\textbackslash}{\_}CHOOSE{\textbackslash}{\_}TARGET\nwendquote}
selects a destination and {\Tt{}FUN{\textbackslash}{\_}6742\nwendquote} computes a direction.
The direction value encodes both movement and commands:

\begin{center}
\begin{tabular}{cl}
\textbf{Value} & \textbf{Action} \\
\hline
1 & North (row$-$) \\
2 & South (row$+$) \\
3 & West (col$-$) \\
4 & East (col$+$) \\
5 & Pass (skip turn) \\
6 & Action 6 $\to$ \$14CD \\
7 & Action 7 $\to$ \$14B7 \\
8 & Action 8 $\to$ set state~1 \\
9 & Fight/attack $\to$ \$143F
\end{tabular}
\end{center}

\paragraph{Movement.}
After applying the direction, the new position is converted via
{\Tt{}COLROW{\textbackslash}{\_}TO{\textbackslash}{\_}POS\nwendquote} and checked with {\Tt{}FIND{\textbackslash}{\_}ENTITY{\textbackslash}{\_}AT{\textbackslash}{\_}POS\nwendquote}.
If the cell is empty, the move is committed (position updated, sprite
redrawn) and adjacent threats are re-checked.  Finding no threats
ends the turn early.

\paragraph{Encounter dispatch.}
If something occupies the destination cell, the result from
{\Tt{}FIND{\textbackslash}{\_}ENTITY{\textbackslash}{\_}AT{\textbackslash}{\_}POS\nwendquote} determines the handler:
\begin{itemize}
\item {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}BF\nwendquote} $\geq$ \$80 --- mob encounter $\to$ \$1E5A
\item Event byte~1 bits~7--6 $\neq$ \$C0 --- {\Tt{}HANDLE{\textbackslash}{\_}ENCOUNTER\nwendquote}
\item \$C0--\$D1 --- {\Tt{}PICKUP{\textbackslash}{\_}TREASURE\nwendquote}
\item \$D2--\$D4 --- {\Tt{}TRIGGER{\textbackslash}{\_}SCENE{\textbackslash}{\_}EVENT\nwendquote}
\item \$D5--\$DA --- map/area event $\to$ \$70DF
\item \$FE --- empty-slot interaction $\to$ \$1D4D
\end{itemize}

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{339}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}}}\moddef{defines~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-1}}}\plusendmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwprevnextdefs{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-24}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-26}\nwenddeflinemarkup
\nwlinkedidentc{CHAR_AI_MODE}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}    EQU     $5A05   ; 0 = player, 2-5 = AI behavior modes
\nwlinkedidentc{TURN_START_COL}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}  EQU     $5A61   ; column at start of turn
\nwlinkedidentc{TURN_START_ROW}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}  EQU     $5A62   ; row at start of turn
\nwlinkedidentc{CURRENT_COL}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}     EQU     $5A63   ; current column during turn
\nwlinkedidentc{CURRENT_ROW}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}     EQU     $5A64   ; current row during turn
\nwlinkedidentc{MOVE_POINTS}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}     EQU     $5A65   ; movement points remaining
\nwlinkedidentc{STEPS_TAKEN}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}     EQU     $5A66   ; steps taken this turn
\nwlinkedidentc{INPUT_DIR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}       EQU     $5A67   ; direction/command from input (1-9)
\nwlinkedidentc{TURN_ACTIVE}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}     EQU     $5B27   ; 1 while turn is in progress
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{CHAR{\_}AI{\_}MODE}}{CHAR:unAI:unMODE}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{CURRENT{\_}COL}}{CURRENT:unCOL}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{CURRENT{\_}ROW}}{CURRENT:unROW}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{INPUT{\_}DIR}}{INPUT:unDIR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{MOVE{\_}POINTS}}{MOVE:unPOINTS}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{STEPS{\_}TAKEN}}{STEPS:unTAKEN}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{TURN{\_}ACTIVE}}{TURN:unACTIVE}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{TURN{\_}START{\_}COL}}{TURN:unSTART:unCOL}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{TURN{\_}START{\_}ROW}}{TURN:unSTART:unROW}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{CHAR{\_}AI{\_}MODE}}{CHAR:unAI:unMODE}}\\{{\nwixident{CURRENT{\_}COL}}{CURRENT:unCOL}}\\{{\nwixident{CURRENT{\_}ROW}}{CURRENT:unROW}}\\{{\nwixident{INPUT{\_}DIR}}{INPUT:unDIR}}\\{{\nwixident{MOVE{\_}POINTS}}{MOVE:unPOINTS}}\\{{\nwixident{STEPS{\_}TAKEN}}{STEPS:unTAKEN}}\\{{\nwixident{TURN{\_}ACTIVE}}{TURN:unACTIVE}}\\{{\nwixident{TURN{\_}START{\_}COL}}{TURN:unSTART:unCOL}}\\{{\nwixident{TURN{\_}START{\_}ROW}}{TURN:unSTART:unROW}}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{340}\nwdocspar

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{341}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-5SXQOZOU4UJBYWY65C5UO66FXM000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-5SXQOZOU4UJBYWY65C5UO66FXM000000-1}}}\moddef{game turn loop~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-5SXQOZOU4UJBYWY65C5UO66FXM000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $19AD
\nwlinkedidentc{GAME_TURN_LOOP}{PYNWmai0-5SXQOZOU4UJBYWY65C5UO66FXM000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    ; --- setup: save position, clear flags ---
    LDA     #$01
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{TURN_ACTIVE}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}
    LDY     #$03
    LDA     ($F8),Y             ; char field 3 = packed position
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{POS_TO_COLROW}{PYNWmai0-AMTAHZ55D6ORMSENT2EMDCDU24000000-1}
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{CURRENT_COL}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{TURN_START_COL}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}
    STY     \nwlinkedidentc{CURRENT_ROW}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}
    STY     \nwlinkedidentc{TURN_START_ROW}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}
    LDA     #$00
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{STEPS_TAKEN}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{CLEAR_RESTRICTED}{PYNWmai0-OXJ6PDFP4WAAZROIET364P3TEQ000000-1}            ; clear restricted flag (bit 2 of field 15)

    ; --- check constitution and encounters ---
    LDY     #$06
    LDA     ($F8),Y             ; char field 6 (constitution/HP)
    AND     #$3F
    CMP     #$03
    BPL     .con_ok
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SET_RESTRICTED}{PYNWmai0-YHGBDEY4D7QOR7DE6PEYT23PTI000000-1}            ; set restricted (too weak)
.con_ok:
    LDY     #$03
    LDA     ($F8),Y
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{CHECK_ENCOUNTER}{PYNWmai0-PIBYNYNPF7BMUKCGA5W4VJAN7E000000-1}
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{ENCOUNTER_RESULT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-16}
    CMP     #$02
    BNE     .enc_ok
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SET_RESTRICTED}{PYNWmai0-YHGBDEY4D7QOR7DE6PEYT23PTI000000-1}            ; set restricted (hostile territory)
.enc_ok:
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{CHAR_AI_MODE}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}
    BEQ     .get_speed
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{AI_CHOOSE_TARGET}{PYNWmai0-KEFBT3V5UBIE5Q2SEGO4W6K6CM000000-1}    ; NPC: pick a destination

    ; --- determine movement points ---
.get_speed:
    LDY     #$0C
    LDA     ($F8),Y             ; char field 12
    AND     #$0F                ; low nibble = speed
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{MOVE_POINTS}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}

    ; --- adjust points based on threats ---
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{ENCOUNTER_RESULT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-16}
    CMP     #$02
    BEQ     .chk_limit          ; hostile → check if enough to limit
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{CHECK_THREATS_HERE}{PYNWmai0-5XFSUJMLANXR5KCTBY476ZV264000000-1}            ; check adjacent threats
    CMP     #$01
    BEQ     .move_loop          ; exactly 1 threat → keep full
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{MOVE_POINTS}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}
    CMP     #$02
    BCC     .move_loop          ; < 2 points → keep as is
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{RANDOM_IN_RANGE}{PYNWmai0-F6322QSFMTRJBO2IS2F3GEYRZU000000-1}     ; random(move_points)
    CMP     #$00
    BEQ     .do_limit           ; random == 0 → force limit
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{MOVE_POINTS}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}         ; reduce randomly
    BNE     .move_loop
.chk_limit:
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{MOVE_POINTS}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}
    CMP     #$02
    BCC     .move_loop          ; < 2 → use as is
.do_limit:
    LDA     #$01
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{RANDOM_IN_RANGE}{PYNWmai0-F6322QSFMTRJBO2IS2F3GEYRZU000000-1}     ; random(1) → 0 or 1
    CLC
    ADC     #$01                ; 1 or 2
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{MOVE_POINTS}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}
    BNE     .move_loop          ; always

    ; === MOVEMENT LOOP ===
.move_loop:
    LDA     #$00
    CMP     \nwlinkedidentc{MOVE_POINTS}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}
    BNE     .has_points
    CMP     \nwlinkedidentc{STEPS_TAKEN}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}
    BNE     .end_turn           ; out of points, took steps → done
    CMP     \nwlinkedidentc{CHAR_AI_MODE}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}
    BEQ     .has_points         ; player with 0 points, 0 steps → still prompt
.end_turn:
    JMP     \nwlinkedidentc{END_TURN}{PYNWmai0-GZTPGL2FM3FQKCWDSITXS6OEXM000000-1}            ; end turn

.has_points:
    CMP     \nwlinkedidentc{CHAR_AI_MODE}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}
    BEQ     .player_input
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{NPC_MOVE_AI}{PYNWmai0-N3DFIYE2R6ICV4QVZCN57IVM74000000-1}            ; NPC movement AI
    JMP     .dispatch_cmd

    ; --- player input ---
.player_input:
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{CONFIGURE_INPUT}{PYNWmai0-5AOH2UYP2OPU5MTN2ZBLLHP5RM000000-1}            ; set up input UI
    LDA     $6081               ; check if input available
    BNE     .have_input
    JMP     \nwlinkedidentc{TEARDOWN_INPUT}{PYNWmai0-OJRO4HJVQSJCJU7YEKWD4RCPVA000000-1}            ; no input → exit
.have_input:
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{GET_INPUT_TABLE_PTR}{PYNWmai0-A6CRSL6GBHUJIXZC3QWZGSPUI4000000-1}
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SETUP_INPUT}{PYNWmai0-MTJUFOYWWTE4EHS6DWZJZ4YJVY000000-1}
    JSR     $A44C               ; resident: read keyboard
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{INPUT_DIR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}
    CMP     #$00
    BNE     .do_move            ; player goes straight to movement
    JMP     \nwlinkedidentc{TEARDOWN_INPUT}{PYNWmai0-OJRO4HJVQSJCJU7YEKWD4RCPVA000000-1}            ; cancelled

    ; --- NPC command dispatch (player skips this) ---
.dispatch_cmd:
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{INPUT_DIR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}
    CMP     #$05
    BCC     .do_move            ; 1-4: movement direction
    BNE     .not_pass
    JMP     .move_loop          ; 5: pass
.not_pass:
    CMP     #$09
    BNE     .not_fight
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SET_RESTRICTED}{PYNWmai0-YHGBDEY4D7QOR7DE6PEYT23PTI000000-1}            ; 9: fight → set restricted
    LDA     #$00
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SET_CHAR_STATE}{PYNWmai0-CBVYIWFRJGEOPJMLWQHLZ77QQI000000-1}
    JMP     \nwlinkedidentc{AUTO_HEAL}{PYNWmai0-AX5PBIYZJSUU5MZQS5PB5ACSEQ000000-1}
.not_fight:
    PHA
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{CHECK_AND_RESTRICT}{PYNWmai0-6C735MBISF6TDYIPESKOAABD74000000-1}            ; re-check encounter
    PLA
    CMP     #$07
    BNE     .not_cmd7
    JMP     \nwlinkedidentc{ENTER_COMBAT_STATE}{PYNWmai0-P3IG7U4WEUQV5DROZT5FODZCNI000000-1}            ; 7: action
.not_cmd7:
    BCS     .cmd8
    JMP     \nwlinkedidentc{START_COMBAT}{PYNWmai0-XGQEWEPLC6SIZ6NLZUAHS4CQIQ000000-1}            ; 6: action
.cmd8:
    JMP     \nwlinkedidentc{SET_STATE_FIGHT}{PYNWmai0-RFGCSXY2WIWVU7LTYYFQA4PGQE000000-1}            ; 8: set state 1

    ; --- apply movement direction ---
.do_move:
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{ENCOUNTER_RESULT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-16}
    CMP     #$02
    BMI     .move_ok
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{CHECK_CAN_LEAVE}{PYNWmai0-WRGS4P24HBUXM42NYFMQYI5N7I000000-1}            ; can we leave hostile zone?
    CMP     #$01
    BEQ     .move_ok
    JMP     \nwlinkedidentc{END_TURN}{PYNWmai0-GZTPGL2FM3FQKCWDSITXS6OEXM000000-1}            ; blocked → end turn
.move_ok:
    LDA     #$00
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{ENCOUNTER_RESULT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-16}
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{INPUT_DIR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}
    DEC     \nwlinkedidentc{MOVE_POINTS}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}
    INC     \nwlinkedidentc{STEPS_TAKEN}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}
    CMP     #$02
    BPL     .not_north
    DEC     \nwlinkedidentc{CURRENT_ROW}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}         ; 1: north
    JMP     .check_dest
.not_north:
    BNE     .not_south
    INC     \nwlinkedidentc{CURRENT_ROW}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}         ; 2: south
    JMP     .check_dest
.not_south:
    CMP     #$03
    BNE     .go_east
    DEC     \nwlinkedidentc{CURRENT_COL}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}         ; 3: west
    JMP     .check_dest
.go_east:
    INC     \nwlinkedidentc{CURRENT_COL}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}         ; 4: east

    ; --- check what's at the destination ---
.check_dest:
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{CURRENT_COL}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}
    LDY     \nwlinkedidentc{CURRENT_ROW}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{COLROW_TO_POS}{PYNWmai0-YXZOC7KQXOV5OPKZ6P7KWNTLUM000000-1}
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{FIND_ENTITY_AT_POS}{PYNWmai0-PLJFN4SECKS5ALV334RXDZNCVU000000-1}  ; → $BE/$BF
    LDA     #$00
    CMP     $BF
    BNE     .something          ; $BF != 0 → occupied
    CMP     $BE
    BEQ     .empty              ; $BE == 0 → empty cell
    LDX     #$0E
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_ENGINE}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-6}       ; display blocked message?
    JMP     \nwlinkedidentc{SHOW_LOCKED_MSG}{PYNWmai0-ZBSSUOFY4GEGVSJE7VA5HJFB4Q000000-1}

.empty:
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{COMMIT_MOVE}{PYNWmai0-ZQVA6GBQYGATH77KOXC5SWQ6UE000000-1}            ; commit move (update pos, draw sprite)
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{CHECK_THREATS_HERE}{PYNWmai0-5XFSUJMLANXR5KCTBY476ZV264000000-1}            ; check adjacent threats
    CMP     #$00
    BNE     .keep_moving        ; threats remain → continue
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{MOVE_POINTS}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}         ; no threats → stop
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{TURN_ACTIVE}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}
.keep_moving:
    JMP     .move_loop

    ; --- destination occupied: dispatch by type ---
.something:
    LDA     $BF
    CMP     #$80
    BMI     .event              ; $BF < $80 → event entry
    JMP     \nwlinkedidentc{HANDLE_MOB_ENCOUNTER}{PYNWmai0-INIHNPSMTLV3IPE46YIYDJUJR4000000-1}            ; $BF >= $80 → mob encounter

.event:
    LDY     #$01
    LDA     ($BE),Y             ; event byte 1
    TAX
    AND     #$C0
    CMP     #$C0
    BEQ     .activated
    JMP     \nwlinkedidentc{HANDLE_ENCOUNTER}{PYNWmai0-Y47L2JLEGWPQ32PCM5VXV43OQI000000-1}    ; non-activated → encounter

.activated:
    TXA
    CMP     #$D2
    BPL     .not_treasure
    JMP     \nwlinkedidentc{PICKUP_TREASURE}{PYNWmai0-54OVBRYVAXX7KYNOX73X7MCSVQ000000-1}     ; $C0-$D1: treasure

.not_treasure:
    CMP     #$D5
    BPL     .not_scene
    JMP     \nwlinkedidentc{TRIGGER_SCENE_EVENT}{PYNWmai0-J7Q7EV5KY4I3TMCLNUF4NZNIK4000000-1} ; $D2-$D4: scene event

.not_scene:
    CMP     #$DB
    BPL     .not_map_event
    LDA     $BE                 ; $D5-$DA: map/area event
    PHA
    LDA     $BF
    PHA
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{COMMIT_MOVE}{PYNWmai0-ZQVA6GBQYGATH77KOXC5SWQ6UE000000-1}            ; commit move first
    PLA
    STA     $BF
    PLA
    STA     $BE
    JMP     \nwlinkedidentc{DISPLAY_SHOP}{PYNWmai0-VNMQ4ORRJVI52HTPPC4BL3BETU000000-1}

.not_map_event:
    CMP     #$FE
    BEQ     .empty_slot
    JMP     \nwlinkedidentc{TEARDOWN_INPUT}{PYNWmai0-OJRO4HJVQSJCJU7YEKWD4RCPVA000000-1}            ; $DB-$FD: unknown

.empty_slot:
    JMP     \nwlinkedidentc{HANDLE_EVENT_SLOT}{PYNWmai0-NUGMS767Y6LLXJJOG3KL2RPOTM000000-1}            ; $FE: empty slot interaction

dent{START{\_}COMBAT}}{START:unCOMBAT}}\\{{\nwixident{STEPS{\_}TAKEN}}{STEPS:unTAKEN}}\\{{\nwixident{TEARDOWN{\_}INPUT}}{TEARDOWN:unINPUT}}\\{{\nwixident{TRIGGER{\_}SCENE{\_}EVENT}}{TRIGGER:unSCENE:unEVENT}}\\{{\nwixident{TURN{\_}ACTIVE}}{TURN:unACTIVE}}\\{{\nwixident{TURN{\_}START{\_}COL}}{TURN:unSTART:unCOL}}\\{{\nwixident{TURN{\_}START{\_}ROW}}{TURN:unSTART:unROW}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{AI{\_}CHOOSE{\_}TARGET}}{AI:unCHOOSE:unTARGET}{PYNWmai0-5SXQOZOU4UJBYWY65C5UO66FXM000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{AUTO{\_}HEAL}}{AUTO:unHEAL}{PYNWmai0-5SXQOZOU4UJBYWY65C5UO66FXM000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{CHAR{\_}AI{\_}MODE}}{CHAR:unAI:unMODE}{PYNWmai0-5SXQOZOU4UJBYWY65C5UO66FXM000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{CHECK{\_}AND{\_}RESTRICT}}{CHECK:unAND:unRESTRICT}{PYNWmai0-5SXQOZOU4UJBYWY65C5UO66FXM000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{CHECK{\_}CAN{\_}LEAVE}}{CHECK:unCAN:unLEAVE}{PYNWmai0-5SXQOZOU4UJBYWY65C5UO66FXM000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{CHECK{\_}ENCOUNTER}}{CHECK:unENCOUNTER}{PYNWmai0-5SXQOZOU4UJBYWY65C5UO66FXM000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{CHECK{\_}THREATS{\_}HERE}}{CHECK:unTHREATS:unHERE}{PYNWmai0-5SXQOZOU4UJBYWY65C5UO66FXM000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{CLEAR{\_}RESTRICTED}}{CLEAR:unRESTRICTED}{PYNWmai0-5SXQOZOU4UJBYWY65C5UO66FXM000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{COLROW{\_}TO{\_}POS}}{COLROW:unTO:unPOS}{PYNWmai0-5SXQOZOU4UJBYWY65C5UO66FXM000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{COMMIT{\_}MOVE}}{COMMIT:unMOVE}{PYNWmai0-5SXQOZOU4UJBYWY65C5UO66FXM000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{CONFIGURE{\_}INPUT}}{CONFIGURE:unINPUT}{PYNWmai0-5SXQOZOU4UJBYWY65C5UO66FXM000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{CURRENT{\_}COL}}{CURRENT:unCOL}{PYNWmai0-5SXQOZOU4UJBYWY65C5UO66FXM000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{CURRENT{\_}ROW}}{CURRENT:unROW}{PYNWmai0-5SXQOZOU4UJBYWY65C5UO66FXM000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{DISPLAY{\_}SHOP}}{DISPLAY:unSHOP}{PYNWmai0-5SXQOZOU4UJBYWY65C5UO66FXM000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{ENCOUNTER{\_}RESULT}}{ENCOUNTER:unRESULT}{PYNWmai0-5SXQOZOU4UJBYWY65C5UO66FXM000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{END{\_}TURN}}{END:unTURN}{PYNWmai0-5SXQOZOU4UJBYWY65C5UO66FXM000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{ENTER{\_}COMBAT{\_}STATE}}{ENTER:unCOMBAT:unSTATE}{PYNWmai0-5SXQOZOU4UJBYWY65C5UO66FXM000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{FIND{\_}ENTITY{\_}AT{\_}POS}}{FIND:unENTITY:unAT:unPOS}{PYNWmai0-5SXQOZOU4UJBYWY65C5UO66FXM000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{GET{\_}INPUT{\_}TABLE{\_}PTR}}{GET:unINPUT:unTABLE:unPTR}{PYNWmai0-5SXQOZOU4UJBYWY65C5UO66FXM000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{HANDLE{\_}ENCOUNTER}}{HANDLE:unENCOUNTER}{PYNWmai0-5SXQOZOU4UJBYWY65C5UO66FXM000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{HANDLE{\_}EVENT{\_}SLOT}}{HANDLE:unEVENT:unSLOT}{PYNWmai0-5SXQOZOU4UJBYWY65C5UO66FXM000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{HANDLE{\_}MOB{\_}ENCOUNTER}}{HANDLE:unMOB:unENCOUNTER}{PYNWmai0-5SXQOZOU4UJBYWY65C5UO66FXM000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{INPUT{\_}DIR}}{INPUT:unDIR}{PYNWmai0-5SXQOZOU4UJBYWY65C5UO66FXM000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{MOVE{\_}POINTS}}{MOVE:unPOINTS}{PYNWmai0-5SXQOZOU4UJBYWY65C5UO66FXM000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{NPC{\_}MOVE{\_}AI}}{NPC:unMOVE:unAI}{PYNWmai0-5SXQOZOU4UJBYWY65C5UO66FXM000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{PICKUP{\_}TREASURE}}{PICKUP:unTREASURE}{PYNWmai0-5SXQOZOU4UJBYWY65C5UO66FXM000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{POS{\_}TO{\_}COLROW}}{POS:unTO:unCOLROW}{PYNWmai0-5SXQOZOU4UJBYWY65C5UO66FXM000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{RANDOM{\_}IN{\_}RANGE}}{RANDOM:unIN:unRANGE}{PYNWmai0-5SXQOZOU4UJBYWY65C5UO66FXM000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SCRIPT{\_}ENGINE}}{SCRIPT:unENGINE}{PYNWmai0-5SXQOZOU4UJBYWY65C5UO66FXM000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SETUP{\_}INPUT}}{SETUP:unINPUT}{PYNWmai0-5SXQOZOU4UJBYWY65C5UO66FXM000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SET{\_}CHAR{\_}STATE}}{SET:unCHAR:unSTATE}{PYNWmai0-5SXQOZOU4UJBYWY65C5UO66FXM000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SET{\_}RESTRICTED}}{SET:unRESTRICTED}{PYNWmai0-5SXQOZOU4UJBYWY65C5UO66FXM000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SET{\_}STATE{\_}FIGHT}}{SET:unSTATE:unFIGHT}{PYNWmai0-5SXQOZOU4UJBYWY65C5UO66FXM000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SHOW{\_}LOCKED{\_}MSG}}{SHOW:unLOCKED:unMSG}{PYNWmai0-5SXQOZOU4UJBYWY65C5UO66FXM000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{START{\_}COMBAT}}{START:unCOMBAT}{PYNWmai0-5SXQOZOU4UJBYWY65C5UO66FXM000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{STEPS{\_}TAKEN}}{STEPS:unTAKEN}{PYNWmai0-5SXQOZOU4UJBYWY65C5UO66FXM000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{TEARDOWN{\_}INPUT}}{TEARDOWN:unINPUT}{PYNWmai0-5SXQOZOU4UJBYWY65C5UO66FXM000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{TRIGGER{\_}SCENE{\_}EVENT}}{TRIGGER:unSCENE:unEVENT}{PYNWmai0-5SXQOZOU4UJBYWY65C5UO66FXM000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{TURN{\_}ACTIVE}}{TURN:unACTIVE}{PYNWmai0-5SXQOZOU4UJBYWY65C5UO66FXM000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{TURN{\_}START{\_}COL}}{TURN:unSTART:unCOL}{PYNWmai0-5SXQOZOU4UJBYWY65C5UO66FXM000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{TURN{\_}START{\_}ROW}}{TURN:unSTART:unROW}{PYNWmai0-5SXQOZOU4UJBYWY65C5UO66FXM000000-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{342}\nwdocspar

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{343}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-Y47L2JLEGWPQ32PCM5VXV43OQI000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-Y47L2JLEGWPQ32PCM5VXV43OQI000000-1}}}\moddef{handle encounter~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-Y47L2JLEGWPQ32PCM5VXV43OQI000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $1C01
\nwlinkedidentc{HANDLE_ENCOUNTER}{PYNWmai0-Y47L2JLEGWPQ32PCM5VXV43OQI000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    ; --- random encounter path (event type $00-$3F) ---
    LDA     #$00
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SET_CHAR_STATE}{PYNWmai0-CBVYIWFRJGEOPJMLWQHLZ77QQI000000-1}            ; set char field 15 state to 0
    LDY     #$01
    LDA     ($BE),Y             ; event byte 1 = type
    CMP     #$40
    BPL     .specific           ; type >= $40 → specific encounter
    LDA     #$14
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{RANDOM_IN_RANGE}{PYNWmai0-F6322QSFMTRJBO2IS2F3GEYRZU000000-1}     ; random(20)
    STA     $5A18
    LDY     #$05
    LDA     ($F8),Y             ; char field 5
    AND     #$1F                ; low 5 bits = avoidance stat
    CMP     $5A18
    BMI     .roll_type          ; stat < random → encounter happens
    JMP     .avoided            ; stat >= random → avoid encounter
.roll_type:
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{STEP_PRNG}{PYNWmai0-3OGDZ4EYEYE7YXQHNEV2CZPRBM000000-1}
    LDA     #$74
    CMP     $5A18
    BPL     .normal             ; $74 >= random → normal encounter
    JMP     .special            ; rare: special encounter
.normal:
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SET_CURSOR_ROW21}{PYNWmai0-UOBA5Y3PKYLQKGPLIBUCA3M2SE000000-1}
    LDA     #$01
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{DISPLAY_MESSAGE}{PYNWmai0-PLQAK2MUE37THNKRCI7RJB7UJY000000-1}     ; "encounter" message
    LDX     #$14
    JMP     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_ENGINE}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-6}       ; run encounter script

    ; --- specific encounter path (type >= $40) ---
.specific:
    LDY     #$00
    LDA     ($BE),Y             ; event byte 0 = position
    STA     $5A5E
    LDA     #$01
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SET_CHAR_STATE}{PYNWmai0-CBVYIWFRJGEOPJMLWQHLZ77QQI000000-1}            ; set state 1
    LDY     #$01
    LDA     ($BE),Y
    AND     #$3F                ; low 6 bits = encounter ID
    BNE     .have_id
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{STEP_PRNG}{PYNWmai0-3OGDZ4EYEYE7YXQHNEV2CZPRBM000000-1}           ; ID 0 → derive from PRNG
    LDA     $5A18
    ROR
    ROR
    AND     #$1C
    ORA     #$01
.have_id:
    STA     $5A29               ; store encounter ID
    ROR
    BCC     .no_clear
    LDY     #$04
    LDA     ($F8),Y             ; char field 4
    BMI     .no_clear
    CMP     #$2A
    BMI     .no_clear
    CMP     #$3F
    BPL     .no_clear
    LDA     #$00
    STA     $5A29               ; clear ID if char in range $2A-$3E
.no_clear:
    LDY     #$02
    LDA     ($BE),Y             ; event byte 2 = destination pos
    STA     $5A5F
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{COMMIT_MOVE}{PYNWmai0-ZQVA6GBQYGATH77KOXC5SWQ6UE000000-1}            ; commit move
    LDA     $7ABE
    STA     $5A8C
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{REORDER_CURRENT_CHAR}{PYNWmai0-L43GPHDOGYAESQOO4UGQZ55M5U000000-1}
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{TIMED_WAIT}{PYNWmai0-TTL3BS3ZNAOH4GH5O7EQQ2NYYQ000000-1}
    LDY     #$03
    LDA     $5A5F
    STA     ($F8),Y             ; update char packed position
    LDA     $5A29
    CMP     $5A02               ; compare encounter ID with current scene
    BEQ     .same_scene
    JMP     \nwlinkedidentc{RESET_TURN_POS}{PYNWmai0-ZQVA6GBQYGATH77KOXC5SWQ6UE000000-1}            ; different → reset position
.same_scene:
    LDA     $5A5F
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{POS_TO_COLROW}{PYNWmai0-AMTAHZ55D6ORMSENT2EMDCDU24000000-1}
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{CURRENT_COL}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}
    STY     \nwlinkedidentc{CURRENT_ROW}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}
    JMP     \nwlinkedidentc{COMMIT_MOVE}{PYNWmai0-ZQVA6GBQYGATH77KOXC5SWQ6UE000000-1}            ; commit to new position

    ; --- encounter avoided ---
.avoided:
    LDY     #$01
    LDA     ($BE),Y
    ORA     #$40                ; mark event as activated
    STA     ($BE),Y
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{CURRENT_COL}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{TURN_START_COL}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}

    STA     $5AA2
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{TURN_START_ROW}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}

    LDA     FONT_CHARNUM
    STA     $5AA4
    LDX     #$0C

    LDA     #$02
    JMP     \nwlinkedidentc{DISPLAY_MESSAGE}{PYNWmai0-PLQAK2MUE37THNKRCI7RJB7UJY000000-1}     ; "avoided encounter" message

    ; --- special encounter (rare) ---
.special:
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SET_CURSOR_ROW21}{PYNWmai0-UOBA5Y3PKYLQKGPLIBUCA3M2SE000000-1}
    LDA     #$09
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SCENE_LOOP}{PYNWmai0-5E23YPEUUG4SZHWM2ZQ6MSHERE000000-1}          ; trigger scene 9
    LDA     #$01
    JMP     \nwlinkedidentc{APPLY_DAMAGE_TO_CURRENT}{PYNWmai0-7WCBQKCPJ4X6WWZUTNPR5LDKNI000000-1}
