\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{345}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-J7Q7EV5KY4I3TMCLNUF4NZNIK4000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-J7Q7EV5KY4I3TMCLNUF4NZNIK4000000-1}}}\moddef{trigger scene event~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-J7Q7EV5KY4I3TMCLNUF4NZNIK4000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $1D04
\nwlinkedidentc{TRIGGER_SCENE_EVENT}{PYNWmai0-J7Q7EV5KY4I3TMCLNUF4NZNIK4000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    LDA     #$00
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SET_CHAR_STATE}{PYNWmai0-CBVYIWFRJGEOPJMLWQHLZ77QQI000000-1}            ; set char field 15 state to 0
    LDA     $BE
    STA     $5A5B               ; save event pointer low
    LDA     $BF
    STA     $5A5C               ; save event pointer high
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{COMMIT_MOVE}{PYNWmai0-ZQVA6GBQYGATH77KOXC5SWQ6UE000000-1}            ; commit move
    LDA     $5A5B
    STA     $BE                 ; restore event pointer
    LDA     $5A5C
    STA     $BF
    LDY     #$02
    LDA     ($BE),Y             ; event byte 2 = scene index
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SCENE_LOOP}{PYNWmai0-5E23YPEUUG4SZHWM2ZQ6MSHERE000000-1}          ; trigger scene
    LDY     #$01
    LDA     ($BE),Y             ; event byte 1 = type
    CMP     #$D3
    BPL     .d3_or_above
    RTS                         ; $D2: trigger scene only
.d3_or_above:
    BNE     .d4
    LDA     #$FE                ; $D3: mark event as empty
    DEY
    STA     ($BE),Y
    RTS
.d4:
    LDA     #$FE                ; $D4: mark event as empty
    DEY
    STA     ($BE),Y
    LDA     #$0F
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SCENE_LOOP}{PYNWmai0-5E23YPEUUG4SZHWM2ZQ6MSHERE000000-1}          ; trigger bonus scene $0F
    LDA     #$03
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{RANDOM_IN_RANGE}{PYNWmai0-F6322QSFMTRJBO2IS2F3GEYRZU000000-1}     ; random(3)
    CLC
    ADC     #$01                ; 1-3
    JMP     \nwlinkedidentc{APPLY_DAMAGE_TO_CURRENT}{PYNWmai0-7WCBQKCPJ4X6WWZUTNPR5LDKNI000000-1}            ; apply effect to char
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{TRIGGER{\_}SCENE{\_}EVENT}}{TRIGGER:unSCENE:unEVENT}{PYNWmai0-J7Q7EV5KY4I3TMCLNUF4NZNIK4000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{TRIGGER{\_}SCENE{\_}EVENT}}{TRIGGER:unSCENE:unEVENT}}}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{APPLY{\_}DAMAGE{\_}TO{\_}CURRENT}}{APPLY:unDAMAGE:unTO:unCURRENT}}\\{{\nwixident{COMMIT{\_}MOVE}}{COMMIT:unMOVE}}\\{{\nwixident{RANDOM{\_}IN{\_}RANGE}}{RANDOM:unIN:unRANGE}}\\{{\nwixident{SCENE{\_}LOOP}}{SCENE:unLOOP}}\\{{\nwixident{SET{\_}CHAR{\_}STATE}}{SET:unCHAR:unSTATE}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{APPLY{\_}DAMAGE{\_}TO{\_}CURRENT}}{APPLY:unDAMAGE:unTO:unCURRENT}{PYNWmai0-J7Q7EV5KY4I3TMCLNUF4NZNIK4000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{COMMIT{\_}MOVE}}{COMMIT:unMOVE}{PYNWmai0-J7Q7EV5KY4I3TMCLNUF4NZNIK4000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{RANDOM{\_}IN{\_}RANGE}}{RANDOM:unIN:unRANGE}{PYNWmai0-J7Q7EV5KY4I3TMCLNUF4NZNIK4000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SCENE{\_}LOOP}}{SCENE:unLOOP}{PYNWmai0-J7Q7EV5KY4I3TMCLNUF4NZNIK4000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SET{\_}CHAR{\_}STATE}}{SET:unCHAR:unSTATE}{PYNWmai0-J7Q7EV5KY4I3TMCLNUF4NZNIK4000000-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{346}\nwdocspar

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{347}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-54OVBRYVAXX7KYNOX73X7MCSVQ000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-54OVBRYVAXX7KYNOX73X7MCSVQ000000-1}}}\moddef{pickup treasure~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-54OVBRYVAXX7KYNOX73X7MCSVQ000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $646B
\nwlinkedidentc{PICKUP_TREASURE}{PYNWmai0-54OVBRYVAXX7KYNOX73X7MCSVQ000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    LDA     #$00
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SET_CHAR_STATE}{PYNWmai0-CBVYIWFRJGEOPJMLWQHLZ77QQI000000-1}            ; set char field 15 state to 0
    LDA     $BE
    STA     $F4                 ; copy event ptr → $F4/$F5
    LDA     $BF
    STA     $F5
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{COMMIT_MOVE}{PYNWmai0-ZQVA6GBQYGATH77KOXC5SWQ6UE000000-1}            ; commit move
    LDY     #$01
    LDA     ($F4),Y             ; event byte 1 = treasure type
    CMP     #$C9
    BPL     .trapped            ; >= $C9 → trapped chest or special
    SEC
    SBC     #$C0                ; $C0-$C8: treasure index 0-8
    STA     $BD
.rejoin:
    LDY     #$02
    LDA     ($F4),Y             ; event byte 2 = quantity
    STA     $BC
    LDY     #$01
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{MODIFY_CURRENT_STATS}{PYNWmai0-D5V5IXS72ERZHRDXR67YWUSOBU000000-1}            ; look up treasure data
    LDY     #$04
    LDA     ($F8),Y             ; char field 4
    CMP     #$15
    BCS     .mark_used          ; inventory full → skip pickup
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{CLEAR_STATUS_SLOTS}{PYNWmai0-6YK2ZNZEB52I3TCO2EM7DE7XLM000000-1}            ; add item to inventory
    LDA     #$AB
    STA     $BA
    LDA     #$7B
    STA     $BB
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{NUM_TO_DECIMAL}{PYNWmai0-NDZSG4V5NI575YZRAEMOIOV6CM000000-1}      ; format quantity
    LDY     #$0D
    LDA     ($F8),Y             ; char field 13 (gold low)
    STA     $BC
    INY
    LDA     ($F8),Y             ; char field 14 (gold high)
    STA     $BD
    LDA     #$CC
    STA     $BA
    LDA     #$7B
    STA     $BB
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{NUM_TO_DECIMAL}{PYNWmai0-NDZSG4V5NI575YZRAEMOIOV6CM000000-1}      ; format gold amount
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SET_CURSOR_ROW21}{PYNWmai0-UOBA5Y3PKYLQKGPLIBUCA3M2SE000000-1}
    LDA     #$84
    STA     $BC
    LDA     #$7B
    STA     $BD
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{CLEAR_AND_DISPLAY}{PYNWmai0-RZF3VVNQCKX33QMOGC4XMJM3PI000000-1}            ; display pickup message
.mark_used:
    LDY     #$00
    LDA     #$FE                ; mark event slot as empty
    STA     ($F4),Y
    RTS

    ; --- trapped chest (type >= $C9) ---
.trapped:
    CMP     #$D1
    BNE     .not_d1
    JMP     .handle_d1          ; $D1: special chest
.not_d1:
    LDA     #$06
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{RANDOM_IN_RANGE}{PYNWmai0-F6322QSFMTRJBO2IS2F3GEYRZU000000-1}     ; random(6)
    AND     #$03                ; trap type 0-3
    STA     $5A58
    LDY     #$04
    LDA     ($F8),Y             ; char field 4
    BMI     .apply_trap
    CMP     #$15
    BPL     .apply_trap
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SET_CURSOR_ROW21}{PYNWmai0-UOBA5Y3PKYLQKGPLIBUCA3M2SE000000-1}
    LDA     #$36
    CLC
    ADC     $5A58               ; scene $36 + trap type
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SCENE_LOOP}{PYNWmai0-5E23YPEUUG4SZHWM2ZQ6MSHERE000000-1}          ; show trap scene
.apply_trap:
    LDA     $5A58
    CMP     #$01
    BMI     .trap0              ; trap 0: lose 1-5 HP
    BEQ     .trap1              ; trap 1: lose 2-9 HP
    CMP     #$02
    BEQ     .trap2              ; trap 2: decrement counter
    BNE     .trap3              ; trap 3: zero gold
.trap0:
    LDA     #$05
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{RANDOM_IN_RANGE}{PYNWmai0-F6322QSFMTRJBO2IS2F3GEYRZU000000-1}
    CLC
    ADC     #$01                ; 1-5 damage
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{APPLY_DAMAGE_TO_CURRENT}{PYNWmai0-7WCBQKCPJ4X6WWZUTNPR5LDKNI000000-1}
    JMP     .after_trap
.trap1:
    LDA     #$08
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{RANDOM_IN_RANGE}{PYNWmai0-F6322QSFMTRJBO2IS2F3GEYRZU000000-1}
    CLC
    ADC     #$02                ; 2-9 damage
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{APPLY_DAMAGE_TO_CURRENT}{PYNWmai0-7WCBQKCPJ4X6WWZUTNPR5LDKNI000000-1}
    JMP     .after_trap
.trap2:
    LDY     #$0B
    LDA     ($F8),Y             ; char field 11
    AND     #$1F
    BEQ     .after_trap         ; already zero
    LDA     ($F8),Y
    SEC
    SBC     #$01                ; decrement
    STA     ($F8),Y
    JMP     .after_trap
.trap3:
    LDY     #$0D
    LDA     #$00
    STA     ($F8),Y             ; zero gold low
    INY
    STA     ($F8),Y             ; zero gold high
.after_trap:
    LDY     #$02
    LDA     ($F8),Y             ; char field 2 = room
    CMP     $5A03               ; current room?
    BEQ     .same_room
    DEY
    LDA     ($F4),Y             ; event byte 1
    SEC
    SBC     #$09                ; step back 9 in treasure table
    STA     ($F4),Y
    RTS
.same_room:
    DEY
    LDA     ($F4),Y             ; event byte 1
    SEC
    SBC     #$C9                ; convert to treasure index
    STA     $BD
    JMP     .rejoin             ; loop: process next treasure

    ; --- special chest $D1 ---
.handle_d1:
    LDA     #$0B
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SCENE_LOOP}{PYNWmai0-5E23YPEUUG4SZHWM2ZQ6MSHERE000000-1}          ; show scene $0B
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{INC_FIELD5_COUNTER}{PYNWmai0-I5VMNMJMB7QQQCVGPRJR54I7BU000000-1}
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{INC_FIELD_COUNTER}{PYNWmai0-I5VMNMJMB7QQQCVGPRJR54I7BU000000-1}
    LDA     #$03
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{RANDOM_IN_RANGE}{PYNWmai0-F6322QSFMTRJBO2IS2F3GEYRZU000000-1}     ; random(3)
    CMP     #$00
    BEQ     .lucky
    RTS                         ; 2/3 chance: nothing
.lucky:
    LDA     #$0C
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SCENE_LOOP}{PYNWmai0-5E23YPEUUG4SZHWM2ZQ6MSHERE000000-1}          ; show bonus scene $0C
    JMP     .mark_used          ; mark event used
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{PICKUP{\_}TREASURE}}{PICKUP:unTREASURE}{PYNWmai0-54OVBRYVAXX7KYNOX73X7MCSVQ000000-1}\eatline

\nwlinkedidentc{AI_CHOOSE_TARGET}{PYNWmai0-KEFBT3V5UBIE5Q2SEGO4W6K6CM000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    ; --- dispatch by AI mode ---
    LDA     #$00
    STA     $5A5D
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{CHAR_AI_MODE}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}
    CMP     #$02
    BPL     .mode_ge2

    ; --- mode 0/1: check if NPC should join party ---
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{PICK_RANDOM_MEMBER}{PYNWmai0-KIOWWHM63CVSG2ITVV6IE52OMY000000-1}
    LDA     $F5
    CMP     #$00
    BEQ     .simple_target      ; no match → simple target
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SET_CURSOR_ROW21}{PYNWmai0-UOBA5Y3PKYLQKGPLIBUCA3M2SE000000-1}
    LDA     #$24
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{DISPLAY_MESSAGE}{PYNWmai0-PLQAK2MUE37THNKRCI7RJB7UJY000000-1}     ; "joins party" message
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{PRINT_MEMBER_NAME}{PYNWmai0-VXBWVWIETO76ZLXVOHQURZSFW4000000-1}
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{RESET_TEXT_WINDOW}{PYNWmai0-HFLOGQNIX4BG5XFWGKDVLOXD6Q000000-1}
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{DELAY_WITH_ANIMATION}{PYNWmai0-GR34WPZFUFAWF4EEF55HS6PMUU000000-1}
    LDA     #$25
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{DISPLAY_MESSAGE}{PYNWmai0-PLQAK2MUE37THNKRCI7RJB7UJY000000-1}
    LDA     #$00
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{CHAR_AI_MODE}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}        ; switch to player control
    LDY     #$04
    LDA     ($F8),Y
    SEC
    SBC     #$15                ; adjust char field 4
    STA     ($F8),Y
    LDY     #$0F
    LDA     ($F4),Y             ; source field 15 high bits
    AND     #$C0
    STA     $BA
    LDA     ($F8),Y             ; target field 15 low bits
    AND     #$3F
    ORA     $BA                 ; merge high bits from source
    STA     ($F8),Y
    LDY     #$08
    LDA     ($FA),Y             ; group field 8
    CLC
    ADC     #$01                ; increment party size
    STA     ($FA),Y
    INC     $5A01               ; increment global party count
    RTS

    ; --- mode 2: compare stats for target ---
.mode_ge2:
    BNE     .mode_ge3
.simple_target:
    LDY     #$05
    LDA     ($F8),Y             ; char field 5
    AND     #$1F
    STA     $BA
    INY
    LDA     ($F8),Y             ; char field 6
    AND     #$3F
    CMP     $BA
    BPL     .use_encounter
    LDA     #$00
    STA     $5A71               ; no target
    JMP     .done
.use_encounter:
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{FIND_NEAREST_EVENT}{PYNWmai0-Z2UK2EYJFTCR4EPPQRZYDPLUMQ000000-1}            ; find encounter position
    STA     $5A71
    JMP     .done

    ; --- mode 3: find nearest hostile ---
.mode_ge3:
    CMP     #$04
    BPL     .mode_ge4
    LDA     $F8
    STA     $BC
    LDA     $F9
    STA     $BD
    LDA     #$3C                ; initial min distance
    STA     $5A72
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{FIRST_GROUP_MEMBER}{PYNWmai0-N5WF7CLBP626OQIPH6GSP4CDCA000000-1}
.loop3:
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{CHECK_HOSTILE}{PYNWmai0-GAQSOYZEBE3NQVLK37GI4L4NOY000000-1}
    CMP     #$00
    BEQ     .skip3
    LDY     #$03
    LDA     ($F4),Y             ; mob packed position
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{MANHATTAN_DISTANCE}{PYNWmai0-VQOMLNLJ3DZRMK7KN267UJMZIA000000-1}            ; compute distance
    CMP     $5A72
    BCS     .skip3              ; not closer
    STA     $5A72               ; new minimum
    LDY     #$03
    LDA     ($F4),Y
    STA     $5A71               ; target = this mob's position
.skip3:
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{NEXT_GROUP_MEMBER}{PYNWmai0-N5WF7CLBP626OQIPH6GSP4CDCA000000-1}            ; next group member
    LDA     $F5
    BNE     .loop3
    LDA     $5A72
    CMP     #$3C
    BNE     .found3
    LDA     $5A5E               ; no hostile found → use default
    STA     $5A71
.found3:
    JMP     .done

    ; --- mode 4: no target ---
.mode_ge4:
    BNE     .mode_gt4
    LDA     #$00
    STA     $5A71
    JMP     .done

    ; --- mode 5+: find strongest hostile ---
.mode_gt4:
    LDA     #$00
    STA     $BF                 ; max strength seen
    LDA     $F8
    STA     $BC
    LDA     $F9
    STA     $BD
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{FIRST_GROUP_MEMBER}{PYNWmai0-N5WF7CLBP626OQIPH6GSP4CDCA000000-1}
.loop5:
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{CHECK_HOSTILE}{PYNWmai0-GAQSOYZEBE3NQVLK37GI4L4NOY000000-1}
    CMP     #$00
    BEQ     .skip5
    LDY     #$05
    LDA     ($F4),Y             ; mob field 5
    AND     #$1F                ; strength stat
    CMP     $BF
    BMI     .skip5              ; not stronger
    STA     $BF                 ; new max
    LDY     #$03
    LDA     ($F4),Y
    STA     $BE                 ; target position
.skip5:
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{NEXT_GROUP_MEMBER}{PYNWmai0-N5WF7CLBP626OQIPH6GSP4CDCA000000-1}            ; next group member
    LDA     $F5
    BNE     .loop5
    LDA     $BF
    BEQ     .no_target5
    LDA     $BE
    STA     $5A71               ; strongest mob's position
    JMP     .done
.no_target5:
    LDA     $5A5E               ; no hostile → use default
    STA     $5A71
    JMP     .done

    ; --- convert target position to col/row ---
.done:
    LDA     $5A71
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{POS_TO_COLROW}{PYNWmai0-AMTAHZ55D6ORMSENT2EMDCDU24000000-1}
    STA     $5A72               ; target column
    STY     $5A73               ; target row
    RTS
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{AI{\_}CHOOSE{\_}TARGET}}{AI:unCHOOSE:unTARGET}{PYNWmai0-KEFBT3V5UBIE5Q2SEGO4W6K6CM000000-1}\eatline

\nwlinkedidentc{PICK_RANDOM_MEMBER}{PYNWmai0-KIOWWHM63CVSG2ITVV6IE52OMY000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE
    ; Pick a random eligible group member (field 4 in $00-$14 range)
    ; Uses ($FA)[8] as group size, calls \nwlinkedidentc{RANDOM_IN_RANGE}{PYNWmai0-F6322QSFMTRJBO2IS2F3GEYRZU000000-1} to pick Nth
.loop:
    LDY     #$08
    LDA     ($FA),Y             ; group size
    BEQ     .zero               ; empty group
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{RANDOM_IN_RANGE}{PYNWmai0-F6322QSFMTRJBO2IS2F3GEYRZU000000-1}     ; random(size)
    CMP     #$00
    BEQ     .loop               ; 0 → retry
    TAX                         ; X = count down to Nth member
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{FIRST_GROUP_MEMBER}{PYNWmai0-N5WF7CLBP626OQIPH6GSP4CDCA000000-1}
.check:
    LDY     #$04
    LDA     ($F4),Y             ; member field 4
    BMI     .next               ; negative → skip
    CMP     #$15
    BPL     .next               ; >= $15 → skip
    DEX
    BNE     .next               ; not Nth yet
    RTS                         ; found: $F4/$F5 points to member
.next:
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{NEXT_GROUP_MEMBER}{PYNWmai0-N5WF7CLBP626OQIPH6GSP4CDCA000000-1}
    JMP     .check
.zero:
    STA     $F4                 ; clear pointer
    STA     $F5
    RTS
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{PICK{\_}RANDOM{\_}MEMBER}}{PICK:unRANDOM:unMEMBER}{PYNWmai0-KIOWWHM63CVSG2ITVV6IE52OMY000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{PICK{\_}RANDOM{\_}MEMBER}}{PICK:unRANDOM:unMEMBER}}}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{FIRST{\_}GROUP{\_}MEMBER}}{FIRST:unGROUP:unMEMBER}}\\{{\nwixident{NEXT{\_}GROUP{\_}MEMBER}}{NEXT:unGROUP:unMEMBER}}\\{{\nwixident{RANDOM{\_}IN{\_}RANGE}}{RANDOM:unIN:unRANGE}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{FIRST{\_}GROUP{\_}MEMBER}}{FIRST:unGROUP:unMEMBER}{PYNWmai0-KIOWWHM63CVSG2ITVV6IE52OMY000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{NEXT{\_}GROUP{\_}MEMBER}}{NEXT:unGROUP:unMEMBER}{PYNWmai0-KIOWWHM63CVSG2ITVV6IE52OMY000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{RANDOM{\_}IN{\_}RANGE}}{RANDOM:unIN:unRANGE}{PYNWmai0-KIOWWHM63CVSG2ITVV6IE52OMY000000-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{352}\nwdocspar


\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{353}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-Z2UK2EYJFTCR4EPPQRZYDPLUMQ000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-Z2UK2EYJFTCR4EPPQRZYDPLUMQ000000-1}}}\moddef{fun 138d~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-Z2UK2EYJFTCR4EPPQRZYDPLUMQ000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $138D
\nwlinkedidentc{FIND_NEAREST_EVENT}{PYNWmai0-Z2UK2EYJFTCR4EPPQRZYDPLUMQ000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE
    ; Find nearest non-activated event (byte 1 < $C0) by Manhattan distance
    ; Returns position in A ($5A13)
    LDA     #$7F                ; initial min distance
    STA     $5A14
    LDY     #$06
    LDA     ($FA),Y             ; event list pointer low
    STA     $BE
    INY
    LDA     ($FA),Y             ; event list pointer high
    STA     $BF
    JMP     .check_end
.eval:
    LDY     #$01
    LDA     ($BE),Y             ; event byte 1 = type
    CMP     #$C0
    BCS     .advance            ; >= $C0 → activated, skip
    LDY     #$00
    LDA     ($BE),Y             ; event byte 0 = position
    STA     $5A15
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{MANHATTAN_DISTANCE}{PYNWmai0-VQOMLNLJ3DZRMK7KN267UJMZIA000000-1}            ; Manhattan distance
    CMP     $5A14
    BPL     .advance            ; not closer
    STA     $5A14               ; new minimum
    LDA     $5A15
    STA     $5A13               ; record position
.advance:
    LDA     $BE
    CLC
    ADC     #$03                ; next 3-byte entry
    STA     $BE
    BCC     .check_end
    INC     $BF
.check_end:
    LDY     #$00
    LDA     ($BE),Y
    CMP     #$FE                ; $FE = empty slot, skip
    BEQ     .advance
    CMP     #$FF                ; $FF = end of list
    BNE     .eval
    LDA     $5A13               ; return nearest position
    RTS
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{FIND{\_}NEAREST{\_}EVENT}}{FIND:unNEAREST:unEVENT}{PYNWmai0-Z2UK2EYJFTCR4EPPQRZYDPLUMQ000000-1}\eatline

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{355}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-VQOMLNLJ3DZRMK7KN267UJMZIA000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-VQOMLNLJ3DZRMK7KN267UJMZIA000000-1}}}\moddef{fun 13db~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-VQOMLNLJ3DZRMK7KN267UJMZIA000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $13DB
\nwlinkedidentc{MANHATTAN_DISTANCE}{PYNWmai0-VQOMLNLJ3DZRMK7KN267UJMZIA000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE
    ; Manhattan distance: |col(A) - col(char)| + |row(A) - row(char)|
    ; Input: A = packed position to measure from
    ; Uses char's position from ($F8)[3]
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{POS_TO_COLROW}{PYNWmai0-AMTAHZ55D6ORMSENT2EMDCDU24000000-1}       ; A → col in A, row in Y
    STA     $5A0C               ; save target col
    STY     $5A0D               ; save target row
    LDY     #$03
    LDA     ($F8),Y             ; char packed position
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{POS_TO_COLROW}{PYNWmai0-AMTAHZ55D6ORMSENT2EMDCDU24000000-1}
    SEC
    SBC     $5A0C               ; char col - target col
    BCS     .pos1
    EOR     #$FF                ; negate (absolute value)
    ADC     #$01
.pos1:
    STA     $BA                 ; |delta col|
    TYA
    SEC
    SBC     $5A0D               ; char row - target row
    BCS     .pos2
    EOR     #$FF
    ADC     #$01
.pos2:
    CLC
    ADC     $BA                 ; |delta col| + |delta row|
    RTS
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{MANHATTAN{\_}DISTANCE}}{MANHATTAN:unDISTANCE}{PYNWmai0-VQOMLNLJ3DZRMK7KN267UJMZIA000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{MANHATTAN{\_}DISTANCE}}{MANHATTAN:unDISTANCE}}}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{POS{\_}TO{\_}COLROW}}{POS:unTO:unCOLROW}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{POS{\_}TO{\_}COLROW}}{POS:unTO:unCOLROW}{PYNWmai0-VQOMLNLJ3DZRMK7KN267UJMZIA000000-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{356}\nwdocspar

    ; call $1156, update current→start, conditionally run script

    ORG     $106F
\nwlinkedidentc{APPLY_DAMAGE}{PYNWmai0-4HLK6PBQJMGXW2NFVH6OY47B5U000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE
    ; Apply damage A to char at ($F6).
    ; Subtracts from field 6 (HP). Displays damage message,
    ; runs script. If HP drops to 0: death handling.
    AND     #$1F
    STA     $5A10               ; damage amount
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SET_CURSOR_ROW21}{PYNWmai0-UOBA5Y3PKYLQKGPLIBUCA3M2SE000000-1}
    LDA     $5A10
    LDX     #$03
.ror_loop:
    INX
    CLC
    ROR
    BNE     .ror_loop           ; count leading zeros → message index
    TXA
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{DISPLAY_MESSAGE}{PYNWmai0-PLQAK2MUE37THNKRCI7RJB7UJY000000-1}     ; show damage message
    LDY     $5A10
    LDX     #$04
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_ENGINE}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-6}       ; run damage script
    LDY     #$06
    LDA     ($F6),Y             ; field 6 (HP + flags)
    TAX
    AND     #$3F                ; HP only
    SEC
    SBC     $5A10               ; HP - damage
    BCC     .dead               ; underflow → dead
    BEQ     .dead               ; zero → dead
    STA     $5A10               ; new HP
    TXA
    AND     #$C0                ; preserve high bits
    ORA     $5A10
    STA     ($F6),Y             ; store updated field 6
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SET_CURSOR_ROW21}{PYNWmai0-UOBA5Y3PKYLQKGPLIBUCA3M2SE000000-1}
    LDA     $5A10
    CMP     #$03
    BPL     .check8
    LDY     #$0F
    LDA     ($F6),Y             ; field 15
    AND     #$F8
    ORA     #$04                ; set restricted flag
    STA     ($F6),Y
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{PRINT_ENTITY_NAME}{PYNWmai0-CZ3MELV3VNRBDPJ735N7ENDE2E000000-1}
    LDA     #$09
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{DISPLAY_MESSAGE}{PYNWmai0-PLQAK2MUE37THNKRCI7RJB7UJY000000-1}     ; "badly hurt" message
    RTS
.check8:
    CMP     #$08
    BPL     .ge8
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{PRINT_ENTITY_NAME}{PYNWmai0-CZ3MELV3VNRBDPJ735N7ENDE2E000000-1}
    LDA     #$0A
    JMP     \nwlinkedidentc{DISPLAY_MESSAGE}{PYNWmai0-PLQAK2MUE37THNKRCI7RJB7UJY000000-1}     ; "wounded" message
.ge8:
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{PRINT_ENTITY_NAME}{PYNWmai0-CZ3MELV3VNRBDPJ735N7ENDE2E000000-1}
    LDA     #$0B
    JMP     \nwlinkedidentc{DISPLAY_MESSAGE}{PYNWmai0-PLQAK2MUE37THNKRCI7RJB7UJY000000-1}     ; "scratched" message

    ; --- character dies ---
.dead:
    LDY     #$04
    LDA     ($F6),Y             ; field 4
    LDX     #$08                ; default script
    CMP     #$15
    BCC     .skip_flag
    LDY     #$0F
    LDA     ($F6),Y
    ORA     #$10                ; set death flag
    STA     ($F6),Y
    LDX     #$0A                ; NPC death script
.skip_flag:
    TXA
    PHA
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{PRINT_ENTITY_NAME}{PYNWmai0-CZ3MELV3VNRBDPJ735N7ENDE2E000000-1}
    LDA     #$03
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{RANDOM_IN_RANGE}{PYNWmai0-F6322QSFMTRJBO2IS2F3GEYRZU000000-1}     ; random(3)
    CMP     #$00
    BEQ     .rand0
    LDA     #$0E
    BNE     .show_death
.rand0:
    LDA     #$02
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{RANDOM_IN_RANGE}{PYNWmai0-F6322QSFMTRJBO2IS2F3GEYRZU000000-1}     ; random(2)
    CLC
    ADC     #$27                ; message $27 or $28
.show_death:
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{DISPLAY_MESSAGE}{PYNWmai0-PLQAK2MUE37THNKRCI7RJB7UJY000000-1}     ; death message
    PLA
    TAX
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SCRIPT_ENGINE}{PYNWmai0-ETUEZGHCU2DXYIDN2GSMAGYCHA000000-6}       ; death script
    LDA     #$00
    STA     $5A29
    LDA     $5A02
    STA     $5A28
    LDA     $F6
    STA     $BC
    LDA     $F7
    STA     $BD
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{REORDER_CHAR}{PYNWmai0-TSZHS7O2FMNRYEK2W57DEKVPQE000000-1}        ; cleanup
    LDY     #$0D
    LDA     ($F6),Y             ; gold low
    STA     $BC
    INY
    LDA     ($F6),Y             ; gold high
    STA     $BD
    LDY     #$00
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{MODIFY_CHAR_STATS}{PYNWmai0-ZD5J5NYKHC2UDBV4IQA4EZDYQE000000-1}   ; subtract gold (Y=0 → subtract)
    LDY     #$03
    LDA     ($F6),Y
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{UPDATE_EVENT_LIST}{PYNWmai0-MRILQSXRUPVDHTVVU52XV2XOQA000000-1}            ; handle death at position
    LDY     #$03
    LDA     ($F6),Y
    JMP     \nwlinkedidentc{DRAW_CHAR_AT_POS}{PYNWmai0-RAACK23HC5EFMXFBXXME6ZKJTE000000-1}    ; redraw position
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{APPLY{\_}DAMAGE}}{APPLY:unDAMAGE}{PYNWmai0-4HLK6PBQJMGXW2NFVH6OY47B5U000000-1}\eatline

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{379}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-CZ3MELV3VNRBDPJ735N7ENDE2E000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-CZ3MELV3VNRBDPJ735N7ENDE2E000000-1}}}\moddef{fun 1142~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-CZ3MELV3VNRBDPJ735N7ENDE2E000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup

\nwlinkedidentc{PRINT_ENTITY_NAME}{PYNWmai0-CZ3MELV3VNRBDPJ735N7ENDE2E000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE
    ; Print entity name: cursor to row 21, load name ptr from ($F6)[0..1],
    ; print centered at bottom, then reset text window.
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SET_CURSOR_ROW21}{PYNWmai0-UOBA5Y3PKYLQKGPLIBUCA3M2SE000000-1}
    LDY     #$00
    LDA     ($F6),Y             ; name pointer low
    STA     $BC
    INY
    LDA     ($F6),Y             ; name pointer high
    STA     $BD

\nwlinkedidentc{UPDATE_EVENT_LIST}{PYNWmai0-MRILQSXRUPVDHTVVU52XV2XOQA000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE
    ; Update event list for position A with value $BC/$BD.
    ; If $BC/$BD = 0, return immediately.
    ; Scans 3-byte event entries at ($FA)[6..7]:
    ;   $FF = end of list → display message $2A
    ;   $FE = empty slot → insert new entry
    ;   matching pos + type $C0-$D0 → add to existing entry
    ;   else → advance to next entry
    STA     $BA                 ; save position
    LDA     #$00
    CMP     $BC
    BNE     .has_value
    CMP     $BD
    BNE     .has_value
    RTS
.has_value:
    LDY     #$06
    LDA     ($FA),Y             ; event list pointer low
    STA     $BE
    INY
    LDA     ($FA),Y             ; event list pointer high
    STA     $BF
.scan:
    LDY     #$00
    LDA     ($BE),Y             ; entry byte 0 = position
    CMP     #$FF
    BNE     .not_end
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{SET_CURSOR_ROW21}{PYNWmai0-UOBA5Y3PKYLQKGPLIBUCA3M2SE000000-1}
    LDA     #$2A
    JMP     \nwlinkedidentc{DISPLAY_MESSAGE}{PYNWmai0-PLQAK2MUE37THNKRCI7RJB7UJY000000-1}     ; "event list full" message
.not_end:
    CMP     #$FE
    BNE     .check_match
    ; Empty slot: insert new entry
    LDA     $BA
    STA     ($BE),Y             ; byte 0 = position
    INY
    LDA     $BD
    AND     #$07
    ORA     #$C0                ; byte 1 = type + high bits
    STA     ($BE),Y
    INY
    LDA     $BC
    STA     ($BE),Y             ; byte 2 = value low
    RTS
.check_match:
    CMP     $BA                 ; same position?
    BNE     .next
    INY
    LDA     ($BE),Y             ; byte 1 = type
    BPL     .next               ; not activated
    CMP     #$C0
    BMI     .next               ; below $C0
    CMP     #$D1
    BPL     .next               ; above $D0
    ; Add to existing entry
    CLC
    LDA     $BC
    INY
    ADC     ($BE),Y             ; byte 2 += value low
    STA     ($BE),Y
    DEY
    LDA     $BD
    AND     #$07
    ADC     ($BE),Y             ; byte 1 += value high (with carry)
    STA     ($BE),Y
    RTS
.next:
    CLC
    LDA     $BE
    ADC     #$03                ; next 3-byte entry
    STA     $BE
    BCC     .no_carry
    INC     $BF
.no_carry:
    JMP     .scan
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{UPDATE{\_}EVENT{\_}LIST}}{UPDATE:unEVENT:unLIST}{PYNWmai0-MRILQSXRUPVDHTVVU52XV2XOQA000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{UPDATE{\_}EVENT{\_}LIST}}{UPDATE:unEVENT:unLIST}}}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{DISPLAY{\_}MESSAGE}}{DISPLAY:unMESSAGE}}\\{{\nwixident{SET{\_}CURSOR{\_}ROW21}}{SET:unCURSOR:unROW21}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{DISPLAY{\_}MESSAGE}}{DISPLAY:unMESSAGE}{PYNWmai0-MRILQSXRUPVDHTVVU52XV2XOQA000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SET{\_}CURSOR{\_}ROW21}}{SET:unCURSOR:unROW21}{PYNWmai0-MRILQSXRUPVDHTVVU52XV2XOQA000000-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{382}\nwdocspar

    SUBROUTINE
    ; Auto-heal: if HP < $28, randomly attempt healing via $1482.
    ; Loops while $5A18 >= $50 (still injured). Shows message $21
    ; if player heals for the first time.
    LDY     #$06
    LDA     ($F8),Y
    AND     #$3F
    CMP     #$28
    BMI     .do_heal
    RTS
.do_heal:
    LDA     #$01
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{RANDOM_IN_RANGE}{PYNWmai0-F6322QSFMTRJBO2IS2F3GEYRZU000000-1}
    CMP     #$00
    BNE     .start_heal
    RTS
.start_heal:
    LDA     #$00
    STA     $5A16
.heal_loop:
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{FUN_1482}{PYNWmai0-JVOCVCYPWDBS3MQJRLMBR4QIDU000000-1}
    JSR     FUN_78A8
    LDA     $5A18
    CMP     #$50
    BPL     .heal_loop
    LDY     #$04
    LDA     ($F8),Y
    CMP     #$15
    BCC     .player

    RTS

    LDA     $5A16
    BNE     .done

    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{RESET_TEXT_WINDOW}{PYNWmai0-HFLOGQNIX4BG5XFWGKDVLOXD6Q000000-1}
    LDA     #$21
    JMP     \nwlinkedidentc{DISPLAY_MESSAGE}{PYNWmai0-PLQAK2MUE37THNKRCI7RJB7UJY000000-1}

\nwlinkedidentc{RESOLVE_ATTACK}{PYNWmai0-3YPN5MCMF2XO67GNNBAWWL3PWE000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE
    ; Combat willingness calculation and attack resolution.
    ; Computes willingness score in $5A76 based on char/target stats,
    ; then rolls random to determine if attack occurs.
    JSR     FUN_16A3
    LDA     $5A74
    CMP     #$01
    BNE     .not_player
    LDA     #$1C
    STA     $5A76
    JMP     .clamp_done
.not_player:
    LDY     #$0B
    LDA     ($F8),Y
    TAX
    AND     #$1F
    STA     $5A76
    TXA
    AND     #$20
    BEQ     .no_bit5
    TXA
    AND     #$EF
    STA     ($F8),Y
    LDA     #$18
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{FUN_169B}{PYNWmai0-7QG2ZQNFKISMRF7FKK63OCGB6U000000-1}
.no_bit5:
    LDA     ($F4),Y
    TAY
    AND     #$40
    BEQ     .no_bit6
    LDA     #$FC
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{FUN_169B}{PYNWmai0-7QG2ZQNFKISMRF7FKK63OCGB6U000000-1}
.no_bit6:
    TYA
    AND     #$80
    BEQ     .no_bit7
    LDA     #$08
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{FUN_169B}{PYNWmai0-7QG2ZQNFKISMRF7FKK63OCGB6U000000-1}
.no_bit7:
    LDY     #$0F
    LDA     ($F4),Y
    TAX
    AND     #$04
    BEQ     .no_restrict
    LDA     #$06
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{FUN_169B}{PYNWmai0-7QG2ZQNFKISMRF7FKK63OCGB6U000000-1}
.no_restrict:
    TXA
    AND     #$03
    CMP     #$01
    BPL     .ge1
    LDA     #$03
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{FUN_169B}{PYNWmai0-7QG2ZQNFKISMRF7FKK63OCGB6U000000-1}
    JMP     .state_done
.ge1:
    BNE     .ne1
    LDA     #$FF
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{FUN_169B}{PYNWmai0-7QG2ZQNFKISMRF7FKK63OCGB6U000000-1}
    JMP     .state_done
.ne1:
    CMP     #$03

\nwlinkedidentc{MODIFY_CHAR_STATS}{PYNWmai0-ZD5J5NYKHC2UDBV4IQA4EZDYQE000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE
    ; Add or subtract gold from char record at ($F6).
    ; Y=0: subtract $BC/$BD from field 13/14
    ; Y≠0: add $BC/$BD to field 13/14
    ; Then recompute field 12 (level/XP encoding).
    CPY     #$00
    BEQ     .subtract
    LDY     #$0D
    LDA     ($F6),Y
    CLC
    ADC     $BC
    STA     ($F6),Y
    INY
    LDA     ($F6),Y
    ADC     $BD
    STA     ($F6),Y
    JMP     .aftermath
.subtract:
    LDY     #$0D
    SEC
    LDA     ($F6),Y
    SBC     $BC
    STA     ($F6),Y
    INY
    LDA     ($F6),Y
    SBC     $BD
    STA     ($F6),Y
.aftermath:
    LDY     #$05
    LDA     ($F6),Y
    ROL
    ROL
    ROL
    AND     #$F8
    STA     $5A7E
    LDY     #$0C
    LDA     ($F6),Y
    PHA
    AND     #$0F
    TAX
    PLA
    ROR
    ROR
    ROR
    ROR
    AND     #$0F
    TAY
.decy:
    DEY
    BMI     .done_cnt
    INX
    BPL     .decy
.done_cnt:
    INY
    STY     $5A7F
    STY     $BA
    STY     $BB
.outer_loop:
    LDY     #$0E
    CPX     #$00
    BEQ     .store_final
    CLC
    LDA     $BA
    ADC     $5A7E
    STA     $BA
    BCC     .no_carry
    INC     $BB
.no_carry:
    LDA     ($F6),Y
    CMP     $BB
    BCC     .store_final
    BNE     .next_iter
    DEY
    LDA     ($F6),Y
    CMP     $BA
    BCC     .store_final
.next_iter:
    DEX
    CLC
    LDA     $5A7F
    ADC     #$10
    STA     $5A7F
    BNE     .outer_loop
.store_final:
    TXA
    ORA     $5A7F
    LDY     #$0C
    STA     ($F6),Y
    RTS
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{MODIFY{\_}CHAR{\_}STATS}}{MODIFY:unCHAR:unSTATS}{PYNWmai0-ZD5J5NYKHC2UDBV4IQA4EZDYQE000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{MODIFY{\_}CHAR{\_}STATS}}{MODIFY:unCHAR:unSTATS}}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{468}\nwdocspar

\subsection{set\_blink\_target (\$16A3)}

Sets up the blink cursor from the current combatant.  On the mob's turn,
the mob's packed position (byte 3 of mob data) is split into column and row,
and its appearance (byte 4) is converted to a font character number.
On the player's turn, the player's column and row are taken directly from
{\Tt{}CURRENT{\textbackslash}{\_}COL\nwendquote}/{\Tt{}CURRENT{\textbackslash}{\_}ROW\nwendquote}, and the font character is looked up via {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}0C7E\nwendquote}.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{469}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-26}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-26}}}\moddef{defines~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-1}}}\plusendmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwprevnextdefs{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}{\relax}\nwenddeflinemarkup
\nwlinkedidentc{IS_PLAYER_TURN}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-26}  EQU     $5A74   ; 0 = mob's turn, 1 = player's turn
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{IS{\_}PLAYER{\_}TURN}}{IS:unPLAYER:unTURN}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-26}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{IS{\_}PLAYER{\_}TURN}}{IS:unPLAYER:unTURN}}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{470}\nwdocspar

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{471}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-2VA524SVP6PHW44TQJEWTMYFGE000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-2VA524SVP6PHW44TQJEWTMYFGE000000-1}}}\moddef{set blink target~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-2VA524SVP6PHW44TQJEWTMYFGE000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $16A3
\nwlinkedidentc{SET_BLINK_TARGET}{PYNWmai0-2VA524SVP6PHW44TQJEWTMYFGE000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{IS_PLAYER_TURN}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-26}
    CMP     #$01
    BEQ     .player

    ; --- mob path: convert packed position to col/row ---
    LDY     #$03
    LDA     ($F4),Y                 ; mob data[3] = packed position
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{POS_TO_COLROW}{PYNWmai0-AMTAHZ55D6ORMSENT2EMDCDU24000000-1}           ; A=col, Y=row
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{BLINK_COL}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-5}
    STY     \nwlinkedidentc{BLINK_ROW}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-5}
    LDY     #$04
    LDA     ($F4),Y                 ; mob data[4] = appearance
    JSR     \nwlinkedidentc{APPEARANCE_TO_FONTCHAR}{PYNWmai0-ZV3SLJLMHDXQXGXKZHHC4ROVNQ000000-1}  ; appearance → font char number
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{BLINK_CHAR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-5}
    RTS

    ; --- player path: col/row already separate ---
.player:
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{CURRENT_COL}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}             ; player font column
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{BLINK_COL}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-5}
    LDA     \nwlinkedidentc{CURRENT_ROW}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-25}             ; player font row
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{BLINK_ROW}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-5}
    LDA     $F4                     ; \\
    STA     $BE                     ;  | copy pointer $F4 → $BE
    LDA     $F5                     ;  |
    STA     $BF                     ; /
    JSR     $0C7E                   ; look up player's font char
    LDA     FONT_CHARNUM
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{BLINK_CHAR}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-5}
    RTS
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{SET{\_}BLINK{\_}TARGET}}{SET:unBLINK:unTARGET}{PYNWmai0-2VA524SVP6PHW44TQJEWTMYFGE000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{SET{\_}BLINK{\_}TARGET}}{SET:unBLINK:unTARGET}}}\nwnotused{set blink target}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{APPEARANCE{\_}TO{\_}FONTCHAR}}{APPEARANCE:unTO:unFONTCHAR}}\\{{\nwixident{BLINK{\_}CHAR}}{BLINK:unCHAR}}\\{{\nwixident{BLINK{\_}COL}}{BLINK:unCOL}}\\{{\nwixident{BLINK{\_}ROW}}{BLINK:unROW}}\\{{\nwixident{CURRENT{\_}COL}}{CURRENT:unCOL}}\\{{\nwixident{CURRENT{\_}ROW}}{CURRENT:unROW}}\\{{\nwixident{IS{\_}PLAYER{\_}TURN}}{IS:unPLAYER:unTURN}}\\{{\nwixident{POS{\_}TO{\_}COLROW}}{POS:unTO:unCOLROW}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{APPEARANCE{\_}TO{\_}FONTCHAR}}{APPEARANCE:unTO:unFONTCHAR}{PYNWmai0-2VA524SVP6PHW44TQJEWTMYFGE000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{BLINK{\_}CHAR}}{BLINK:unCHAR}{PYNWmai0-2VA524SVP6PHW44TQJEWTMYFGE000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{BLINK{\_}COL}}{BLINK:unCOL}{PYNWmai0-2VA524SVP6PHW44TQJEWTMYFGE000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{BLINK{\_}ROW}}{BLINK:unROW}{PYNWmai0-2VA524SVP6PHW44TQJEWTMYFGE000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{CURRENT{\_}COL}}{CURRENT:unCOL}{PYNWmai0-2VA524SVP6PHW44TQJEWTMYFGE000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{CURRENT{\_}ROW}}{CURRENT:unROW}{PYNWmai0-2VA524SVP6PHW44TQJEWTMYFGE000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{IS{\_}PLAYER{\_}TURN}}{IS:unPLAYER:unTURN}{PYNWmai0-2VA524SVP6PHW44TQJEWTMYFGE000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{POS{\_}TO{\_}COLROW}}{POS:unTO:unCOLROW}{PYNWmai0-2VA524SVP6PHW44TQJEWTMYFGE000000-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{472}\nwdocspar

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{473}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-X4FLZFQK2PJN7VH3YTA5N5PTO4000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-X4FLZFQK2PJN7VH3YTA5N5PTO4000000-1}}}\moddef{Hit chance~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-X4FLZFQK2PJN7VH3YTA5N5PTO4000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwenddeflinemarkup
(15AB)
.compute_to_hit:
    JSR      \nwlinkedidentc{SET_BLINK_TARGET}{PYNWmai0-2VA524SVP6PHW44TQJEWTMYFGE000000-1}
    LDA      \nwlinkedidentc{IS_PLAYER_TURN}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-26}
    CMP      #$01
    BNE      .mob
    LDA      #$1C
    STA      TO_HIT
    JMP      .roll

.mob:
    ; Base chance = dexterity (-1)
    LDY      #$0B
    LDA      (MOB_PTR?),Y
    TAX
    AND      #$1F
    STA      TO_HIT
    TXA

    ; If DEX bit 5 set, clear DEX bit 4
    ; and add 75% to chance.
    AND      #$20
    BEQ      LAB_15d6
    TXA
    AND      #$EF
    STA      (MOB_PTR?),Y
    LDA      #$18
    JSR      add_to_to_hit

LAB_15d6:
    ; If opponent DEX bit 6 set,
    ; subtract 12.5% (particularly difficult
    ; to hit).
    LDA      (THING_PTR?),Y
    TAY
    AND      #$40
    BEQ      LAB_15e2
    LDA      #$FC
    JSR      add_to_to_hit

LAB_15e2:
    ; If opponent DEX bit 7 set,
    ; add 25% (extremely easy to hit).
    TYA
    AND      #$80
    BEQ      .check_thing_f
    LDA      #$08
    JSR      add_to_to_hit

.check_thing_f:
    ; If opponent F bit 2 set,
    ; add 18.75% (down: unconscious, in hand to hand combat,
    ; or resting)
    LDY      #$0F
    LDA      (THING_PTR?),Y
    TAX
    AND      #$04
    BEQ      LAB_15fa
    LDA      #$06
    JSR      add_to_to_hit

LAB_15fa:
    ; If opponent F bits 1,0 < 1
    ; add 9.375% (currently resting)
    TXA
    AND      #$03
    CMP      #$01
    BPL      LAB_1609
    LDA      #$03
    JSR      add_to_to_hit
    JMP      .check_thing_6

LAB_1609:
    ; subtract 3.125% ("running" -- bugged?)
    BNE      LAB_1613
    LDA      #$FF
    JSR      add_to_to_hit
    JMP      .check_thing_6

LAB_1613:
    ; If opponent F bits 1,0 == 3
    ; subtract 9.375% (opponent is defending)
    CMP      #$03
    BNE      .check_thing_6
    LDA      #$FD
    JSR      add_to_to_hit

.check_thing_6:
    ; If opponent CON <= 3
    ; add 75%.
    LDY      #$06
    LDA      (THING_PTR?),Y
    AND      #$3F
    CMP      #$03
    BCS      LAB_162b
    LDA      #$18
    JSR      add_to_to_hit

LAB_162b:
    ; If mob[3] == thing[3]...
    LDY      #$03
    LDA      (MOB_PTR?),Y
    CMP      (THING_PTR?),Y
    BNE      .limit_to_hit

    ; add Thing[STR]/2 & 0x0F - Mob[STR]/2 & 0x0F
    LDY      #$05
    LDA      (THING_PTR?),Y
    ROR      A
    AND      #$0F
    STA      DAT_5a77
    LDA      (MOB_PTR?),Y
    ROR      A
    AND      #$0F
    SEC
    SBC      DAT_5a77
    JSR      add_to_to_hit

.limit_to_hit:
    LDA      TO_HIT
    BPL      .adjust_for_automatic_fail
    LDA      #$00
    STA      TO_HIT
    JMP      .roll

.adjust_for_automatic_fail:
    CMP      #$1F
    BMI      .roll
    LDA      #$1E
    STA      TO_HIT

.roll:
    LDA      #$1F
    JSR      get_random
    CMP      TO_HIT
    BMI      .do_hit
    BEQ      .do_hit
    JSR      clear_row_21
    JSR      print_name_of_actor
    JSR      scroll_status_window_up
    LDA      #$D2
    STA      DATA_PTR2
    LDA      #$7C
    STA      DATA_PTR2+1
    JSR      print_centered_row_23
    JSR      scroll_status_window_up
    LDA      #$01
    CMP      \nwlinkedidentc{IS_PLAYER_TURN}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-26}
    BEQ      .do_blink
    JSR      print_thing_name_centered_row_23
.do_blink:
    JSR      blink
    RTS
.do_hit:
    LDA      \nwlinkedidentc{IS_PLAYER_TURN}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-26}
    BEQ      .hit_mob
    JMP      hit_nonmob?
.hit_mob:
    JMP      hit_mob?
\nwnotused{Hit chance}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{IS{\_}PLAYER{\_}TURN}}{IS:unPLAYER:unTURN}}\\{{\nwixident{SET{\_}BLINK{\_}TARGET}}{SET:unBLINK:unTARGET}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{IS{\_}PLAYER{\_}TURN}}{IS:unPLAYER:unTURN}{PYNWmai0-X4FLZFQK2PJN7VH3YTA5N5PTO4000000-1}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{SET{\_}BLINK{\_}TARGET}}{SET:unBLINK:unTARGET}{PYNWmai0-X4FLZFQK2PJN7VH3YTA5N5PTO4000000-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{474}\nwdocspar

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{475}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-QT6ETJXFJSZ45KITEMECPS3GYA000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-QT6ETJXFJSZ45KITEMECPS3GYA000000-1}}}\moddef{Get item at pos in room~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-QT6ETJXFJSZ45KITEMECPS3GYA000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG      $0B62
    ; Takes A (pos) and \nwlinkedidentc{TMP_PTR}{PYNWmai0-AJE4SNIWWSAT23GB2VNG3SS6JI000000-2} (pointer to room data)
get_item_at_pos_in_room:
    SUBROUTINE

    STA      \nwlinkedidentc{DAT_5a17_pos}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-9}

    ; load1 <- \nwlinkedidentc{TMP_PTR}{PYNWmai0-AJE4SNIWWSAT23GB2VNG3SS6JI000000-2}
    ; load3 <- \nwlinkedidentc{TMP_PTR}{PYNWmai0-AJE4SNIWWSAT23GB2VNG3SS6JI000000-2}

    LDA      \nwlinkedidentc{TMP_PTR}{PYNWmai0-AJE4SNIWWSAT23GB2VNG3SS6JI000000-2}+1
    STA      .load1+2
    STA      .load3+2
    LDA      \nwlinkedidentc{TMP_PTR}{PYNWmai0-AJE4SNIWWSAT23GB2VNG3SS6JI000000-2}
    STA      .load1+1
    STA      .load3+1
    JMP      .get_mob_link

.inner_loop:
    ; load2 <- room data[MAP]

    LDX      #$06
.load1:
    LDA      .load1+1,X
    STA      .load2+1-6,X
    INX
    BNE.X    #$08, .load1

.load2:
    ; Y <- (load2)

    LDY      .load2+1
    BNE.Y    #$FF, .not_ff          ; (load2) != 0xFF?
    JMP      \nwlinkedidentc{is_at_outer_limits}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-9}     ; else goto \nwlinkedidentc{is_at_outer_limits}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-9}

.not_ff:
    BEQ.Y    \nwlinkedidentc{DAT_5a17_pos}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-9}, .return_load2  ; (load2) == \nwlinkedidentc{DAT_5a17_pos}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-9}?

    ; load2 += 3

    \nwlinkedidentc{INCW}{PYNWmai0-UDRZI6QCMYPCHBPEW5VLDMJPJU000000-8}     .load2
    \nwlinkedidentc{INCW}{PYNWmai0-UDRZI6QCMYPCHBPEW5VLDMJPJU000000-8}     .load2
    INC      .load2+1
    BNE      .load2
    INC      .load2+2
    JMP      .load2

.return_load2:
    ; \nwlinkedidentc{DATA_PTR}{PYNWmai0-AJE4SNIWWSAT23GB2VNG3SS6JI000000-2} <- load2

    \nwlinkedidentc{STOW}{PYNWmai0-UDRZI6QCMYPCHBPEW5VLDMJPJU000000-1}     .load2+1, \nwlinkedidentc{DATA_PTR}{PYNWmai0-AJE4SNIWWSAT23GB2VNG3SS6JI000000-2}
    RTS

.get_mob_link:

    LDX      #$02
.load3:
    LDA      .load3+1,X  ; A <- load3[MOB]
    BEQ.A    #$00, .inner_loop
    JSR      mob_dataptr_to_load4

    LDX      #$03
.load4:
    LDY      .load4+1,X  ; Y <- load4[POS]
    BEQ.Y    \nwlinkedidentc{DAT_5a17_pos}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-9}, .return_load4

    ; load3 <- load4

    \nwlinkedidentc{STOW}{PYNWmai0-UDRZI6QCMYPCHBPEW5VLDMJPJU000000-1}     .load4+1, .load3+1
    JMP      .get_mob_link

.return_load4:
    ; \nwlinkedidentc{DATA_PTR}{PYNWmai0-AJE4SNIWWSAT23GB2VNG3SS6JI000000-2} = 0x8000 | load4

    LDA      #$80
    ORA      .load4+2
    STA      \nwlinkedidentc{DATA_PTR}{PYNWmai0-AJE4SNIWWSAT23GB2VNG3SS6JI000000-2}+1
    LDA      .load4+1
    STA      \nwlinkedidentc{DATA_PTR}{PYNWmai0-AJE4SNIWWSAT23GB2VNG3SS6JI000000-2}
    RTS

mob_dataptr_to_load4:
    SUBROUTINE
    ; load4 <- mob data for A

    JSR      \nwlinkedidentc{GET_MOB_DATA}{PYNWmai0-VTKXUQPSOCRIDYWOEIFECHPTSM000000-1}
    \nwlinkedidentc{STOW}{PYNWmai0-UDRZI6QCMYPCHBPEW5VLDMJPJU000000-1}     \nwlinkedidentc{DATA_PTR3}{PYNWmai0-AJE4SNIWWSAT23GB2VNG3SS6JI000000-2}, .load4
    RTS

\subsection{get\_mob\_data (\$0C32)}

Converts a 1-based mob index in {\Tt{}A\nwendquote} to a pointer to its 16-byte data
record, stored in {\Tt{}DATA{\textbackslash}{\_}PTR3\nwendquote} ({\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}BA/{\textbackslash}{\$}BB\nwendquote}).  The mob data table
starts at the address stored in {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}4000/{\textbackslash}{\$}4001\nwendquote} (within the decrypted
game data region), with each record being 16 bytes.  The formula is:

\begin{center}
{\Tt{}DATA{\textbackslash}{\_}PTR3\nwendquote} = {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}4000/{\textbackslash}{\$}4001\nwendquote} + (A $-$ 1) $\times$ 16
\end{center}

The multiplication by 16 is done by rotating the decremented index
left by 4 bits through carry, then splitting the result into high and
low byte contributions.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{477}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-VTKXUQPSOCRIDYWOEIFECHPTSM000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-VTKXUQPSOCRIDYWOEIFECHPTSM000000-1}}}\moddef{get mob data~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-VTKXUQPSOCRIDYWOEIFECHPTSM000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $0C32
\nwlinkedidentc{GET_MOB_DATA}{PYNWmai0-VTKXUQPSOCRIDYWOEIFECHPTSM000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    CLC
    ADC     #$FF                    ; A = index - 1, C = 1
    ROL                             ; \\
    ROL                             ;  | rotate \{C, A\} left 4 bits
    ROL                             ;  | = (index-1) * 16 with bits split
    ROL                             ; /
    TAY                             ; save rotated value
    ROL                             ; one more rotate
    AND     #$0F                    ; high byte contribution = (index-1) >> 4
    CLC
    ADC     $4001                   ; add base page
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{DATA_PTR3}{PYNWmai0-AJE4SNIWWSAT23GB2VNG3SS6JI000000-2}+1
    TYA
    AND     #$F0                    ; low byte contribution = ((index-1) & $0F) << 4
    CLC
    ADC     $4000                   ; add base offset
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{DATA_PTR3}{PYNWmai0-AJE4SNIWWSAT23GB2VNG3SS6JI000000-2}
    BCC     .done
    INC     \nwlinkedidentc{DATA_PTR3}{PYNWmai0-AJE4SNIWWSAT23GB2VNG3SS6JI000000-2}+1             ; carry to high byte
.done:
    RTS
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{GET{\_}MOB{\_}DATA}}{GET:unMOB:unDATA}{PYNWmai0-VTKXUQPSOCRIDYWOEIFECHPTSM000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{GET{\_}MOB{\_}DATA}}{GET:unMOB:unDATA}}}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{DATA{\_}PTR3}}{DATA:unPTR3}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{DATA{\_}PTR3}}{DATA:unPTR3}{PYNWmai0-VTKXUQPSOCRIDYWOEIFECHPTSM000000-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{478}\nwdocspar

\subsection{init\_mob\_count (\$0C51)}

Called once during {\Tt{}GAME{\textbackslash}{\_}INIT\nwendquote} to initialize {\Tt{}TOTAL{\textbackslash}{\_}MOB{\textbackslash}{\_}COUNT\nwendquote}.
Walks all 9-byte character records starting from index~1 (skipping
the group-0 header at {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}4000\nwendquote}), summing byte~8 (group member count)
of each record until the end sentinel (byte~1 = {\Tt{}{\textbackslash}{\$}FF\nwendquote}) is reached.

The result is the total number of mobs assigned to groups~1 and above.
At startup, byte~8 contains only the group count in bits~3--0 (the
upper bits---pending XP and status flag---are zero), so the sum is
simply the total mob count.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{479}\sublabel{PYNWmai0-FUVGEE5QFLBSHT5MZWRVT5CDCY000000-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-FUVGEE5QFLBSHT5MZWRVT5CDCY000000-1}}}\moddef{init mob count~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{PYNWmai0-FUVGEE5QFLBSHT5MZWRVT5CDCY000000-1}}}\endmoddef\nwstartdeflinemarkup\nwusesondefline{\\{PYNWmai0-4RSQDT2TWU2QLEUIDKRLWKU4JE000000-1}}\nwenddeflinemarkup
    ORG     $0C51
\nwlinkedidentc{INIT_MOB_COUNT}{PYNWmai0-FUVGEE5QFLBSHT5MZWRVT5CDCY000000-1}:
    SUBROUTINE

    LDA     #$00                    ; \\
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{TOTAL_MOB_COUNT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-10}         ; / clear total
    LDA     #$09                    ; \\ $FA/$FB = $4009 (record 1)
    STA     $FA                     ;  |
    LDA     #$40                    ;  |
    STA     $FB                     ; /
.loop:
    LDY     #$01
    LDA     ($FA),Y                 ; byte 1 of record
    CMP     #$FF                    ; $FF = end sentinel
    BNE     .count
    RTS
.count:
    LDY     #$08
    LDA     ($FA),Y                 ; byte 8 = group member count
    CLC
    ADC     \nwlinkedidentc{TOTAL_MOB_COUNT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-10}         ; accumulate
    STA     \nwlinkedidentc{TOTAL_MOB_COUNT}{PYNWmai0-4XHAE6ADBEGDO3TDMJXX7ROHNM000000-10}
    LDA     #$09                    ; \\ advance $FA by 9 (next record)
    ADC     $FA                     ;  |
    STA     $FA                     ;  |
    BCC     .loop                   ;  |
    INC     $FB                     ;  |
    BCS     .loop                   ; / always taken
\nwindexdefn{\nwixident{INIT{\_}MOB{\_}COUNT}}{INIT:unMOB:unCOUNT}{PYNWmai0-FUVGEE5QFLBSHT5MZWRVT5CDCY000000-1}\eatline
\nwidentdefs{\\{{\nwixident{INIT{\_}MOB{\_}COUNT}}{INIT:unMOB:unCOUNT}}}\nwidentuses{\\{{\nwixident{TOTAL{\_}MOB{\_}COUNT}}{TOTAL:unMOB:unCOUNT}}}\nwindexuse{\nwixident{TOTAL{\_}MOB{\_}COUNT}}{TOTAL:unMOB:unCOUNT}{PYNWmai0-FUVGEE5QFLBSHT5MZWRVT5CDCY000000-1}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{480}\nwdocspar
